# cs.LG [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [A Differentiable Measure of Algebraic Complexity: Provably Exact Discovery of Group Structures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.23152)
*Dongsung Huh,Lior Horesh,Halyun Jeong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过Cayley表补全（Cayley-table completion）形式化离散代数规则的发现，证明HyperCube张量分解的目标函数可精确刻画代数的可结合性（associativity），并为群结构提供一个可微分的全局特征函数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从数据中发现离散代数规则是机器学习中的基础难题，现有方法多依赖组合搜索（combinatorial search），缺乏可微分的连续度量来直接刻画代数结构的复杂性。

Method: 将问题形式化为Cayley表补全（矩阵补全的代数对偶），以可结合性违反程度（degree of associativity violation）代替线性秩（linear rank）作为复杂度度量；对算子值张量分解HyperCube进行严格的景观分析（landscape analysis），证明其目标函数可分解为几何对齐（collinearity）与逆ℓ2惩罚（inverse ℓ2 penalty）两个连续变分分量。

Result: 建立了共线性与可结合性之间的等价关系（Collinearity–Associativity Equivalence），证明逆ℓ2惩罚在共线性流形（collinear manifold）上等价于逆秩惩罚；推导出绝对下界 H(Θ) ≥ H_inf(δ) ≥ 3|δ|，并证明该下界当且仅当目标表与某个群同痕（isotopic to a group）时达到；将全局最小化器刻画为底层群的正则表示（regular representation）（模去酉规范）。

Conclusion: 该工作证明了某些离散代数结构可以被可微分的度量精确刻画，从而实现基于梯度的发现（gradient-based discovery）而无需组合搜索；所有理论结果已通过Lean 4机械验证和小规模实验确认。

Abstract: Discovering discrete algebraic rules from data is a fundamental challenge in machine learning. We formalize this problem through Cayley-table completion -- an algebraic counterpart to classical matrix completion -- where the degree of associativity violation replaces linear rank as the intrinsic measure of complexity. We provide a rigorous landscape analysis of HyperCube, an operator-valued tensor factorization, on the fully observed target table $δ$, proving that its global infimum $H_{\inf}(δ) := \inf_{Θ\in F_δ} H(Θ)$ implicitly defines an exact differentiable measure for this complexity. We show that HyperCube's native objective $H(Θ)$ decomposes into two components: geometric alignment (collinearity) and an inverse $\ell_2$ penalty. We establish that these continuous variational pressures induce core discrete properties: collinearity enforces associativity (Collinearity--Associativity Equivalence), and the inverse $\ell_2$ penalty reduces to an exact inverse rank penalty within the collinear manifold, driving the parameters toward full-rank unitarity. Consequently, we derive an absolute lower bound $H(Θ) \ge H_{\inf}(δ) \ge 3 \, |δ|$, where $|δ|$ is the target table size. We prove this absolute floor is attained if and only if the target is isotopic to a group, and characterize the global minimizer as the regular representation of the underlying group (up to unitary gauge), resolving the central open conjecture of Huh (2025). This work serves as an existence proof that certain discrete algebraic structures can be exactly characterized by differentiable measures, enabling gradient-based discovery without the need for combinatorial search. All theoretical results are mechanically verified in Lean 4 and confirmed via small-scale experiments.

</details>


### [2] [LEAP: A closed-loop framework for perovskite precursor additive discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20242)
*Xin-De Wang,Zhi-Rui Chen,Ze-Feng Gao,Peng-Jie Guo,Cheng Mu,Zhong-Yi Lu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出LEAP框架，将领域专用大语言模型（LLM）与主动学习相结合，用于钙钛矿太阳能电池前驱体添加剂的优先排序。实验验证表明，该方法在三轮筛选中优于对照组，器件平均光电转换效率（PCE）最高达20.87%，冠军器件达21.32%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高效发现前驱体添加剂（precursor additives）对提升钙钛矿太阳能电池（perovskite solar cells）性能至关重要，但庞大的化学空间使得传统试错筛选效率低下，亟需更智能的筛选方法。

Method: 开发了LEAP（LLM-driven Exploration via Active Learning for Perovskites）框架，这是一个专家在环（expert-in-the-loop）的闭环系统，将领域专用大语言模型与主动学习（active learning）相结合；LLM从添加剂文献中提取机制相关知识，通过可解释描述符（interpretable descriptors）表示候选分子，并集成到贝叶斯优化（Bayesian optimization）流程中，在低数据条件下进行不确定性感知的优先排序。

Result: 在未见文献上的基准测试中，领域专用模型在机制一致性推理上优于通用模型。专家在环的概念验证实验中，三轮筛选的添加剂优先排序得到改善：6-CDQ和2-CNA处理组器件的平均PCE分别为20.13%和20.87%，对照组为19.25%，冠军器件PCE达21.32%。

Conclusion: 初步证据表明，基于文献的机理描述符结合贝叶斯优化与专家可行性审查，能够支持钙钛矿光伏中机制感知的添加剂优先排序。

Abstract: Efficient discovery of precursor additives is essential for improving the performance of perovskite solar cells, yet the large chemical space makes conventional trial-and-error screening inefficient. We develop LEAP(LLM-driven Exploration via Active Learning for Perovskites), an expert-in-the-loop closed framework that couples a domain-specialized large language model(LLM) with active learning for iterative additive prioritization. The LLM is trained to extract mechanism-relevant knowledge from the perovskite additive literature and to represent candidate molecules through interpretable descriptors, which are further integrated into a Bayesian optimization workflow for uncertainty-aware prioritization under low-data conditions. Benchmark results on unseen literature show that the domain-specialized model outperforms general-purpose models in mechanism-consistent reasoning. Experimental validation in an expert-in-the-loop proof-of-concept study suggests improved additive prioritization across three screening rounds, leading to average device PCEs of 20.13% and 20.87% for the later-round 6-CDQ- and 2-CNA-treated devices, respectively, compared with 19.25% for the control, with a champion PCE of 21.32%. These results provide preliminary evidence that literature-grounded mechanistic descriptors, when coupled with Bayesian optimization and expert feasibility review, can support mechanism-aware additive prioritization in perovskite photovoltaics.

</details>


### [3] [Approximation Theory for Neural Networks: Old and New](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21451)
*Soumendu Sundar Mukherjee,Himasish Talukdar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文综述了通用逼近定理（universal approximation theorems）的经典结论与近期进展，涵盖单隐层网络的密度结果、逼近率与网络规模的定量关系、深度与宽度的权衡，以及Kolmogorov–Arnold网络（KANs）这一新兴架构的逼近理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从数学上解释神经网络表达能力的基础，并为不同网络架构的设计与效率分析提供理论依据。

Method: 通过文献综述（survey）的方式，回顾经典密度结果与定量逼近界，重点分析深度-宽度权衡以及目标函数光滑性对逼近误差的影响。

Result: 单隐层前馈网络在广泛函数类中具有稠密性；定量逼近界将网络规模与逼近误差关联；深层结构在特定函数类中可取得更优的参数效率；KANs作为替代架构展现出有前景的逼近理论特性。

Conclusion: 逼近理论已从定性结果发展为丰富的定量理论，深度-宽度权衡与KANs等新架构是当前活跃的研究方向。

Abstract: Universal approximation theorems provide a mathematical explanation for the expressive power of neural networks. They assert that, under mild conditions on the activation function, feedforward neural networks are dense in broad function classes, such as continuous functions on compact subsets of $\mathbb{R}^d$, $L^p$ spaces, or Sobolev spaces. Over the past four decades, these qualitative universality results have evolved into a rich quantitative theory addressing approximation rates, parameter efficiency, and the role of architectural features such as depth and width. This survey presents several glimpses into this theory. We review classical density results for single-hidden-layer networks, as well as quantitative bounds that relate approximation error to network size and smoothness assumptions on target functions. Particular emphasis is placed on depth--width trade-offs and on results demonstrating that deeper architectures can achieve superior parameter efficiency for structured function classes. In addition to standard feedforward neural networks, we also review recent developments on Kolmogorov--Arnold Networks (KANs), which offer an alternative architectural paradigm and whose approximation-theoretic properties have begun to attract significant theoretical attention.

</details>


### [4] [Quantifying Hyperparameter Transfer and the Importance of Embedding Layer Learning Rate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21486)
*Dayal Singh Kalra,Maissam Barkeshli*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出量化超参数迁移（hyperparameter transfer）的三个指标框架，并通过大量消融实验发现，μP相比标准参数化（SP）的优势主要源于其对嵌入层学习率的放大作用，而非现有理论所解释的内容。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超参数迁移对于训练大语言模型（LLMs）至关重要，但现有理论无法充分解释为什么Maximal Update（μP）相比标准参数化（SP）能提供更高质量的学习率迁移。

Method: 首先构建一个包含三个指标的框架来量化超参数迁移：尺度律拟合质量（quality of scaling law fit）、外推误差鲁棒性（robustness to extrapolation errors）以及参数化选择导致的渐近损失惩罚（asymptotic loss penalty）。随后使用AdamW优化器进行一系列全面的消融实验。

Result: μP相对于SP的优势几乎完全源于嵌入层学习率的最大化：SP中嵌入层学习率成为导致训练不稳定的瓶颈，将其放大宽度倍（width factor）以匹配μP可显著平滑训练并改善超参数迁移；权重衰减（weight decay）改善尺度律拟合，但在固定token-per-parameter设定下会损害外推鲁棒性。

Conclusion: μP的高质量学习率迁移主要归因于嵌入层学习率的适当放大，而非现有理论解释的深层机制；嵌入层学习率是SP训练不稳定的关键瓶颈。

Abstract: Hyperparameter transfer allows extrapolating optimal optimization hyperparameters from small to large scales, making it critical for training large language models (LLMs). This is done either by fitting a scaling law to the hyperparameters or by a judicious choice of parameterization, such as Maximal Update ($μ$P), that renders optimal hyperparameters approximately scale invariant. In this paper, we first develop a framework to quantify hyperparameter transfer through three metrics: (1) the quality of the scaling law fit, (2) the robustness to extrapolation errors, and (3) the asymptotic loss penalty due to choice of parameterization. Next, we investigate through a comprehensive series of ablations why $μ$P appears to offer high-quality learning rate transfer relative to standard parameterization (SP), as existing theory is inadequate. We find that the overwhelming benefit of $μ$P relative to SP when training with AdamW arises simply from maximizing the learning rate of the embedding layer. In SP, the embedding layer learning rate acts as a bottleneck that induces training instabilities; increasing it by a factor of width to match $μ$P dramatically smooths out training while improving hyperparameter transfer. We also find that weight decay improves the scaling law fits, while, in the fixed token-per-parameter setting, it hurts the robustness of the extrapolation.

</details>

# physics.soc-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [5] [Equilibrium and dynamics of a three-state opinion model on a network of networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20979)
*Irene Ferri,Albert Díaz-Guilera,Hiroki Sayama*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过引入内部信念图（internal belief graph）和外部社交图（external social graph）的双层网络（network of networks）模型，研究了个体内在信念结构如何影响集体意见极化（opinion polarization）的临界行为。研究发现，星状（star-like）内部拓扑中临界温度随信念数量增加而上升，而环状（ring-like）和团状（clique）拓扑则呈现饱和特性；二元混合体系中主导拓扑依赖于中性参数（neutrality parameter）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统意见形成模型（opinion formation models）将每个个体简化为单一变量，忽略了个体内部信念之间相互关联的组织结构。本文旨在探索个体内部信念组织如何影响宏观集体意见的演化与稳定性。

Method: 采用双层网络（network of networks）框架，每个智能体（agent）拥有内部信念图，智能体之间通过外部社交图（external social graph）交互。信念取三种状态：两种对立极化态和一种中性态，引入中性参数（neutrality parameter）调节中性立场的相对坚定程度，并加入温度（temperature）刻画外部社会扰动与内部认知失调容忍度。在全连接外部社交图上，通过解析方法和蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulation）研究内部拓扑为一维链（one-dimensional chain）、团（clique）和星状（star-like）结构时的稳态与动力学。

Result: 星状内部拓扑中，临界温度（critical temperature）随信念数量增加而升高；而环状和团状内部拓扑中临界温度趋于饱和。对于等比例的二元混合体系，智能体间的相互作用呈现出区域依赖性（regime-dependent），主导拓扑随中性参数取值变化。

Conclusion: 个体内部信念的结构组织显著影响集体意见极化的临界行为，中性参数与内部拓扑的匹配关系决定了混合体系中的主导意见动力学模式。

Abstract: Opinion formation models typically represent each individual as a single variable. However, in practice each individual holds interconnected beliefs whose internal organization may influence collective outcomes. To explore this dependence, we study a three-state opinion model on a network of networks in which each agent has an internal belief graph and interacts with other agents through an external social graph. Each belief can take two opposite polarized states or a neutral one and a neutrality parameter tunes the relative conviction of the neutral stance. We incorporate temperature into the model to account for external social agitation and for the tolerance of internal cognitive dissonance. We explore the stationary state and dynamics of the model using analytical approaches and Monte Carlo simulations on a fully connected external social graph, with internal belief topologies given by one-dimensional chains, cliques, and star-like structures, where there is a central core belief to which all other beliefs are connected. We find that the critical temperature at which the polarized consensus destabilizes increases with the addition of more beliefs to star-like agents but saturates in the case of ring- and clique-like internal topologies. We also consider binary mixtures of agents with different internal topologies in equal proportions, showing that the interplay between agents is regime-dependent, with the dominant topology depending on the value of the neutrality parameter.

</details>

# stat.ML [[Back]](#toc)

### [6] [Memorisation, convergence and generalisation in generative models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21402)
*Antoine Maillard,Sebastian Goldt*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文通过解析线性生成模型，精确刻画了从记忆（memorisation）到泛化（generalisation）的转变。研究发现，当样本数量与输入维度成线性关系时，收敛（convergence）会连续出现，而数据主潜在因子（principal latent factors）的恢复则呈现尖锐相变。这表明生成模型的泛化至少可分解为两个不同的目标：匹配数据分布的主体与恢复主潜在因子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Kadkhodaie等人（ICLR '24）发现，基于不相交子集训练的扩散模型在大样本下会收敛到近似的密度。这引出了两个基本问题：需要多少数据才能实现收敛，以及收敛在多大程度上反映了对数据分布的学习。本文旨在从理论上回答这些问题。

Method: 作者在线性生成模型框架下进行了精确解析分析，研究了从记忆到泛化的转变。随后将分析扩展到具有幂律谱（power-law spectra）的数据，并在卷积去噪器（convolutional denoisers）以及Kadkhodaie等人的实验数据上进行了验证。

Result: 线性生成模型在小样本量下表现为记忆，当样本数量与输入维度呈线性关系时，收敛会连续出现。数据主潜在因子的恢复则表现出尖锐的相变，且收敛对主因子的恢复不敏感。在幂律谱数据和真实实验数据中，这种收敛与潜在因子恢复之间的区别同样存在。

Conclusion: 生成模型的泛化至少包含两个不同目标：匹配数据分布的主体（对应收敛）和恢复主潜在因子（对应尖锐相变）。这两个目标对应真实分布与学习分布之间的两种不同距离，而收敛仅捕获第一个目标。

Abstract: Generative neural networks learn how to produce highly realistic images from a large, but finite number of examples - or do they simply memorise their training set? To settle this question, Kadkhodaie, Guth, Simoncelli and Mallat (ICLR '24) trained diffusion models independently on disjoint subsets of a dataset and showed that they converge to nearly the same density when the number of training images is large enough. This result raises two basic questions: how much data do you need for convergence, and what does convergence capture about learning the data distribution? Here, we address these questions by providing an exact analytical characterisation of the transition from memorisation to generalisation in linear generative models. We find that these models memorise at small load, while convergence emerges continuously when the number of samples is linear in the input dimension. Strikingly, we find that convergence is insensitive to recovery of the principal latent factors of the data, which are recovered in a sharp transition. After extending our approach to data with power-law spectra, we find the same distinction between convergence and latent recovery in our experiments with convolutional denoisers and in the data of Kadkhodaie et al. We thus show that generalisation in generative models decomposes into at least two distinct objectives: matching the bulk of the data distribution and recovering the principal latent factors. These objectives correspond to two different distances between true and learnt data distribution, and only the first one is captured by convergence.

</details>


<div id='math.NA'></div>

# math.NA [[Back]](#toc)

### [7] [Persistent-Homology-Guided Topology Scanning of Qualitative Indicators for Acoustic Inverse Scattering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20673)
*Xiaomei Yang,Jiaying Jia,Zhiliang Deng*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于持续同调（persistent homology）的拓扑感知后处理框架，用于从定性逆散射（qualitative inverse scattering）方法生成的灰度指标场中自动提取散射体的二值形状，解决了传统阈值选择不稳定且无法处理多分量或带孔等非平凡拓扑的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 线性采样法（linear sampling method）和分解法（factorization method）等定性方法通过采样指标重建声学散射体，其输出为灰度场，需通过阈值化获得二值形状。然而，阈值选择通常依赖经验，在指标存在噪声伪影或散射体具有多分量、孔洞等非平凡拓扑时不稳定。为此，本文希望开发一种无需人为设定阈值、能够自动感知并利用拓扑信息进行后处理的框架。

Method: 提出一个拓扑感知后处理框架，其核心是持续同调。对于任意归一化的定性指标，计算其超水平集（superlevel sets）的持续同调，利用零维和二维持续性特征来估计或施加未知散射体的拓扑结构。随后通过最小化贝蒂数差异（Betti-number discrepancy）并加入轻微几何惩罚来选择拓扑引导的阈值。该框架与具体指标无关，可应用于线性采样指标、分解法指标或归一化融合指标，且主要公式基于单频设置。

Result: 数值测试验证了所提方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的方法能够自动、稳定地从定性逆散射指标中提取具有正确拓扑结构的二值形状，且无需针对不同指标调整算法。

Abstract: Qualitative methods such as the linear sampling method and the factorization method reconstruct acoustic scatterers through sampling indicators. In practice, these indicators are gray-scale fields on a prescribed sampling window and a binary obstacle shape is obtained only after thresholding. The choice of threshold is usually empirical and may be unstable when the indicator contains noise-induced artifacts or when the scatterer has nontrivial topology, such as multiple components or holes. This paper proposes a topology-aware postprocessing framework based on persistent homology. Given any normalized qualitative indicator, we scan the persistent homology of its superlevel sets and use the resulting zero- and one-dimensional persistent features to estimate or impose the topology of the unknown scatterer. A topology-guided threshold is then selected by minimizing a Betti-number discrepancy together with mild geometric penalties. The method is indicator-agnostic: it can be applied to the linear sampling indicator, the factorization-method indicator, or a normalized fusion of indicators. The main formulation is single-frequency and therefore remains close to the classical qualitative inverse scattering setting. We present the mathematical construction, an automatic topology detection rule based on persistence lifetimes and lifetime gaps, and a detailed algorithmic protocol for numerical implementation. Numerical tests verify that the proposed method is effective.

</details>


<div id='hep-ph'></div>

# hep-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [8] [Impact of matter effects on the unitarity test of lepton mixing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20859)
*Ryuichiro Kitano,Joe Sato,Sho Sugama*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种不依赖特定参数化形式的轻子混合矩阵（lepton mixing matrix）元素提取方法，利用长基线中微子实验（如T2HK和J-PARC的中微子工厂）的能谱信息，在考虑物质效应（matter effects）的情况下检验轻子混合矩阵的幺正性（unitarity）。以四代模型为例，通过CP共轭道和T共轭道（CP-conjugate and T-conjugate channels）的能谱观测，可最有效地进行幺正性检验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验轻子混合矩阵的幺正性是探测超出标准三代框架新物理的重要途径，类似于夸克部分CKM矩阵的幺正性检验（unitarity tests）。当前缺乏一种不依赖特定参数化形式的矩阵元素直接提取方法。

Method: 利用长基线中微子振荡实验（long baseline neutrino oscillation experiments）的能谱信息，将振荡概率公式写为混合矩阵元素组合项的和，各系数对能量依赖不同。考虑物质效应后，提取混合矩阵元素以检验幺正性，并在四代模型中通过定义幺正模型中应消失的量来进行验证。

Result: 在多种测量组合中，最有力的检验来自T2HK实验中CP共轭外观道（appearance channels）$ν_μ\to ν_e$和$\barν_μ\to \barν_e$的能谱，以及中微子工厂中T共轭对（T-conjugate pair）$ν_μ\to ν_e$和$ν_e \to ν_μ$的观测。

Conclusion: 未来长基线实验（如T2HK和中微子工厂）通过能谱信息提取混合矩阵元素，可有效检验轻子混合矩阵的幺正性，为探测超出三代框架的新物理提供有力手段。

Abstract: Testing the unitarity of the lepton mixing matrix, in a manner analogous to the unitarity tests of the CKM matrix in the quark sector, is an important step toward probing physics beyond the standard three-generation framework. In long baseline neutrino oscillation experiments, the formula of the oscillation probabilities can be written as a sum of terms with various combinations of the mixing-matrix elements, and their coefficients depend differently on energy. By observing the spectral information of long baseline experiments such as T2HK and a future neutrino factory at J-PARC with a $ν_e$ beam, the elements of the mixing matrix can be extracted without assuming a specific parametrization of the mixing matrix. We investigate how such an extraction method can be applied to neutrino oscillations by taking into account matter effects, and discuss how one can test unitarity of the mixing matrix in future long baseline experiments. As a concrete example, we examine the unitarity test by using a four-generation model, where we look at a quantity which should be vanishing in a unitary model. Among possible combinations of measurements, the most powerful test can be provided from the energy spectra of the CP-conjugate appearance channels $ν_μ\to ν_e$ and $\barν_μ\to \barν_e$ at T2HK, as well as from the T-conjugate pair $ν_μ\to ν_e$ and $ν_e \to ν_μ$ available at neutrino factories.

</details>


### [9] [The Single Photon Signature of a Light Long-lived Neutralino at Remote Detectors at the LHC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21065)
*Herbi K. Dreiner,Julian Günther,Dominik Köhler,Apoorva Shah*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了LHC上多个远程探测器（remote detectors）对轻长寿命中性层子（long-lived neutralinos）在破缺R宇称（R-parity violating）超对称模型中的探测灵敏度，发现在所考虑的基准场景中ANUBIS灵敏度最高，FASER最低但已开始采集数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究主要聚焦于FASER和FASER2两个探测器，而对其他远程探测器在破缺R宇称超对称模型下对长寿命中性层子的探测能力缺乏系统比较；此外，以往模拟未充分考虑母介子（parent meson）的延长飞行路径（extended flight path）带来的影响。

Method: 在破缺R宇称超对称模型中，假设中性层子通过稀有标量介子衰变（rare scalar meson decays）在ATLAS或CMS对撞点产生，并考虑中性层子主导衰变通道为~χ^0_1→γ+ν。针对六个破缺R宇称基准场景（benchmark scenarios），改进了模拟方法，将母介子的延长飞行路径纳入计算，依次评估ANUBIS、CODEX-b、FACET、FASER、FASER2、MAPP、MAPP2和MATHUSLA八个远程探测器的预期搜索灵敏度（projected search sensitivity）。

Result: 在所有考虑的实验中，ANUBIS对所选基准场景的探测灵敏度最佳，而FASER的灵敏度最差；但FASER已实际采集了数据。

Conclusion: 不同远程探测器在搜索破缺R宇称超对称模型中的长寿命中性层子时灵敏度差异显著，ANUBIS在理论预期上表现最优；改进母介子飞行路径的模拟方法有助于获得更准确的灵敏度估计。

Abstract: We investigate the phenomenology of light long-lived neutralinos in R-parity violating supersymmetric models, focusing on the proposed remote detectors $\texttt{ANUBIS}$, $\texttt{CODEX-b}$, $\texttt{FACET}$, $\texttt{FASER}$, $\texttt{FASER2}$, $\texttt{MAPP}$, $\texttt{MAPP2}$, and $\texttt{MATHUSLA}$ at the LHC. We assume the production of the neutralinos at the ATLAS or CMS interaction points via rare scalar meson decays induced by R-parity violating couplings. We study six supersymmetric R-parity violating benchmark scenarios in which the dominant neutralino decay is $\tildeχ^0_1 \rightarrow γ+ ν$. For each scenario, we determine the projected search sensitivity at the above listed detectors. Extending previous work focused primarily on $\texttt{FASER}$ and $\texttt{FASER2}$, we improve the simulation by taking into account the extended flight path of the parent meson. We find that $\texttt{ANUBIS}$ provides the best sensitivity to our benchmark scenarios and $\texttt{FASER}$ the least among the considered experiments, while of course $\texttt{FASER}$ has already taken data.

### [10] [Impact of Hadronic Resonances on $B\to K^{(*)}τ^+τ^-$ decays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21291)
*Guillermo Baltà,Andreas Crivellin,Rafel Escribano,Joaquim Matias,Martín Novoa-Brunet*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种将共振贡献（尤其是ψ(2S)）纳入B→K^(*)τ^+τ^-衰变预言的新策略，而非回避这些共振效应。利用LHCb对B→K^(*)μ^+μ^-的数据驱动方法，给出不同初始运动学点的预言；发现包含共振能显著增强标准模型预言，但在足够大的新物理贡献下短距离贡献可超越共振效应，从而可借助共振区相空间探测新物理，并适用于无法分辨共振的强子对撞机数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中微子味中性流（neutral-current）半轻子B衰变受到强子共振（hadronic resonances）的严重干扰。对于轻子（e, μ）可通过q²截断回避共振，但对τ模式因中微子能量缺失难以重建q²，这在强子对撞机环境下尤为困难，因此需要描述共振效应以正确解读b→sτ⁺τ⁻测量结果。

Method: 采用包含共振贡献（特别是ψ(2S)）而非回避的方法，基于LHCb对B→K^(*)μ^+μ^-衰变的测量数据，通过数据驱动（data-driven）方法对B→K^(*)τ⁺τ⁻衰变给出1.预言。分别计算了4m_τ²、14.18 GeV²和15 GeV²等不同初始运动学点（initial kinematic points）的结果，以适应LHCb、CMS和Belle II的实验条件。

Result: 包含共振并在全q²范围积分后，标准模型（Standard Model）预言显著增强。但在R(D^(*))和B→K^(*)νν衰变现有张力的新物理（New Physics）足够大时，短距离贡献（short-distance contribution）可与共振贡献相当甚至超越。量化了是否包含共振对总分支比的影响。

Conclusion: 该策略具有双重优势：一是利用共振区的额外相空间（phase space）探测大新物理贡献，二是使其适用于无法分辨共振的强子对撞机数据（如LHCb、CMS），扩展了B→K^(*)τ⁺τ⁻衰变在搜索新物理方面的实验可及性。

Abstract: Neutral-current semileptonic $B$ decays are plagued by hadronic resonances across the dilepton invariant-mass squared spectrum, $q^2$. For light leptons, $\ell=e,μ$, these resonances can be avoided with suitable $q^2$ cuts. This strategy is less straightforward for $τ$ modes, where missing energy from the $τ$ decay makes $q^2$ difficult to reconstruct. In fact, while Belle II is able to discriminate between different regions in $q^2$ due to its clean environment, this is not directly possible in a hadronic one. Therefore, the interpretation of $b\to sτ^+τ^-$ measurements from e.g. LHCb, CMS requires the description of these resonant effects. In this article, we adopt a different strategy by including the resonant contributions (in particular from $ψ(2S)$) into our predictions for $B\to K^{(*)}τ^+τ^-$ decays, instead of avoiding them. We provide predictions for different initial kinematic points ($4m_τ^2, 14.18\,$GeV$^2$ and $15\,$GeV$^2$) that can be convenient for LHCb, CMS and Belle II. For this, we use a data-driven approach based on the LHCb measurements of $B\to K^{(*)}μ^+μ^-$ decays. Including the resonances and integrating over the full $q^2$ range substantially enhances the Standard Model predictions. However, for sufficiently large New Physics, motivated by the current tensions in $R(D^{(*)})$ and $B\to K^{(*)}νν$ decays, the short-distance contribution becomes comparable to or even exceeds the resonant one. This highlights two advantages of this strategy: it exploits the additional phase space associated with the resonant regions to probe large New Physics contributions, and it enables the use of hadron-collider data, where the resonances cannot be resolved. We further quantify how including or neglecting the resonances affects the total branching ratio as a function of New Physics contributions and, equivalently, of the experimental precision.

</details>


### [11] [Statistical sensitivity of neutrinoless double-beta decay exchange mechanism discrimination by tracking experiments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21315)
*Jason Detwiler,Ke Han,Tao Li*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，即使只有少量（约10–25个）经过良好重建的无中微子双β衰变（neutrinoless double-beta decay）事件，也能在1σ到3σ显著性水平上区分其背后的超越标准模型（beyond-the-Standard-Model）交换机制，挑战了“需要高统计量”的常见观点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 重建无中微子双β衰变中电子的单个能量及它们之间的张角，有望揭示该过程背后的超越标准模型交换机制（exchange mechanism）。然而，常有人认为这类机制区分需要高统计量测量；本文旨在检验这一观点是否正确。

Method: 作者通过理论分析，研究了在单一机制主导衰变过程的假设下，所需事件数随显著性水平（σ）的变化，并考虑了实际重建不确定性的影响。

Result: 在理想条件下，仅需几个良好重建的事件即可在1σ水平上区分机制；达到3σ发现灵敏度仅需约10个事件。计入实际重建不确定性后，所需事件数增至约25个，表明只要本底（background）足够小，区分能力仍能保持。

Conclusion: 即使对于预期信号计数很少的“发现级”（discovery-class）实验，发展径迹探测器（tracking detectors）以用于交换机制区分仍然具有重要价值。

Abstract: Reconstruction of the individual energies and the opening angle between the electrons emitted in neutrinoless double-beta decay can probe the nature of the beyond-the-Standard-Model exchange mechanism that underlies the process. Although it is often stated that discrimination of the mechanism would require such measurements to be performed with high statistics, we show that this is not the case. If a single mechanism dominates the process, its discrimination at the 1$σ$ level is already achieved with just a few well-reconstructed events; only $\sim$10 such events are required to reach 3$σ$-level discovery sensitivity. In the presence of realistic reconstruction uncertainties, this requirement increases to $\sim$25 events, indicating that substantial discrimination power is retained as long as backgrounds remain small. We conclude that the pursuit of tracking detectors for exchange-mechanism discrimination remains valuable even for ``discovery-class'' experiments in which only a few signal counts are expected.

### [12] [Sensitivity of the FCC-ee to axion-like particles at different center-of-mass energies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21452)
*Juliette Alimena,Elnura Bakhishova,Freya Blekman,Jannah Darwish Abdelhafiz,Christina Dorofeev,Jeremi Niedziela,Giacomo Polesello,Anna Przybyl,Lovisa Rygaard*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了未来对撞机FCC-ee在全部计划质心能量下对轴子类似粒子（axion-like particles, ALPs）的探测灵敏度，重点关注ALP主要与电弱规范玻色子（electroweak gauge bosons）耦合的情形。通过分析ALP与光子联合产生后衰变为双光子的三光子末态过程，发现FCC-ee在Z极点运行期间可将耦合灵敏度压低至$10^{-6} \mathrm{GeV}^{-1}$量级，在WW、ZH和$t\bar{t}$阈值运行期间可达$10^{-5} \mathrm{GeV}^{-1}$量级。对于质量低于$Z$玻色子质量的ALP，该末态还有潜力探测ALP耦合的电弱结构。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在Z极点运行期间，FCC-ee可将ALP与光子的耦合灵敏度探测至$10^{-6} \mathrm{GeV}^{-1}$量级；在WW、ZH和$t\bar{t}$阈值运行期间，灵敏度可达$10^{-5} \mathrm{GeV}^{-1}$量级。对于质量低于$Z$玻色子质量的ALP，三光子末态还能揭示ALP耦合中潜在的完整电弱结构信息。

Conclusion: FCC-ee通过三光子末态过程能够对ALP与电弱规范玻色子的耦合实现高灵敏度探测，并能对质量低于$Z$玻色子质量的ALP提供关于其耦合电弱结构（electroweak structure）的额外物理信息。

Abstract: The sensitivity of the proposed FCC-ee collider to axion-like particles (ALPs) is investigated at all planned center-of-mass energies, with focus on the case where the ALP couples primarily to electroweak gauge bosons at leading order. We study the associated production of the ALP with a photon, with the ALP decaying in turn to two photons, yielding a three-photon final state. The ALP coupling to the photon is evaluated for ALP masses of 5 to 320 GeV. In this effective model, the FCC-ee will be able to detect ALPs for couplings down to a few $10^{-6} \mathrm{GeV}^{-1}$ ($10^{-5} \mathrm{GeV}^{-1}$) during the Z pole run (WW, ZH, and $t\bar{t}$ threshold runs). Additionally, this final state has the potential to probe the underlying electroweak structure of ALP couplings for ALP masses below the $Z$-boson mass.

### [13] [Explicit Conditions for Diagnosing Tree-Level Unitarity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12057)
*Jaehoon Jeong,Pyungwon Ko,Yu-Hui Zheng*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文系统推导了自旋≤1的粒子体系中树级幺正性（tree unitarity）所需的所有耦合条件，证明四点振幅可通过树级幺正性条件实现壳上构造（on-shell constructible），并指出五点点振幅已完全涵盖所有约束，无需检验更高点振幅。应用于暗扇区（dark sector）发现，无标量粒子（scalar）的理论需要无限多的矢量（vector）和费米子（fermion）塔才能满足树级幺正性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有树级幺正性条件缺乏对所有自旋≤1粒子的系统化表述，且依赖完整拉格朗日量（Lagrangian）的重构；本文旨在仅基于质量本征态（mass basis）下的粒子内容来诊断树级幺正性，避免重建完整拉格朗日量，并澄清高阶振幅检验的必要性。

Method: 通过分析四点振幅的高能增长行为导出树级幺正性条件；利用Stückelberg形式（Stückelberg formulation）简化拉格朗日量结构，从更高点振幅中推导相应的树级幺正性条件；并证明所有条件在五点点振幅层面已完全收敛。

Result: 所有四点振幅在满足树级幺正性条件后均可在壳上构造；树级幺正性条件至多到五点点振幅即可完全捕获，无需考虑更高点振幅；对于无标量粒子的理论，树级幺正性要求无限多的矢量与费米子塔；应用于暗光子（dark photon）暗扇区，分析了质量生成的关键特征。

Conclusion: 本文提供了一套系统诊断自旋≤1粒子体系树级幺正性的方法，大幅简化了理论检验流程，并为暗扇区及无标量理论的结构约束提供了重要结论。最后简要讨论了希格斯门户（Higgs portal）矢量暗物质模型（VDM）中的幺正性问题。

Abstract: We explicitly present all coupling conditions required for tree-level unitarity (tree unitarity) in theories with a finite number of massive and massless particles of spin up to 1. They allow us to diagnose tree unitarity of a system using only its particle content in the mass basis, without reconstructing the full Lagrangian. We show that all four-point amplitudes whose high-energy growth is canceled by tree unitarity conditions are on-shell constructible, thereby motivating the recursive construction of four-point amplitudes. By examining their high-energy growth, we derive tree unitarity conditions for four-point amplitudes. Imposing these conditions to simplify the Lagrangian structure, we use the Stückelberg formulation to derive the tree unitarity conditions arising from all higher-point amplitudes. We show that all tree unitarity conditions are fully captured up to five-point amplitudes, ensuring no necessity of examining higher-point ones. We apply our results to systematically examine tree unitarity conditions in the dark sector with a massive dark photon and dark matter particles of spin up to 1, and extract the essential features for mass generation in the massive dark photon case. In addition, we show that our results allow us to conclude that theories without scalars require an infinite tower of vectors and fermions for tree unitarity. Finally unitarity and related issues in the Higgs portal VDM are discussed in brief.

</details>


### [14] [Indirect Parametric Resonance of the Electromagnetic Field Driven by an Oscillating SU(2) Dark Matter Condensate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20333)
*Tatsuya Daniel,Vahid Kamali,Robert Brandenberger*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究闵可夫斯基时空下一块局域的类轴子暗区（axion-like dark sector），包含初始均匀各向同性的非阿贝尔SU(2)凝聚体和一个实赝标量场χ，后者通过Chern-Simons相互作用分别耦合到阿贝尔U(1)规范场（可对应普通电磁场）和SU(2)凝聚体。分析表明，均匀振荡的SU(2)背景Q(t)作为周期性源驱动χ，产生振荡凝聚体，进而调制U(1)螺旋度模的频率；在线性区得到Hill方程（第一谐波主导时简化为Mathieu方程），推导了共振条件、Floquet指数及两级放大条件，并指出在精确周期零偏置极限下该间接共振本征地不具有手征性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索类轴子暗区中非阿贝尔SU(2)凝聚体通过赝标量场χ对阿贝尔U(1)规范场（如电磁场）的间接共振放大机制，揭示其线性动力学特征及手征性（chirality）性质。

Method: 采用解析分析方法：将均匀振荡的SU(2)背景Q(t)视为周期性源，驱动赝标量场χ产生振荡凝聚体；进而分析χ对U(1)螺旋度模频率的调制，在线性近似下导出Hill方程，并在第一谐波主导时简化为Mathieu方程（Mathieu equation）；推导共振条件、主导Floquet指数（Floquet exponent）及两级放大条件。

Result: 获得了间接共振的近似共振条件、主导Floquet指数以及Q→χ→U(1)两级增强的条件；同时发现，在精确周期零偏置极限下，该间接共振不具内在手征性，因为两种阿贝尔螺旋度（helicities）之间存在半周期时间平移对称性。

Conclusion: 均匀振荡的SU(2)凝聚体可通过赝标量场χ间接驱动U(1)规范场的参数共振（parametric resonance），此过程在特定条件下可实现两级放大，但非本征地手征。

Abstract: We study a local patch of an axion-like dark sector in Minkowski spacetime, containing an initially homogeneous and isotropic non-Abelian $SU(2)$ condensate, and a real pseudoscalar field $χ$, coupled to an Abelian $U(1)$ gauge field which could be that of usual electromagnetism. The pseudoscalar couples directly to both gauge sectors through Chern-Simons interactions, while the $U(1)$ field couples to the $SU(2)$ condensate only indirectly, through the pseudoscalar. We show analytically that a homogeneous oscillating $SU(2)$ background $Q(t)$ acts as a periodic source for $χ$, generating a homogeneous oscillatory condensate $\dotχ$ that in turn modulates the frequency of the $U(1)$ helicity modes. In the linear regime this produces a Hill equation, and when the first harmonic dominates it reduces to a Mathieu equation. We derive the approximate resonance conditions, the leading Floquet exponent, and the conditions for a two-stage enhancement $Q \to χ\to U(1)$. We also highlight an important point: in the exactly periodic, zero-bias limit, the indirect resonance is not intrinsically chiral, because the two Abelian helicities are related by a half-period time shift.

</details>


### [15] [First mass determination of electroweak vortex rings in the Standard Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20791)
*Dan Zhu,Xurong Chen,Qingyue Zhang,Khai-Ming Wong*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文首次严格评估了电弱涡环（electroweak vortex rings）的物理质量，确定了两种不同绕数（winding numbers）解的质量分别为18.01 TeV和26.80 TeV；通过内部分析揭示了排斥相互作用对几何结构的塑造作用，以及复杂电流分布导致的安培环路定律（Ampere's circuital law）中性类比，暗示存在自稳定箍缩机制（self-stabilizing pinch mechanism），从而为未来对撞机观测这类拓扑结构（topological structures）设定了能量标度，并为理解标准模型（Standard Model）中的拓扑结构提供了框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 填补电弱涡环物理质量缺乏严格评估的空白，并为未来在高能对撞机实验中观测这类拓扑激发态提供能量标度依据。

Method: 通过严格计算对两种不同绕数（winding numbers）的电弱涡环解进行物理质量评估，并对其内部几何结构、排斥相互作用以及电流分布进行理论分析。

Result: 确定了两种绕数不同的电弱涡环的精确质量分别为18.01 TeV和26.80 TeV；发现排斥相互作用决定了构型的几何形状，而复杂电流分布则产生了安培环路定律（Ampere's circuital law）的中性化类比，进而暗示存在自稳定箍缩机制（self-stabilizing pinch mechanism）。

Conclusion: 上述质量标度为未来对撞机实验中观测电弱涡环提供了能量参考，同时为理解标准模型（Standard Model）中的拓扑结构（topological structures）建立了一个理论框架。

Abstract: We report the first rigorous evaluation of the physical mass of electroweak vortex rings, establishing precise values of 18.01 and 26.80 TeV for solutions characterized by different winding numbers. Analysis of the internal structure reveals that repulsive interactions shape the geometry of these configurations, while complex current distributions lead to a neutral analogue of Ampere's circuital law, suggesting a corresponding self-stabilizing pinch mechanism. These findings set the energy scales for the potential observation of such configurations at future colliders and offer a framework for understanding topological structures in the Standard Model.

</details>


### [16] [Cosmological History of Flavour Deconstruction Models: Constraints from Monopole Production](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20332)
*Marko Pesut,Davide Racco,Yunlong Zhao*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文揭示了标准模型扩展中低尺度半单群嵌入与早期宇宙磁单极子现象学之间的通用联系，指出味道非普适模型自然产生质量远低于大统一理论（GUT）尺度的轻磁单极子，并联合宇宙学、天体物理与直接搜寻约束压低允许的暴胀窗口，从而将味道物理与早期宇宙热历史直接关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探索标准模型（Standard Model）扩展中低尺度半单规范群嵌入与磁单极子（magnetic monopole）早期宇宙现象学之间的通用联系，并利用味道非普适（flavour non-universal）模型框架来协调汤川耦合（Yukawa couplings）的层级结构（hierarchical structure）与TeV尺度附近新动力学之间的自洽性。

Method: 通过分析半单规范群（semi-simple gauge groups）的序贯破缺（sequential breaking）过程（中间阶段包含未破缺的U(1)因子）来研究轻磁单极子的产生机制；综合宇宙学、天体物理与直接搜寻（direct-search）约束来限定模型参数区域。

Result: 模型自然预言的参数区域要求低尺度暴胀（low-scale inflation）以稀释磁单极子，随后重加热（reheating）温度低于磁单极子产生能标（约10^3–10^4 TeV）；该结果显著缩小了原本允许的暴胀窗口（inflationary window）。

Conclusion: 建立了味道物理（flavour physics）与早期宇宙热历史（thermal history）之间的直接联系：未来味道非普适相互作用的证据将指向低尺度重加热，而对原初引力波（primordial gravitational waves）的探测可直接约束味道模型中半单规范群出现的能标。

Abstract: We highlight a generic connection between extensions of the Standard Model featuring low-scale semi-simple embeddings of $\rm{U}(1)_{\rm EM}$ and the phenomenology of magnetic monopoles in the early Universe. In particular, flavour non-universal models provide a well-motivated framework to address the hierarchical structure of Yukawa couplings while allowing new dynamics close to the TeV scale compatible with experimental bounds. In these constructions, the sequential breaking of semi-simple gauge groups through intermediate stages containing an unbroken $\rm{U}(1)$ factor generically leads to the production of light magnetic monopoles whose masses are set by scales far below the scale of Grand Unified Theories. Combining cosmological, astrophysical, and direct-search constraints, the parameter region naturally predicted by these models requires low-scale inflation to dilute the monopoles, followed by reheating below the monopole-production scale, typically around $10^{3}\text{--}10^4\,\mathrm{TeV}$. These results significantly reduce the otherwise large allowed inflationary window and establish a direct connection between flavour physics and the thermal history of the early Universe: future evidence for flavour non-universal interactions would point towards a low-scale reheating, while probes of primordial gravitational waves could directly constrain the scale at which semi-simple groups can appear in flavour models.

</details>


### [17] [$D^0$--$D_s^+$ elliptic-flow splitting from sequential hadronization in O--O collisions at $\sqrt{s_{NN}} = 5.36$ TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21222)
*Hui Du,Xiao-Wei Hao,Wei Dai,Jiaxing Zhao,Ben-Wei Zhang,Enke Wang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在重夸克输运框架与顺序强子化（sequential hadronization）模型下，研究了O-O和Pb-Pb碰撞中$D^0$与$D_s^+$介子的椭圆流劈裂（elliptic-flow splitting），发现$D^0$的$v_2$大于$D_s^+$的$v_2$，O-O碰撞中的劈裂显著小于Pb-Pb碰撞，且两者之间存在普适线性标度关系，表明该劈裂可作为夸克-胶子等离子体的强子化计时器（hadronization chronometer）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究不同强子化温度下$D^0$（在$T_c$处形成）与$D_s^+$（在$1.2\,T_c$处形成）之间的椭圆流劈裂，以验证顺序强子化场景能否解释实验观测到的$v_2(D^0) > v_2(D_s^+)$顺序，并检验O-O碰撞作为一种较小系统是否也能产生可观测的劈裂信号。

Method: 采用重夸克输运框架（heavy-quark transport framework）结合顺序强子化机制，其中$D_s^+$在温度$1.2\,T_c$时形成，$D^0$在温度$T_c$时形成。研究对比了顺序强子化与同时强子化（simultaneous hadronization）基线场景，并在O-O与Pb-Pb碰撞的多个碰撞构型下进行系统扫描。

Result: 顺序强子化场景成功重现了ALICE初步数据中$v_2(D^0) > v_2(D_s^+)$的顺序，并预测低$p_T$区$D_s^+/D^0$产额比增强；而同时强子化基线给出相反的$v_2$顺序。O-O碰撞中的劈裂显著小于Pb-Pb碰撞（$30$--$50\%$），归因于初始几何偏心率（eccentricity）与$1.2\,T_c \to T_c$演化窗口时长的竞争。九个碰撞构型的系统扫描揭示了强子化劈裂与这一窗口内部分子流增量（partonic flow increment）之间的普适线性标度关系。

Conclusion: $D^0$与$D_s^+$之间的椭圆流劈裂可作为一种强子化计时器（hadronization chronometer），用于诊断夸克-胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma）的强子化时间序列。

Abstract: We investigate the elliptic-flow splitting between prompt $D^0$ and $D_s^+$ mesons in O--O and Pb--Pb collisions within a heavy-quark transport framework with sequential hadronization, in which $D_s^+$ forms at $1.2\,T_c$ and $D^0$ at $T_c$. We present predictions for the $p_T$-differential $v_2$ and $D_s^+/D^0$ yield ratio in O--O $0$--$20\%$ collisions at $\sqrt{s_{NN}} = 5.36$~TeV. The sequential scenario reproduces the $v_2(D^0) > v_2(D_s^+)$ ordering observed in preliminary ALICE data and predicts an enhanced $D_s^+/D^0$ ratio at low $p_T$, whereas a simultaneous baseline yields the opposite $v_2$ ordering. The splitting in O--O is substantially smaller than in Pb--Pb $30$--$50\%$, which we trace to the competition between the initial geometric eccentricity and the duration of the $1.2\,T_c \to T_c$ evolution window. A systematic scan across nine collision configurations reveals a universal linear scaling between the hadronic splitting and the partonic flow increment accumulated during this window, establishing the $D^0$--$D_s^+$ flow splitting as a hadronization chronometer of the quark-gluon plasma.

</details>


### [18] [Self-Consistent Parker Bound on Magnetic Monopoles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21281)
*Chen Zhang,Chun-Yan Jiang,Nayun Jia,Xin Zhang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于星系平均场发电机（galactic mean-field dynamo）的最低本征模，构建了一个自洽的帕克极限（Parker bound），用于约束磁单极子（magnetic monopole）的通量。研究发现，小尺度湍流场（small-scale turbulent fields）通过随机加速（stochastic acceleration）决定单极子速度，并影响了标准扩展帕克极限，尤其是在低中质量区域。所得通量上限对原初磁场（primordial magnetic fields, PMFs）具有鲁棒性，除非原初磁场强到受莱曼α（Lyα）数据或21厘米与宇宙学探针约束的程度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁单极子是大统一理论（grand unified theories, GUTs）中的普遍预言，并能为电荷量子化（charge quantization）提供自然解释。除对撞机搜索和宇宙线实验外，其通量受到帕克型边界（Parker-type bounds）的限制，该边界要求银河磁场不能因单极子能量提取（energy extraction）而消亡。

Method: 将帕克极限锚定于银河平均场发电机（galactic mean-field dynamo）的最低本征模（lowest eigenmode），并将所得限值转换为当前单极子通量。同时纳入小尺度湍流场（small-scale turbulent fields）的双重作用：既为发电机本征模提供种子（seed），又通过随机加速度决定单极子从相干场（coherent field）提取能量前的速度。

Result: 这些不可避免的效应显著修改了标准扩展帕克极限（standard extended Parker bound）在低质量与中间质量区域的行为。所得通量上限对原初磁场（primordial magnetic fields, PMFs）具有鲁棒性；能够改变这一上限的足够强的原初磁场，要么已受莱曼α数据约束，要么可通过21厘米（21-cm）和宇宙学探针（cosmological probes）进行检验。

Conclusion: 研究表明，通过自洽考虑湍流加速和发电机本征模，可以得到更为鲁棒的磁单极子通量上限。强原初磁场场景的可检验性为未来的宇宙学观测提供了额外约束途径。

Abstract: Magnetic monopoles arise generically in unified theories and offer a natural explanation of charge quantization. Beyond collider searches and cosmic-ray experiments, their flux is constrained by Parker-type bounds requiring galactic magnetic fields to survive monopole energy extraction. We formulate a self-consistent Parker bound anchored in the lowest eigenmode of the galactic mean-field dynamo and convert the resulting limit to the present flux. Small-scale turbulent fields both seed this eigenmode and set the monopole velocity via stochastic acceleration before energy extraction from the coherent field. These unavoidable effects substantially modify the standard extended Parker bound at low and intermediate masses, yielding flux limits robust to primordial magnetic fields (PMFs); PMFs strong enough to alter them lie in regimes constrained by Ly$α$ data or testable by 21-cm and cosmological probes.

</details>


### [19] [Cosmological Collider Signatures from Right-Handed Neutrino Loop](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21419)
*Jingtao You,Linghao Song,Chengcheng Han,Hong-Jian He,Xingang Chen,Zhong-Zhi Xianyu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究在暴胀（inflation）与中微子跷跷板机制（seesaw mechanism）相结合的框架下，由右手中微子圈产生的宇宙学对撞机（cosmological collider, CC）信号。通过引入保持移位对称性的维度-5算符，诱导产生有效化学势，从而增强手征依赖的右手中微子产生及CC信号。利用Schwinger-Keldysh形式论推导费米子传播子的种子积分，计算三点暴胀子关联函数中的非局域贡献，并指出化学势可显著缓解重质量玻尔兹曼抑制、放大振荡非高斯性信号，为分析费米子圈信号提供了系统框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索暴胀与中微子跷跷板机制耦合下，右手中微子圈在宇宙学对撞机物理中产生的可观测信号，揭示重型右手中微子可能留下的原初非高斯性（primordial non-Gaussianities）印记。

Method: 通过保持移位对称性（shift symmetry）的维度-5算符构建暴胀子（inflaton）与右手中微子的相互作用，引入有效化学势；使用两分量Weyl旋量（two-component Weyl spinor）描述具有马约拉纳质量项（Majorana mass term）的右手中微子；采用Schwinger-Keldysh（SK）形式论推导右手中微子传播子的种子积分，并计算三点暴胀子关联函数中由右手中微子三角形圈产生的因子化非局域贡献。

Result: 化学势能够显著缓解重质量玻尔兹曼抑制（Boltzmann suppression），并放大主导手征模式（helicity mode）相关的振荡非高斯性信号。

Conclusion: 本研究为分析宇宙学对撞机物理中的费米子圈信号提供了系统框架，并表明跷跷板机制中的重型右手中微子可能在原初非高斯性中留下可观测的印记。

Abstract: We study cosmological collider (CC) signatures generated by right-handed neutrino loops in the setup of inflation combined with neutrino seesaw mechanism. We formulate the inflaton interaction with the right-handed neutrino through a unique dimension-5 operator respecting shift symmetry, which induces an effective chemical potential in the slow-roll background, leading to helicity-dependent right-handed-neutrino production and enhancing the CC signatures. The right-handed neutrino is described by two-component Weyl spinor with Majorana mass term. Using the Schwinger-Keldysh (SK) formalism, we derive a set of seed integrals for fermion propagators of the right-handed Majorana neutrino. With these we compute the factorized nonlocal contributions to the three-point inflaton correlator generated by the right-handed-neutrino triangle loop. We show that the chemical potential can substantially soften the heavy-mass Boltzmann suppression and amplify the oscillatory non-Gaussianity signatures associated with the dominant helicity mode. These provide a systematic framework for analyzing the fermion loop signatures in the cosmological collider physics and demonstrate that the heavy right-handed neutrinos associated with seesaw mechanism may leave observable imprints in the primordial non-Gaussianities.

</details>


### [20] [Gravitational Waves from Black Hole Reheating: The Scalar-Induced Component](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21474)
*Yann Gouttenoire,Nicholas Leister,Pedro Schwaller*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了原初黑洞（PBH）蒸发产生的Poltergeist随机引力波背景，发现考虑广义相对论引力坍缩所蕴含的不可约质量展宽（红外尾标度 $d f_{\rm PBH}/d\ln M_{\rm PBH}\propto M_{\rm PBH}^{3.78}$）后，该信号会被抑制数个数量级，降至与标量诱导引力波相当的水平。对八种标量诱导频谱产生通道的完整分解表明，除PBH形成通道外，其他通道均无法触及 $\Delta N_{\rm eff}$ 上限或未来引力波观测台的预期灵敏度，从而重新开放了此前被认为已被排除的超轻PBH参数空间区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原初黑洞（primordial black holes, PBHs）蒸发再加热宇宙的过程会在早期宇宙中留下随机引力波（gravitational-wave, GW）背景。在单色（monochromatic）极限近似下，PBH的同时蒸发会产生突然的物质-辐射相变，触发所谓的Poltergeist GW信号，该信号通常被认为占主导且可观测。本文的动机是检验这一结论在考虑更现实的质量展宽后的可靠性。

Method: 研究通过纳入广义相对论（General Relativity）引力坍缩所蕴含的不可约质量展宽（其红外尾标度为 $d f_{\rm PBH}/d\ln M_{\rm PBH}\propto M_{\rm PBH}^{3.78}$），重新计算了PBH蒸发产生的GW背景。同时，对早期物质主导时期产生的标量诱导引力波（scalar-induced GW signal）频谱进行了完整的八通道分解分析。

Result: 最小质量展宽足以将再加热过程平滑化，使Poltergeist背景被抑制数个数量级，降至与一般早期物质时期（如重粒子衰变驱动）产生的标量诱导GW信号相当的水平。在八个产生通道中，除PBH形成通道外，其余通道均未达到 $\Delta N_{\rm eff}$ 约束上限或未来GW观测台的预期灵敏度。

Conclusion: 原先被认为已被排除的超轻PBH参数空间区域因该结果而被重新开放。这表明，在评估PBH蒸发产生的GW信号时，必须考虑质量展宽等现实物理效应，否则会高估信号的观测可行性。

Abstract: The reheating of the universe by the evaporation of light primordial black holes (PBHs) can leave a stochastic gravitational-wave (GW) background in the early Universe. In the monochromatic limit, their simultaneous evaporation produces an abrupt matter-to-radiation transition, triggering the so-called Poltergeist GW signal, usually predicted to be dominant and observable. We revisit this result by including the irreducible mass spread implied by gravitational collapse in General Relativity, whose infrared tail scales as $d f_{\rm PBH}/d\ln M_{\rm PBH}\propto M_{\rm PBH}^{3.78}$. We show that this minimal width smooths reheating enough to suppress the Poltergeist background by orders of magnitude, down to the level of the scalar-induced GW signal produced during a generic early matter era, such as one driven by the decay of a heavy relic. We provide a complete decomposition of the scalar-induced spectrum into eight production channels and find that none, except the one from PBH formation, reaches either the $ΔN_{\rm eff}$ bound or the projected sensitivity of future GW observatories. This reopens regions of ultra-light PBH parameter space previously thought to be excluded by these constraints.

</details>

### [21] [Double-transform Tauberian method for precise large deviations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21005)
*Giampaolo Cristadoro,Gaia Pozzoli*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文将针对单变量拉普拉斯-斯蒂尔切斯变换的 Tauber 方法扩展至双变量（bivariate）情形，用于分析属于谱正稳定律（spectrally positive stable laws）吸引域中的随机过程的大偏差行为，并通过对随机和与路径依赖观测量的具体示例展示了该方法在描述渐近行为方面的优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在许多随机模型中，可观测量（observables）自然地编码在耦合空间变量与时间变量的双变换（double transforms，例如拉普拉斯变换）之中，而且双变换往往是研究具有相关增量或路径约束（path constraints）过程的唯一解析上可行的出发点。现有单变量 Tauber 方法虽能处理部分大偏差问题，但尚缺乏面向双变量情形的系统扩展。

Method: 本文将此前针对单变量拉普拉斯-斯蒂尔切斯变换（Laplace–Stieltjes transforms）开发的 Tauber 方法（Tauberian approach）扩展至双变量情形，用于处理属于谱正稳定律吸引域的随机过程的精确大偏差（precise large deviations）。

Result: 通过两个示例展示了该方法的有效性：一是增量与停时（stopping time）相关的随机和（random sums）的精确大偏差；二是受限于保持正值（positive）的随机游走（random walks）的路径依赖可观测量（path-dependent observables）的精确大偏差。

Conclusion: 该双变量 Tauber 方法为利用双变换直接获取渐近行为提供了途径，弥补了单变换技术难以刻画此类行为的不足，从而扩展了对具有相关增量或路径约束的随机过程的大偏差分析能力。

Abstract: In many stochastic models, the observables of interest are naturally encoded in double transforms (e.g., Laplace transforms) that couple spatial and temporal variables. Notably, the double transform often provides the only analytically tractable starting point for the study of processes with correlated increments or path constraints. We extend the Tauberian approach for precise large deviations of stochastic processes belonging to the domain of attraction of spectrally positive stable laws, previously developed for single-variable Laplace--Stieltjes transforms [9], to the bivariate setting. This methodology provides a direct route to asymptotic behaviour that is otherwise difficult to characterize using single-transform techniques. As illustrative examples, we derive precise large deviations for random sums with increments correlated to the stopping time and for path-dependent observables of random walks constrained to remain positive.

</details>


### [22] [A random walk approach to high-dimensional critical phenomena](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21438)
*Hugo Duminil-Copin,Aman Markar,Romain Panis,Gordon Slade*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个“黑箱”（black box）方法，在给定少数假设的条件下，统一证明$\mathbb Z^d$（$d>2$）上若干统计力学模型的两点函数在近临界（near-critical）区域表现出平均场（mean-field）行为，其衰减形式为$|x|^{-d-2-\varepsilon}\exp[-c|x|/ξ]$（$\varepsilon>0$）。证明基于随机游走（random walk）技术，适用于自避行走、逾渗、自旋模型（Ising、XY、$|\varphi|^4$）以及格子树等模型，所有模型均在其上临界维度（upper critical dimensions）之上。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法对各类统计力学模型在近临界区域的临界行为缺乏统一、简洁的证明框架。本文旨在通过一个通用的“黑箱”论证，将不同模型的近临界衰减行为归结为少数可验证假设，从而提供一个统一且简化概率证明。

Method: 作者建立了一个“黑箱”证明框架，该框架仅依赖一组短列表假设，即可推导出函数（两点函数）在近临界区域的衰减形式。证明核心基于随机游走技术，通过概率方法统一处理多个模型。

Result: 对于$\mathbb Z^d$（$d>2$）上满足假设的函数族，严格证明了两点函数在亚临界（subcritical）和临界（critical）区域具有形式为$|x|^{-d-2-\varepsilon}\exp[-c|x|/ξ]$（$\varepsilon>0$）的衰减。该结果适用于自避行走、逾渗、Ising、XY、$|\varphi|^4$自旋模型及格子树等模型，均在其上临界维度之上。

Conclusion: 本文提供了一个新的、统一的、概率性的且相对简单的平均场近临界行为证明方法。该“黑箱”框架显著简化了多个重要统计力学模型临界行为的分析，并使后续研究者只需验证假设即可应用该结果。

Abstract: We present a "black box" proof of mean-field near-critical behaviour for a family of functions on $\mathbb Z^d$ (${d>2}$) satisfying a short list of assumptions. The functions represent two-point functions of a lattice statistical mechanical model in the subcritical or critical regimes, and are proved to have decay of the form $|x|^{-d-2-\varepsilon}\exp[-c|x|/ξ]$, for any $\varepsilon>0$. The black box applies to several models for which commonplace methods can be used to verify the assumptions. Applications include models of self-avoiding walk, percolation, spins (Ising, XY, $|\varphi|^4$), and lattice trees, all above their upper critical dimensions. The proof is based on random walk techniques, and provides a new, unified, probabilistic, and relatively simple proof of mean-field near-critical behaviour.

</details>

### [23] [Properties of the skyrmion crystal SkX-2 in the Heisenberg triangular lattice with scalar chirality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21010)
*H. Bocquet,C. J. Ganahl,M. Scheurer,P. M. Derlet,A. M. Läuchli*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文发现一种每个原胞携带两个拓扑荷（topological charges）且倒易空间中铁磁点处无磁化的斯格明子晶体（SkX-2），可在三角格子上带有标量手性（scalar chirality）的海森堡模型（Heisenberg model）所实现的SO(3)对称短程相互作用模型中自然稳定存在。通过数值计算和理论分析描述了从铁磁基态到SkX-2的相变过程及拓扑荷密度的演化。SkX-2在有限温度下同时表现出与平移对称性破缺相关的一级相变以及到浮动固体（floating solid）的连续相变。此外，反铁磁相互作用支持的正四面体相（tetrahedral phase）在有限温度下承载Z₂涡旋（ℤ₂-vortices），预示存在额外的涡旋拓扑相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 斯格米子晶体（skyrmion crystals）最初主要在有磁场且具有非中心对称相互作用（non-centrosymmetric interactions）的材料中发现。近年来，研究者开始探索在无磁场条件下，在巡游磁体（itinerant magnets）中斯格米子晶体的稳定性。本研究旨在寻找一种无需外磁场即可自然稳定的新类型斯格米子晶体结构。

Method: 采用三角格子（triangular lattice）上的海森堡模型（Heisenberg model），引入标量手性（scalar chirality）相互作用，构建了一个具有SO(3)对称性和短程相互作用的模型。通过数值计算与理论分析相结合，定量描述从铁磁基态到SkX-2的相变过程以及拓扑荷密度（topological charge density）的演化。

Result: 发现一种带有两个拓扑荷（topological charges）且铁磁点无磁化的斯格米子晶体SkX-2在模型中自然稳定存在。该结构在有限温度下同时存在一级相变（与平移对称性破缺相关）和到浮动固体（floating solid）的连续相变，相变类型由模型参数控制的电荷密度决定。反铁磁相互作用支持的正四面体相（tetrahedral phase）在有限温度下承载Z₂涡旋（ℤ₂-vortices）。

Conclusion: 在无外加磁场条件下，SO(3)对称的短程相互作用模型可自然稳定一种新型双拓扑荷斯格米子晶体SkX-2。该结构展现出丰富的相变行为，包括一级和连续相变。正四面体相中Z₂涡旋的存在暗示了额外的涡旋拓扑相变（vortex topological transition），这些发现拓展了对无磁场条件下斯格米子晶体稳定性和拓扑相变行为的理解。

Abstract: Skyrmion crystals have been primarily discovered under a magnetic field for materials with non-centrosymmetric interactions. More recent developments have investigated the stability of skyrmion crystals in itinerant magnets without magnetic field. In this study, we find that a type of skyrmion crystal with two topological charges per unit cell and no magnetization at the ferromagnetic point in reciprocal space, SkX-2, is naturally stabilized in an $SO(3)$-symmetric model with short-range interactions realized by the Heisenberg model on the triangular lattice with scalar chirality. We complement our numerical results with a theoretical analysis that quantitatively describes the transition from the ferromagnetic ground state to the SkX-2 and the evolution of the topological charge density. Despite the constraints given by the Mermin-Wagner theorem at finite temperature, the SkX-2 exhibits both a first-order phase transition associated with translation symmetry breaking and a continuous transition to a floating solid, depending on the charge density controlled by the model parameters. Finally, the tetrahedral phase supported by an antiferromagnetic interaction in our model is found to host $\mathbb{Z}_2$-vortices at finite temperature, suggesting the existence of an additional vortex topological transition.

### [24] [Observation of a tripartite quantum phase for coexisting extended, localized, and critical states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21441)
*Zhongshu Hu,Yajing Guo,Yu-Dong Wei,Bing-Chen Yao,Zhentian Qian,Xin-Chi Zhou,Bao-Zong Wang,Jianing Yang,Xuzong Chen,Shengjie Jin,Xiong-Jun Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本实验在准周期驱动的轨道光学晶格（orbital optical lattice）中，利用超冷原子实现了扩展态、局域态和临界态三种量子态共存的“三分相”（tripartite phase），并通过两阶段协议精确制备与检测，揭示了其普适输运性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 实验上构建了具有准周期Floquet调制的光学晶格，该调制耦合s轨道和p轨道；基于精确理论预测该体系可容纳三分相。进一步开发了一套两阶段协议（two-stage protocol），用于精确制备和检测三种量子态。

Result: 通过膨胀动力学（expansion dynamics）确定了三种量子态的特征指数（characteristic exponents），展示了它们各自不同的普适输运性质（universal transport properties）。

Conclusion: 本工作标志着利用超冷原子探索非常规临界现象（unconventional critical phenomena）和局域化物理（localization physics）的重要进展。

Abstract: The disordered quantum world hosts three fundamental types of states: extended, localized, and critical, of which the critical states are confined to fine-tuned critical points or mobility edges in randomly disordered systems. The tripartite phase, with all three types of states coexisting over finite spectral windows, represents a hallmark distinction between quasiperiodic and truly random systems in the localization physics. Here, we report the realization of this exotic phase in a quasi-periodically driven orbital optical lattice with ultracold atoms. The optical lattice with a quasiperiodic Floquet modulation coupling s and p orbitals is realized in experiment and shown to host the tripartite phase from exact theory. We develop a two-stage protocol to precisely prepare and detect the three types of quantum states. The characteristic exponents of these states are determined from expansion dynamics, showing their distinct universal transport properties. Our study marks a significant advancement in exploring unconventional critical phenomena and localization physics with ultracold atoms.

### [25] [General method for obtaining the energy minimum of spin Hamiltonians for separable states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03022)
*Géza Tóth,József Pitrik*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种通用方法，用于确定可分离态（separable states）下自旋哈密顿量（spin Hamiltonians）在固定单粒子约化密度矩阵（single-particle reduced density matrices）时的能量最小值。对于不同维数晶格及全连接图上的铁磁伊辛模型（ferromagnetic Ising model），该最小值可通过包含量子Fisher信息（quantum Fisher information）的紧凑解析公式给出；对于自旋1/2的铁磁海森堡链（ferromagnetic Heisenberg chain），则通过Uhlmann-Jozsa保真度（Uhlmann-Jozsa fidelity）表达。这些关系使得能够直接从适当设计的自旋模型基态的相关测量中提取量子Fisher信息和保真度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法难以在固定单粒子约化密度矩阵条件下，系统性地确定可分离态上自旋哈密顿量的能量最小值。本文旨在建立一种通用解析方法，以填补这一空白。

Method: 采用变分方法，在可分离态的限制下，固定单粒子约化密度矩阵，对不同自旋模型（包括伊辛模型和Heisenberg模型）的能量最小值进行解析推导。最小值分别通过量子Fisher信息和Uhlmann-Jozsa保真度表达。

Result: 对于任意维数晶格和全连接图上的铁磁伊辛及类伊辛模型，能量最小值由含量子Fisher信息的紧凑解析公式给出；对于自旋1/2的铁磁Heisenberg链，最小值由Uhlmann-Jozsa保真度表达。此外，这些公式使得从基态相关测量中直接提取量子Fisher信息和保真度成为可能。

Conclusion: 所提出的方法建立了自旋模型能量最小值与量子信息量（量子Fisher信息、保真度）之间的直接联系，提供了一种通过基态关联测量来实验提取这些关键量子信息量的实用途径。

Abstract: We present a general method to determine the energy minimum of spin Hamiltonians over separable states when the single-particle reduced density matrices are fixed. For ferromagnetic Ising and Ising-like models with nearest-neighbor interactions on lattices of any dimension and on a fully connected graph in an external field, this minimum is given by a compact analytic formula involving the quantum Fisher information. For the ferromagnetic Heisenberg chain of spin-1/2 particles, the minimum is expressed via the Uhlmann-Jozsa fidelity. These relations enable the direct extraction of both the quantum Fisher information and the fidelity from correlation measurements on the ground states of suitably engineered spin models.

### [26] [Relations between different definitions of the quantum Wasserstein distance for qubits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03027)
*Géza Tóth,József Pitrik*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明了由 Golse 等人与 De Palma 和 Trevisan 分别定义的两种量子 Wasserstein 距离（quantum Wasserstein distances）在单算符代价函数情形下对量子比特（qubits）等价，且此时自距离（self-distance）等于 Wigner-Yanase 偏斜信息（Wigner-Yanase skew information）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子 Wasserstein 距离是经典最优传输理论在量子力学中的推广，存在多种不同定义方式。明确这些定义之间的等价性关系，有助于统一量子最优传输的理论框架，并揭示其与量子信息论中已有量（如 Wigner-Yanase 偏斜信息）的内在联系。

Method: 通过对 Golse-Mouhot-Paul-Caglioti 定义与 De Palma-Trevisan 定义的量子 Wasserstein 距离进行理论比较，聚焦于代价函数中仅含单个算符（single operator）的特例，并针对量子比特系统进行解析推导与证明。

Result: 在该特例下，两种量子 Wasserstein 距离的定义在量子比特系统中完全一致；进一步地，该距离的自距离恰好等于 Wigner-Yanase 偏斜信息。

Conclusion: 该结果建立了两种量子 Wasserstein 距离之间的等价关系，并揭示了其与 Wigner-Yanase 偏斜信息这一重要量子信息度量之间的直接联系，为量子最优传输理论的应用提供了新见解。

Abstract: The quantum Wasserstein distances defined by Golse, Mouhot, Paul, and Caglioti and by De Palma and Trevisan coincide for qubits when a single operator appears in the cost function. As a consequence, the self-distance equals the Wigner-Yanase skew information in this case.

</details>


### [27] [Entangling Power: A Probe of Symmetry and Integrability in Quantum Many-Body Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20661)
*Ian Low,Pallab Goswami*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究各向异性海森堡自旋链（anisotropic Heisenberg spin chains）的纠缠能力（entangling power），发现两站点模型中对称性越大纠缠能力越弱（SU(2)点最小），有限尺寸XXZ链在SU(2)点和自由费米子点（free-fermion point）出现骤降，但在热力学极限下SU(2)点散射S矩阵纠缠能力为零而自由费米子点达到最大，表明纠缠能力可作为对称性和可积性（integrability）的算符诊断（operator diagnostic）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子酉算符的纠缠能力量化了从纯积态产生纠缠的能力，是量子多体动力学（quantum many-body dynamics）的自然探针；此前在高能散射（high-energy scattering）中已观察到对称性增强点处的纠缠极值现象，但尚未在各向异性自旋链系统中系统研究纠缠能力与对称性及可积性之间的关系。

Method: 计算了各向异性海森堡自旋链的时间平均纠缠能力，涵盖两站点模型和有限尺寸系统，以及在热力学极限（thermodynamic limit）下双磁子散射S矩阵的纠缠能力；将双磁子S矩阵分解为量子逻辑门——Identity门、SWAP门和σ_z⊗σ_z门，并基于此分解计算纠缠能力。

Result: 两站点模型中纠缠能力随对称群增大而单调递减，在SU(2) XXX点达到最小值。有限尺寸XXZ链在SU(2)点Δ=±1和自由费米子点Δ=0处出现尖锐下降，但自由费米子点的下降随系统尺寸增大衰减更慢。热力学极限下，SU(2)点S矩阵退化为Identity门，纠缠能力对所有散射能量为零；而自由费米子点纠缠能力达到最大——与有限尺寸多体行为相反。

Conclusion: 纠缠能力可作为量子模拟中自旋链动力学的对称性和可积性方面的算符诊断工具（operator diagnostic）。

Abstract: The entangling power of a unitary operator quantifies its ability to generate entanglement from product states and provides a natural probe of quantum many-body dynamics. Entanglement extremization at points of enhanced symmetry has previously been observed in high-energy scattering. In this work we compute the time-averaged entangling power of anisotropic Heisenberg spin chains across two-site models and finite-size systems, as well as the entangling power of the two-magnon $S$-matrix in the thermodynamic limit. For two-site models we establish a monotonic hierarchy: the entangling power decreases as the symmetry group grows, reaching its minimum at the $SU(2)$ XXX point. Finite-size XXZ chains exhibit sharp dips at the $SU(2)$ points $Δ=\pm 1$ and the free-fermion point $Δ=0$, with the free-fermion dip decaying much more slowly with system size. In the thermodynamic limit, we decompose the two-magnon $S$-matrix into quantum logic gates -- Identity, SWAP, and $σ_z\otimesσ_z$ -- and show that the entangling power vanishes for all scattering energies at the $SU(2)$ points, where the $S$-matrix reduces to the Identity gate, while the free-fermion point achieves the maximum -- the opposite of the finite-size many-body behavior. The entangling power can serve as an {\em operator} diagnostic for symmetry and selected aspects of integrability in quantum simulations of spin-chain dynamics.

</details>


### [28] [Velocity-Controlled Directional Readout of Single Photons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21206)
*Mohamed Hatifi*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究均匀运动的Glauber探测器对单光子探测的影响，发现运动导致探测器实现的方向敏感POVM，且有限带宽将传播方向转化为无退相干的探测偏差，揭示了运动测量与被动协变性的分离。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统光电探测理论通常假设探测器与光学装置相对静止，但现实中探测器运动可能影响测量结果。作者希望揭示均匀运动如何改变单光子探测的POVM（positive operator-valued measure，正算子值测度），并理解运动对量子测量协变性的影响。

Method: 采用理论分析方法，将Glauber探测器置于均匀运动框架中，研究其对两个反向传播单光子模（counterpropagating single-photon modes）的单次点击POVM。通过多普勒效应（Doppler effect）引入探测器框架中的频率偏移，并考虑有限带宽响应以及Lorentzian（洛伦兹型）响应函数的时间积分效应。

Result: 运动使探测器的POVM从相位敏感（phase-sensitive）转变为方向敏感（direction-sensitive），且转变阈值由品质因子（quality factor）增强。有限时间积分引入多普勒拍（Doppler-beat）可见度损失，导致被动协方差（passive covariance）与测量变化（measurement change）分离。

Conclusion: 探测器运动不可简化为被动坐标系变换，而是实际改变了量子测量本身。该结果对运动中的量子光学实验、相对论量子信息处理及精密测量具有理论意义。

Abstract: Photodetection is usually treated in the frame in which the detector is at rest relative to the optical apparatus. We show that uniform motion of an electric Glauber detector changes the single-click POVM realized on two counterpropagating single-photon modes. Motion Doppler-shifts the alternatives in the detector frame; finite bandwidth then converts propagation direction into a detection bias without decohering the photon. For a Lorentzian response near one Doppler branch, the readout crosses from phase-sensitive to direction-sensitive with a quality-factor-enhanced onset. Finite-time integration adds Doppler-beat visibility loss, separating passive covariance from measurement change.

</details>


### [29] [Sampling Noise and Optimized Measurement Distribution in Imaginary-Time Quantum Dynamics Simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20378)
*Feng Zhang,Niladri Gomes,Joshua Aftergood,Thomas Iadecola,Yong-Xin Yao,Peter P. Orth*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了采样噪声（sampling noise）对变分量子动力学模拟（VQDS）的影响，重点以伊辛自旋模型（Ising spin model）的基态制备为例，比较了不同正则化策略，并提出通过最小化运动方程误差的成本函数来优化测量分配（shot allocation），从而在保持高保真度的同时将总测量成本降低一半以上。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 变分量子动力学模拟（VQDS）在有噪中等规模量子（NISQ）设备上具有重要应用前景，但其实际性能受限于有限电路测量带来的采样噪声。文章旨在系统理解采样噪声对VQDS的影响，并探索缓解噪声、提升计算效率的实用策略。

Method: 采用一维伊辛自旋模型（one-dimensional Ising spin model）作为基准系统，通过虚时演化（imaginary time evolution）进行基态制备。比较了多种正则化策略以稳定运动方程，并开发了一种基于最小化运动方程求解误差的成本函数来分配测量资源的方法。

Result: Tikhonov正则化（Tikhonov regularization）在带噪虚时演化中表现出稳健性；优化后的测量分配策略相比均匀分配能将态保真度（state fidelity）显著提升，并将总测量成本降低一半以上。此外，为所有电路保证足够多的测量次数可获得最佳结果，表明应保留一部分测量资源进行均匀分配。

Conclusion: 研究为在近-term量子硬件上实现测量高效的变分量子动力学模拟与基态制备提供了实用指导原则，强调了正则化与智能测量分配在抑制采样噪声中的关键作用。

Abstract: Variational quantum dynamics simulations (VQDS) provide a promising route to simulate real- and imaginary-time quantum dynamics on noisy intermediate-scale quantum devices using fixed-depth circuits. However, their practical performance is strongly limited by sampling noise arising from a finite number of circuit measurements. In this work, we systematically investigate the impact of sampling noise on VQDS, with a focus on ground-state preparation in one-dimensional Ising spin models using imaginary time evolution. We compare different regularization strategies for stabilizing the equations of motion and show that Tikhonov regularization provides robust performance in noisy imaginary-time evolution. We then benchmark measurement-distribution strategies that allocate shots by minimizing a cost function that characterizes the error in solving the equation of motion. Using noisy circuit simulations, we demonstrate that such optimized shot allocation can significantly improve state fidelity and reduce the total measurement cost by more than a factor of two compared to uniform shot distributions. We observe that the best results are found if a sufficiently large number of measurements is guaranteed for all circuits, suggesting that a finite fraction of shots should be distributed evenly. Our results provide practical guidelines for implementing measurement-efficient variational quantum dynamics and ground-state preparation on near-term quantum hardware.

</details>


### [30] [WSi weak link element with a non-sinusoidal current-phase relation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20652)
*Sarah Garcia Jones,Trevyn F. Q. Larson,Sai Pavan Chitta,Heli Vora,Varun Verma,Sae Woo Nam,José Aumentado,Jens Koch,Raymond W. Simmonds,András Gyenis*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文展示了基于非晶高动感材料硅化钨（tungsten silicide）制成的收缩结构（constriction）嵌入三维射频超导量子干涉器（RF-SQUID）中的非线性行为，结果表明该弱连接可表现为具有锯齿状电流-相位关系的约瑟夫森结（Josephson junction）或量子相位滑移（quantum phase slip）元件，并测量了势能局域极小值中亚稳态持续电流态的弛豫时间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非线性是编码非均匀能级间距的量子态、实现相干量子门、读取量子比特以及放大与混合电磁信号的关键要素，因此探索新型非线性超导元件具有重要意义。

Method: 采用非晶高动感材料硅化钨制成收缩结构，并将其嵌入三维射频超导量子干涉器（RF-SQUID）中，通过实验观测其非线性行为，并与理论模型进行对比分析。

Result: 实验结果表明，该弱连接的行为与具有锯齿状电流-相位关系（sawtooth-like current-phase relation）的约瑟夫森结或量子相位滑移元件一致；同时测量了势能局域极小值中亚稳态持续电流态（metastable persistent-current states）的弛豫时间（relaxation times）。

Conclusion: 非晶高动感材料制成的收缩结构可作为一种新型非线性超导元件，其行为可归因于约瑟夫森效应或量子相位滑移，并在量子信息处理中具有潜在应用价值。

Abstract: Nonlinearity is an essential ingredient for encoding quantum states with non-uniform energy spacing, implementing coherent quantum gates, reading out qubits, amplifying, and mixing electromagnetic signals. In this work, we demonstrate the nonlinear behavior of a constriction fabricated from an amorphous, high-kinetic inductance material, tungsten silicide, embedded in a three-dimensional RF-SQUID. We find that the results are consistent with the weak link behaving as a Josephson junction with a sawtooth-like current-phase relation or a quantum phase slip element. Finally, we measure relaxation times of the metastable, persistent-current states trapped in the local minima of the potential.

</details>


### [31] [Entanglement Growth from Structured Initial States in Many-Body Localized Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20656)
*Chen Xu,Pengfei Zhang*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过分析随机场XXZ模型中的Rényi纠缠熵和Wehrl-Rényi熵，揭示了多体局域化系统中纠缠熵增长对初始纠缠的非单调依赖起源于局域积分运动相关的有限磁化与站点间关联的竞争；不同初始态极化方向会导致截然不同的纠缠动力学行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解复杂纠缠结构如何涌现是量子多体物理（quantum many-body physics）的核心问题。Zhang等人的近期工作发现，在多体局域化（many-body localized）系统中，总纠缠熵（entanglement entropy）增长随初始纠缠调谐呈现先增后减的双重行为，但其物理起源尚不明确。本文旨在识别这一现象的物理根源。

Method: 研究在随机场XXZ模型（random-field XXZ model）中进行，通过分析Rényi纠缠熵（Rényi entanglement entropy）和Wehrl-Rényi熵（Wehrl-Rényi entropy）的动力学来刻画多体纠缠；后者用于表征多体纠缠（multipartite entanglement）。初始态设置为沿特定方向极化的乘积态（product state）。

Result: 对于沿$z$方向极化的乘积态，Wehrl-Rényi熵的净增长表现出与初始纠缠类似的非单调依赖：第一个增长区间由与局域积分运动（local integrals of motion）相关的有限磁化（finite magnetization）主导，第二个区间反映的是站点间关联（inter-site correlations）。相比之下，沿$x/y$方向极化的乘积态，纠缠增长呈现单调衰减（monotonic decay）。

Conclusion: 研究结果提供了更精细的图像，揭示了不同的初始态性质如何塑造多体局域化系统中的纠缠动力学（entanglement dynamics）。

Abstract: Understanding how complex entanglement structures emerge is a central problem in quantum many-body physics. Recent work by Zhang et al. has considered structured initial states prepared by evolving a product state under a chaotic Hamiltonian for a finite time before quenching to the target Hamiltonian. In this setup, total entanglement entropy growth in many-body localized systems exhibits two distinct regimes, first increasing and then decreasing as the initial entanglement is tuned. In this work, we identify the physical origin of this behavior by analyzing the dynamics of both the Rényi entanglement entropy and the Wehrl-Rényi entropy in the random-field XXZ model, the latter of which characterizes multipartite entanglement. We show that a similar non-monotonic dependence on the initial entanglement also appears in the net growth of the Wehrl-Rényi entropy for product states polarized along the $z$-direction. The first regime is governed by a finite magnetization associated with local integrals of motion, while the second reflects inter-site correlations. In contrast, for product states in the $x/y$-direction, the entanglement growth exhibits a monotonic decay. Our results provide a more fine-grained picture of how distinct initial-state properties shape entanglement dynamics in many-body localized systems.

</details>

*Cameron Jones,Jonathan Y. Huang,Santiago Serrano,MengKe Feng,Gerardo A. Paz-Silva,Tuomo Tanttu,Paul Steinacker,Fay E. Hudson,Wee Han Lim,Nikolay V. Abrosimov,Hans-Joachim Pohl,Michael L. W. Thewalt,Andrew S. Dzurak,Andre Saraiva,Arne Laucht,Chih Hwan Yang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种两单元、四量子比特的SiMOS处理器，具备通用可控性和全并行的状态初始化与读出能力。采用全对称动态解耦门序列（fully symmetric dynamically decoupled gate sequence）来生成纠缠态，以延长纠缠寿命。

Result: 成功生成了最大纠缠的三量子比特态，包括Greenberger-Horne-Zeilinger (GHZ)态，并通过违反经典Mermin见证界认证了多体纠缠。纠缠寿命超出了T2*，受到T2^Hahn的限制。

Conclusion: 这些成果为更大规模SiMOS处理器的可扩展运行以及在处理器中实现高纯度、长寿命的多量子比特纠缠态铺平了道路。

Abstract: Spin qubits in silicon-MOS (SiMOS) quantum dots have recently demonstrated compatibility with existing industry standard CMOS fabrication techniques. These devices have routinely achieved single- and two-qubit gate fidelities above 99% and demonstrated highly entangled two-qubit Bell states in isolated double quantum dot (DQD) unit cells, however coupling between unit cells has remained challenging. In this work, we present a two unit cell, four-qubit SiMOS processor with universal controllability and fully parallelised state initialisation and readout. We use this processor to generate maximally entangled three-qubit states, including the Greenberger-Horne-Zeilinger (GHZ) state, and certify multipartite entanglement through violation of the classical Mermin-witness bound. By using a fully symmetric dynamically decoupled gate sequence to create our entangled states, we are able to preserve the lifetime of the entanglement beyond $T_2^*$, to a time limited instead by $T_2^\textrm{Hahn}$. These demonstrations pave a road to the scalable operation of larger SiMOS processors, and achieving high purity, long-lived multi-qubit entangled states in them.

### [33] [Symmetry-Protected Fast Relaxation and the Strong Quantum Mpemba Effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20930)
*Zijun Wei,Mingdi Xu,Yefeng Song,Yangqian Yan,Lei Pan*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文揭示了一个对称性选择的刘维尔机制（symmetry-selective Liouvillian mechanism），在存在退相噪声的长程XXZ自旋链中保护一个孤立的快衰变通道；在SU(2)对称点上，高度对称的初态与指数衰减率为λ=-2的精确刘维尔本征模（Liouvillian eigenmode）耦合，产生与系统大小和相互作用范围无关的普适指数弛豫；对称性破缺会恢复与慢刘维尔模的重叠并显著抑制弛豫动力学，从而自然导致强量子姆潘巴效应（quantum Mpemba effect）——远离稳态的状态反而比更热的状态弛豫更快。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解对称性如何约束开放量子多体系统中的耗散弛豫，是非平衡物理学中的一个核心挑战。作者旨在揭示对称性在控制弛豫动力学中的具体机制，并探索其与非平衡现象（如量子姆潘巴效应）之间的联系。

Method: 作者在长程XXZ自旋链中引入退相噪声，构建开放量子系统的刘维尔超算符（Liouvillian superoperator）框架，通过分析刘维尔本征模（Liouvillian eigenmode）及其与系统对称性的关系来研究弛豫动力学。

Result: 在SU(2)对称点上，高度对称的初态仅耦合到一个精确的刘维尔本征模，其衰减速率为λ=-2，产生与系统尺寸和相互作用范围无关的普适指数弛豫。对称性破缺会引入与慢刘维尔模的耦合，显著抑制弛豫。这一对称滤波的模可及性（symmetry-filtered mode accessibility）自然导致强量子姆潘巴效应，即远离稳态的状态比更接近稳态的热态弛豫更快。

Conclusion: 研究确立了对称性保护的快弛豫（symmetry-protected fast relaxation）作为一种控制开放量子系统非平衡路径的机制，为设计和调控非平衡动力学提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: Understanding how symmetry constrains dissipative relaxation in open quantum many-body systems remains a central challenge in nonequilibrium physics. Here we uncover a symmetry-selective Liouvillian mechanism that protects an isolated fast-decay channel in a long-range XXZ spin chain subject to dephasing noise. At the \(SU(2)\)-symmetric point, highly symmetric initial states couple exclusively to an exact Liouvillian eigenmode with decay rate \(λ=-2\), producing universal exponential relaxation independent of system size and interaction range. Breaking the symmetry restores overlap with slow Liouvillian modes and substantially suppresses the relaxation dynamics. This symmetry-filtered mode accessibility naturally gives rise to a strong quantum Mpemba effect, where a state farther from the steady state relaxes anomalously faster than closer thermal states. Our results establish symmetry-protected fast relaxation as a mechanism for controlling nonequilibrium pathways in open quantum systems.

</details>


### [34] [Towards transistor-based quantum computing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21045)
*Y. -D. Liu,X. Xu,Q. -R. Wang,D. -S. Wang*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本论文提出并深入研究了一种基于量子晶体管（telesistors）的通用量子计算架构，该晶体管利用对称保护拓扑序（symmetry-protected topological order）的基态实现，无需主动纠错即可提供高保真度的克利福德门（Clifford gates），并可通过常规容错编码（fault-tolerant encoding）扩展为通用量子计算。该架构在模块化、集成度和程序存储方面优于传统量子比特电路，且有望在近期实验实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量子计算架构依赖主动纠错（active error correction）来实现容错，开销较大。本研究旨在探索一种基于拓扑物理保护的低开销方案，以简化容错量子计算的实现。

Method: 提出基于量子晶体管的“telesistors”架构，利用对称保护拓扑序（symmetry-protected topological order）的基态作为信息载体，依赖弦序参量（string order parameters）量化物理保护，并结合传统稳定子码（stabilizer codes）实现通用量子计算。

Result: 该架构无需主动纠错即可实现高保真度克利福德门（Clifford gates），在模块化、集成度和程序存储方面比基于量子比特（qubit）的电路更具优势，且与现有架构存在丰富联系。

Conclusion: 研究表明，该基于telesistors的量子计算架构在近期现有技术条件下具有可行性，为低开销通用量子计算提供了一条有前景的路径。

Abstract: In this work, we propose and study in depth a universal quantum computing architecture based on a quantum construction of transistors. Our teleportation-based quantum transistors, called ``telesistors'', are ground states of systems with symmetry-protected topological order, hence suppress certain noises and provide high-fidelity Clifford gates without the need for active error correction. This physical protection, quantified by the string order parameters, serves as a low-overhead foundation upon which conventional fault-tolerant encoding (e.g., with stabilizer codes) can be built to achieve universal quantum computation. This architecture shows rich connections with current known architectures, and some desirable merits especially compared with the qubit-based circuits regarding modularity, integration, and program storage. Our study shows that it is plausible to realize it with current technology in the near future.

</details>

### [35] [Polynomial diagrams for microstructure modelling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20816)
*David P. Bourne,Maciej Buze,Thomas Gallouët,Quentin Mérigot*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文提出了多项式图（polynomial diagrams）框架，是幂图（power diagrams）和各向异性幂图（anisotropic power diagrams）的推广，允许单元边界为指定次数的代数曲线。通过线性参数化最小化图（linear parametrised minimisation diagrams）重新表述幂图，并开发了基于GPU加速的拟合算法，应用于钢的电子背散射衍射图像分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有幂图（PDs）和各向异性幂图（APDs）的单元边界仅限于线性或二次曲面，无法描述更复杂的代数曲线边界。本文旨在构建一个更一般的图框架——多项式图（polynomial diagrams），使单元之间的边界可以是指定次数的代数曲线，从而提升对复杂空间结构的表征能力。

Method: 首先将幂图和各向异性幂图重新表述为线性参数化最小化图（linear parametrised minimisation diagrams）的一阶和二阶特例，以此自然导出多项式图框架。随后开发了基于GPU加速的拟合框架，利用勒让德多项式（Legendre polynomials）并通过最大化正则化的凹目标函数（concave objective function）来拟合图像数据，该目标函数改编自经典逻辑回归（logistic regression）文献。此外，提供了优化算法的自包含分析，包括尺度（scale）和规范（gauge）不变性的识别，以及正则化参数趋于零时的极限目标函数分析。

Result: 成功将所提出的算法应用于钢的电子背散射衍射（electron backscatter diffraction）图像，拟合了多项式图。

Conclusion: 多项式图作为幂图和各向异性幂图的高阶推广，能够描述更复杂的代数曲线边界。所提出的GPU加速拟合框架结合正则化逻辑回归目标函数，可有效用于图像数据分析（如材料科学的电子背散射衍射图像）。

Abstract: We formulate a framework of polynomial diagrams, which are a generalisation of power diagrams (PDs) and anisotropic power diagrams (APDs) allowing for boundaries between cells to be algebraic curves of a prescribed degree. We show that they arise naturally from rephrasing PDs (APDs) as first-degree (second-degree) instances of linear parametrised minimisation diagrams. We also develop an efficient GPU-accelerated framework for fitting polynomial diagrams to image data using Legendre polynomials and by maximising a regularised concave objective function adapted from classical logistic regression literature. A largely self-contained analysis of the optimisation algorithm is also provided, including identification of scale and gauge invariances and the limiting objective function as the regularisation parameter vanishes. We apply the algorithm to fit polynomial diagrams to electron backscatter diffraction images of steel.

</details>

### [36] [Topology sums, sectorwise holography, and horizon normalcy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20294)
*Naman Kumar*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了“信息全息性”（holography of information, HoI）原理在允许拓扑和与婴儿宇宙（baby universe）及α-扇区（α-sector）下的条件性修正。如果婴儿宇宙希尔伯特空间（ℋ_BU）非平凡（如在Marolf–Maxfield形式或JT引力中），HoI需被细化为α-扇区内的完备性陈述，且在此情形下，基于HoI的防火墙缺失结论依赖于全局扇区数据，与局部半经典几何决定地平线正常性的协变期望产生张力；若ℋ_BU在一致理论中坍缩为一维，则该阻碍消失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: HoI原理声称引力可在渐进可观测量中冗余编码信息，但其标准动机依赖于半经典引力约束与哈密顿量的边界性。作者希望检验当半经典路径积分推理允许拓扑和（topology sums）生成婴儿宇宙或α-扇区数据时，HoI是否仍然成立，以及其与AMPS分解与平滑视界（smooth horizon）的关系。

Method: 采用半经典路径积分推理（semiclassical path-integral reasoning），引入拓扑和与会生成婴儿宇宙或α-扇区数据的机制。通过条件性分析（conditional analysis）考察ℋ_BU的维度（如McNamara–Vafa的婴儿宇宙假说要求dim ℋ_BU=1 in d>3），并利用Bell对诊断（Bell-pair diagnostic）检验扇区无关的平滑内部重构条件。

Result: 若ℋ_BU非平凡（如Marolf–Maxfield形式或JT引力中的系综类例子），HoI需被细化为α-扇区内的陈述（α-sectorwise statement）：在固定α-扇区内，HoI可能阻碍AMPS因子化并允许平滑视界；在无条件拓扑求和态中，扇区无关的阻碍则非自动成立。Bell对诊断表明，扇区无关的平滑内部需要对齐的内部重构或访问扇区标号（sector label）。

Conclusion: 基于HoI的防火墙缺失（firewall absence）变得依赖于全局扇区数据，这与Bousso强调的局域半经典几何应决定地平线正常性的协变期望产生张力。若精确理论将ℋ_BU坍缩为一维，则此处讨论的阻碍消失。

Abstract: The ``holography of information'' (HoI) principle argues that gravity can encode information redundantly in asymptotic observables. Although HoI is ultimately a nonperturbative claim, its standard motivation uses semiclassical gravitational constraints, the boundary nature of the Hamiltonian, and vacuum-sector cyclicity. We ask what happens when the same semiclassical path-integral reasoning allows topology sums that generate baby-universe or $α$-sector data. Our analysis is conditional: such sectors need not survive in every unitary completion, and the Baby Universe Hypothesis of McNamara and Vafa instead suggests $\dim\mathcal H_{\rm BU}=1$ in consistent $d>3$ quantum gravity. If $\mathcal H_{\rm BU}$ is nontrivial, as in the Marolf--Maxfield formulation and in ensemble-like examples such as JT gravity, then HoI is naturally refined to an $α$-sectorwise statement, $\overline{\mathcal A_\infty^{(α)}|0_α\rangle}=\mathcal H_α$, rather than completeness on the full topology-summed Hilbert space. In a fixed $α$-sector, HoI may obstruct AMPS factorization and allow a smooth horizon; in an unconditioned topology-summed state, the sector-independent obstruction is not automatic. A Bell-pair diagnostic shows that a sector-independent smooth interior requires aligned interior reconstructions, or access to the sector label. Thus the HoI-based absence of firewalls becomes conditional on global sector data, in tension with the generally covariant expectation emphasized by Bousso that horizon normalcy should be determined by local semiclassical geometry. If the exact theory collapses $\mathcal H_{\rm BU}$ to one dimension, the obstruction discussed here is absent.

</details>

Method: 利用散射过程的高能领头行为不依赖于荷（charge）的普适性假设（即等效原理（equivalence principle）），从树级引力散射分析出发，推导出单粒子态必须填满从单一种子荷构造出的所有不可约表示。

Result: 发现新推导出的单粒子态在散射中表现出民主贡献（democratic contribution），即所有态具有相等的相互作用强度（interaction strength）。
