Abstract: We prove a version of the completeness hypothesis that follows from the coexistence of symmetry and gravity: tree-level gravitational scattering mandates single-particle states in all possible irreducible representations of the symmetry group constructible from a single seed charge. Our main assumption is that the leading high-energy behavior of scattering is universal irrespective of charge, thus satisfying the equivalence principle. Curiously, we discover that these newly-deduced states contribute democratically - that is, with equal interaction strengths - to scattering.

### [38] [Poles-zeros duality in semi-holographic Mott insulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20321)
*Thomas Kögel,Alessio Caddeo,Amelie Pitters,Francesca Paoletti,Lorenzo Crippa,Giorgio Sangiovanni,René Meyer,Johanna Erdmenger*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种半全息（semi-holographic）方法来描述莫特绝缘体（Mott insulator），通过将基本费米子与大N强相互作用区耦合，在格林函数（Green's function）中实现了极点-零点对偶（poles-zeros duality），并以此表征了半全息金属相和莫特绝缘相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受强关联凝聚态系统中进入莫特绝缘相时格林函数所呈现的极点-零点对偶启发，旨在发展一种统一的理论框架来解释莫特绝缘体的形成机制。

Method: 提出半全息方法，将基本费米子（fundamental fermion）与一个大N强相互作用区耦合；该耦合等效于基本费米子与强关联费米子复合体的杂化（hybridization），在全息框架下复合费米子的格林函数自然呈现极点-零点对偶。

Result: 计算了基本费米子的谱函数（spectral function），并据此表征了半全息金属相和莫特绝缘相。零点的物理起源被解释为自能（self-energy）极点所对应的全息强相互作用区的集体多体激发。

Conclusion: 为零点提供了新的物理解释，并通过强耦合区中标准量子化（standard quantization）与替代量子化（alternative quantization）之间的选择自由，建立了关于极点-零点对偶的一个清晰图像。

Abstract: Inspired by the poles-zeros duality of Green's functions that appears in transitions into Mott-insulating phases in strongly correlated condensed matter systems, we propose a semi-holographic approach to Mott insulators. In this model, a fundamental fermion is coupled to a large-$N$, strongly interacting sector that generates a self-energy for the fundamental fermion's Green's function. This coupling amounts to a hybridization of the fundamental fermion with a strongly correlated fermionic composite. Within the holographic framework, at large $N$, the Green's function of the composite fermion naturally exhibits a poles-zeros duality. Zeros of the Green's function are caused by the poles of the self-energy that correspond to collective many-body excitations of the holographic strongly interacting sector. We calculate the spectral function of the fundamental fermion, from which we characterize the semi-holographic metallic and the Mott-insulating phases. In addition to the new physical interpretation of the zeros, our analysis yields a well-defined picture of the poles-zeros duality in terms of the freedom to choose between standard and alternative quantization in the strongly coupled sector.

</details>


### [39] [Closed String Field Theory in 25.99 Dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20324)
*Ahmadain Amr,Frenkel Alexander,Yin Xi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文重新审视并改进了Zwiebach关于非临界背景下闭弦场论（closed string field theory, CSFT）的表述，限制在属零（genus zero）情形。论文构造了经典BV作用量所需的混合模空间（mixed moduli spaces），证明了其存在性，并将Sen-Zwiebach背景独立性论证扩展至共形轨迹（conformal locus）外的一阶偏离。最后将该形式应用于非临界性的最弱偏差——非零中心荷的世界面共形场论（worldsheet CFT），包括D=26-ε维平坦空间和玻色弦理论中的线性胀子（linear dilaton）轮廓。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有闭弦场论主要在临界背景（critical backgrounds）下建立，其核心结构（如BRST不变性）依赖于世界面共形场论的中心荷为零的条件。为了将弦场论推广至非临界背景（non-critical backgrounds），需要回到并修正Zwiebach此前针对该问题的表述，并严格化其中的几何与代数结构。

Method: 聚焦于属零（genus zero）情形，利用一个特殊弦态F编码世界面BRST不变性的破缺，并引入依赖于度量的下降算子B（descent operator）以适应Weyl标架（Weyl frame）。通过构造混合模空间（mixed moduli spaces）来支撑经典Batalin-Vilkovisky（BV）作用量，并将Sen-Zwiebach背景独立性论证推广至共形轨迹（conformal locus）外的一阶邻域。

Result: 成功构造了经典BV作用量所需的混合模空间并证明了其存在性；将背景独立性论证扩展至共形轨迹外的一阶偏离。在应用层面，针对D=26-ε维平坦空间和线性胀子轮廓这两种非临界背景，构建了仅依赖于一个D维空间坐标的简化解。

Conclusion: 该工作为非临界背景下的闭弦场论提供了更严格的形式化基础，为后续研究广义背景下的弦场论（包括非临界弦和含胀子背景）奠定了基础。

Abstract: We return to and refine Zwiebach's formulation of closed string field theory (CSFT) built around non-critical backgrounds [1,2], restricting our attention to genus zero. The structure involves a special string state $F$ that encodes the failure of worldsheet BRST invariance, and a metric-dependent descent operator $\mathcal{B}$ adapted to the Weyl frame. We construct the mixed moduli spaces needed for the classical BV action, prove their existence, and extend the Sen-Zwiebach background independence argument to first order off of the conformal locus. We apply the formalism to the mildest deviation away from criticality - worldsheet CFTs with nonzero central charge: we consider both D=26-$ε$ dimensional flat space and linear dilaton profiles in bosonic string theory, focusing for simplicity on building solutions that depend on only one of the D dimensions.

### [40] [The fate of Reissner--Nordström--de Sitter black holes: nonequilibrium discharge and evaporation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20349)
*Damien A. Easson*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过结合二维伸缩引力模型（two-dimensional dilaton gravity model）与Polyakov反常反作用（Polyakov anomaly backreaction），建立了Reissner-Nordström–de Sitter (RN–dS)黑洞蒸发的半经典描述，推导了质量和电荷的绝热演化方程，并证明在快速放电机制下带电黑洞会迅速退化为中性黑洞沿Schwarzschild–de Sitter通道蒸发至空de Sitter时空。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对RN–dS时空的蒸发过程缺乏基于绝热反作用的半经典解析描述，经典不动点（如lukewarm、extremal等）在半经典框架下的动态角色尚不明确。

Method: 采用球对称约化的二维伸缩引力模型，引入Polyakov反常反作用效应，推导出Killing能流（Killing-energy flux）和电荷演化的封闭方程组，并通过解析分析证明中性分支的单调蒸发性质。

Result: Killing能流表达式为$\mathcal F=(N_{\rm eff}/48π)(κ_b^2-κ_c^2)$；质量演化方程$\dot M=-\mathcal F+Φ_b\dot Q$包含反常热流项和电磁功项。解析证明中性SdS分支始终满足$κ_b>κ_c$，确保单调质量损失。经典lukewarm曲线不是半经典演化不变量，各经典不动点在快速放电条件下均非吸引子。

Conclusion: 在反常诱导能流和快速放电主导的演化通道中，RN–dS黑洞的终态为空de Sitter时空；该结果为广义第二定律单调性和量子极值面/孤岛估计提供了半经典背景。

Abstract: We develop a semiclassical description of Reissner--Nordström--de Sitter (RN--dS) evaporation by combining a spherically reduced two-dimensional dilaton gravity model with Polyakov anomaly backreaction. The framework captures the causal and thermodynamic structure of the static patch and yields closed adiabatic evolution equations for the mass and charge. With an outward-oriented flux convention, the anomaly-induced Killing-energy flux is $\mathcal F=(N_{\rm eff}/48π)(κ_b^2-κ_c^2)$, while the full mass evolution is $\dot M=-\mathcal F+Φ_b\dot Q$, with $Φ_b=Q/r_b$. We prove analytically that along the entire sub-Nariai neutral Schwarzschild--de Sitter branch $κ_b>κ_c$, so neutral black holes lose mass monotonically. Schwinger pair production provides the discharge channel. In the rapid-discharge regime, controlled charged trajectories become effectively neutral on a timescale short compared with the anomaly-driven Hawking mass-loss time and then follow the neutral SdS channel toward empty de Sitter space. The classical lukewarm locus $T_b=T_c$ is only the nullcline of the anomaly-induced heat flux: the electromagnetic work term tilts the full semiclassical vector field away from this curve, so it is not an invariant trajectory. When sufficiently light charged species provide a rapid-discharge channel, the classical cold/extremal, charged Nariai, ultracold, and lukewarm loci are not semiclassical attractors for controlled nondegenerate trajectories. These results give an adiabatically backreacted derivation of the RN--dS evaporation endpoint in the regime controlled by anomaly-induced flux and rapid charge discharge, and provide the semiclassical background for generalized-second-law monotonicity and conservative quantum-extremal-surface/island estimates.

</details>

Abstract: Holographic superfluids/superconductors are one of the most studied systems in the AdS/CFT duality. In the low-energy, in the long-wavelength limit, they should be described by a Ginzburg-Landau theory. For critical dynamics, one expects that they belong to "model F" universality class. We consider a bulk 5-dimensional holographic superfluid/superconductor in the probe limit. For the holographic superconductor, we impose the boundary Maxwell equation to make the boundary Maxwell field dynamical. We identify the dual model F equations where numerical coefficients are obtained exactly.

### [42] [Conformal anomaly in a vector field model with auxiliary scalar field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20427)
*Samuel W. P. Oliveira,Públio Rwany B. R. do Vale,Ilya L. Shapiro*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文探讨了规范矢量场中通过引入辅助标量场（补偿子）来实现共形不变性（conformal invariance）的方法，并分析了该辅助场对共形反常（conformal anomaly）及反常诱导作用量（anomaly-induced action）的影响。结果表明，在取4维极限后，该标量自由度获得独立动力学，并展现出若干有趣性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 共形反常在正则化和重整化（renormalization）方案下存在众所周知的歧义。在维数正则化（dimensional regularization）框架中，一种方案是将理论在非4维维度下构造为共形不变。对于规范矢量场，有多种实现方式，其中引入辅助标量作为补偿子（compensator）的方法既能保持规范对称性（gauge symmetry），又可避免幺正性（unitarity）可能被破坏的问题。作者旨在探索引入该辅助场对反常及反常诱导作用量的具体后果。

Method: 采用维数正则化方法，在 $D \neq 4$ 维度下构造共形不变的规范矢量场理论。通过引入一个辅助标量场作为补偿子来维持共形对称性，并在取 $D \to 4$ 极限后分析该标量自由度的动力学行为及其对共形反常的影响。

Result: 引入的辅助标量场在取4维极限后获得独立的动力学，不再仅仅是一个补偿子。该残余标量（remnant scalar）展现出若干有趣的物理性质。

Conclusion: 引入补偿子标量场是一种在维数正则化框架下构造共形不变规范矢量场理论的可行方案，它保持了规范对称性和幺正性。该辅助场在4维极限下并非冗余，而是成为一个具有独立动力学的额外自由度，可能对反常结构产生重要影响。

Abstract: The conformal anomaly has well-known ambiguities related to the possible schemes of regularization and renormalization. In case of dimensional regularization, one of the options is to formulate the theory as conformal in the dimension $D \neq 4$. For a gauge vector field this can be done in several ways and one of the options is to introduce an auxiliary scalar playing the role of a compensator. The advantage of this approach is that it preserves gauge symmetry and avoids problems with possible violation of unitarity. We explore the consequences of introducing such an auxiliary field for the anomaly and anomaly-induced action. It is shown that the new scalar degree of freedom gains an independent dynamics after taking the $4D$ limit. The remnant scalar, also, demonstrates some interesting properties.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对可积量子场论中缺陷融合的描述尚不完整，尤其是在非拓扑缺陷与缺陷-边界融合的精确函数形式与熵效应方面缺乏系统分析。

Method: 通过缺陷g函数（defect $g$-function）构建精确描述；对拓扑缺陷采用对数相加性与透射因子（transmission factor）的乘法复合；对非拓扑缺陷利用Bethe-Yang方程（Bethe-Yang equations）中的分离依赖相位；以伊辛模型（Ising model）作为具体算例进行验证。

Result: 拓扑缺陷的分离对数g函数具有可加性，融合极限由透射因子的乘法复合控制；非拓扑缺陷的分离依赖相位产生振荡有限尺寸效应，融合后由有效反射和透射振幅描述；在伊辛模型中，非拓扑缺陷融合降低有限局域熵贡献，拓扑缺陷-边界融合则不改变熵。

Conclusion: 缺陷g函数对拓扑与非拓扑缺陷的融合行为提供了统一且精确的刻画；不同融合类型的熵效应差异揭示了缺陷拓扑性与非拓扑性在物理效应上的本质区别。

Abstract: We study exact defect $g$-functions for integrable line defects in two-dimensional integrable quantum field theory and use them to probe defect fusion. We consider three settings: fusion of purely transmitting topological defects, fusion of non-topological defects with reflection and transmission, and fusion of a defect with an integrable boundary. For topological defects, the separated logarithmic $g$-function is additive, and the fusion limit is controlled by the multiplicative composition of transmission factors. For non-topological defects, separation-dependent phases in the Bethe-Yang equations produce oscillatory finite-size effects, while the fused defect is described by effective reflection and transmission amplitudes. In the Ising examples studied here, fusion involving non-topological defects lowers the finite localized contribution to the entropy, whereas topological defect-boundary fusion leaves it unchanged.

Result: 在 h₄ 李代数上获得 34 种不等价的代数 Haantjes 结构；并通过求解可积条件，在 H₄ 李群上获得三个新的可积 sigma 模型。

Abstract: By solving algebraic relations for the conditions of Haantjes structure on a Lie algebra ${\G}$ and by using the corresponding automorphism group we proceed to classify all inequivalent algebraic Haantjes structures on ${\G}$. In this manner, we obtain 34 inequivalent algebraic Haantjes structures on the ${h_{4}}$ Lie algebra. We deform the chiral sigma model on a Lie group by using Haantjes structure on it. Then we try to obtain conditions on this structure such that the deformed sigma model remains to be integrable. *Leon Miyahara,Shono Shibuya*

TL;DR: 本文在超对称模型中，仅利用BPS子空间（BPS subspace）的谱统计，展示了从混沌（$\mathcal{N}=2$ SYK模型）到可积（$\mathcal{N}=2$ "commuting" SYK模型）的平滑过渡，为仅从BPS态诊断混沌-可积性交叉提供了直接示例。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在靠近$\mathcal{N}=2$ SYK（混沌）极限时，谱统计呈现随机矩阵行为（random-matrix behavior）；靠近可积（integrable）极限时，谱统计平滑过渡为泊松统计（Poisson statistics）。

Abstract: We study chaos-integrability transition purely within a BPS subspace of a specific supersymmetric model that interpolates between the chaotic $\mathcal{N}=2$ SYK model and an integrable $\mathcal{N}=2$ "commuting" SYK model. Using the framework of BPS chaos, we analyze the spectrum of an operator projected onto the BPS subspace. We numerically find that its spectral statistics exhibit random-matrix behavior near the SYK limit and smoothly transitions to Poisson statistics near the integrable limit. Our results provide a direct example of a chaos-integrability crossover diagnosed solely from BPS states.

### [46] [Wasserstein Space of Quantum Chaos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20995)
*Koji Hashimoto,Norihiro Tanahashi,Kentaroh Yoshida*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出 Wasserstein 空间的“有效维数（effective dimension）”随量子系统混沌程度增强而降低。通过耦合谐振子系统、Husimi Q-表示、Sinkhorn正则化最优输运和 Gram-谱方法构建嵌入几何，发现指数级 OTOC 增长诱导折叠结构，Wasserstein 距离可捕获 Lyapunov 指数，且 Wasserstein 空间中的分支结构可标识混沌海中的量子疤痕态（quantum scar states）。该方法为量子混沌、量子 scrambing、量子疤痕和 Lyapunov 指数提供新诊断工具，并支持 Wasserstein 空间作为全息涌现空间（emergent holographic space）的猜想。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子混沌（quantum chaos）的定量表征是量子多体物理的核心难题之一。本文旨在利用最优输运（optimal transport）几何来检测量子混沌、量子 scrambling、量子疤痕以及 Lyapunov 指数，并检验 Wasserstein 空间是否可作为全息对偶中的涌现空间。

Method: 研究一个量子耦合谐振子系统，使用 Husimi Q-表示（Husimi Q-representation）描述量子态；应用 Sinkhorn 正则化最优输运（Sinkhorn-regularized optimal transport）计算态间距离；通过 Gram-谱方法（Gram-spectrum method）构建嵌入几何并提取 Wasserstein 空间的有效维数。

Result: 1）Wasserstein 空间的有效维数随着系统混沌程度的增强而降低（chaotic dimensional reduction）；2）指数级 OTOC 增长在 Wasserstein 空间中诱导折叠结构（folding structure）；3）在反谐振子（inverted harmonic oscillator）的分界线（separatrix/scrambling point）处，Wasserstein 距离准确捕获 Lyapunov 指数；4）Wasserstein 空间中的分支结构（branching structure）标识混沌海中的量子疤痕态。

Conclusion: 最优输运方法为量子混沌、量子 scrambling、量子疤痕和 Lyapunov 指数提供了一种新的几何诊断工具。观测到的混沌维数降低（chaotic dimensional reduction）支持最近猜想（arXiv:2604.17649），即通过流形假设（manifold hypothesis），Wasserstein 空间可作为全息中的涌现全息空间（emergent holographic space），因为混沌性是黑色在壳全息中的典型特征。

Abstract: We find that the effective dimension of the Wasserstein space of energy eigenstates decreases as a quantum system becomes more chaotic. To demonstrate this, we study a quantum coupled harmonic oscillator system using Husimi Q-representations, to which Sinkhorn-regularized optimal transport is applied to construct an embedding geometry via the Gram-spectrum method. We also demonstrate that exponential OTOC growth, referred to here as quantum scrambling even in the absence of chaos, induces a folding structure in the emergent Wasserstein space, which may underlie the chaotic reduction of the Wasserstein dimension. At the separatrix (the scrambling point) of the inverted harmonic oscillator, the Wasserstein distance correctly captures the Lyapunov exponent. Furthermore, we discover that a branching structure in the Wasserstein space signals quantum scar states within the chaotic sea of phase space. Our optimal transport approach thus provides a new diagnostic for quantum chaos, quantum scrambling, quantum scars, and quantum Lyapunov exponents. The observed chaotic dimensional reduction also supports the recent conjecture [arXiv:2604.17649] that the Wasserstein space serves as an emergent holographic space through the manifold hypothesis, since chaoticity is a characteristic signature of black holes in holography.

</details>


### [47] [Exact Holographic Kinematics in AdS/CFT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21252)
*Haitang Yang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出全息对偶中存在着一个精确的运动学（kinematic）部分，该部分与全息动力学（holographic dynamics）截然不同。其核心设定是外尔标架（Weyl frame）下开实心环面（open solid torus）上的共形场论（CFT），在无需任何近似（如大N极限、强耦合近似等）的条件下，即可获得精确且有限的体-边界对（bulk-boundary pairs）。其中出现的AdS几何被理解为运动学几何，仅在特殊CFT和适当极限下才提升为动力学的半经典体。标准边界锚定字典条目仅作为奇异极限恢复。作为重要演示，外尔标架两点函数提供了无需复制的纠缠熵定义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有全息对偶（holographic duality）通常依赖大N极限、强耦合和重算子近似等假设，且体边界对应存在紫外截断。本文试图寻找一个精确的、无需这些近似的运动学（kinematic）全息部分，以区分纯粹的几何运动学与完整的动力学全息。

Method: 采用外尔标架（Weyl frame）下的开实心环面（open solid torus）上的共形场论（CFT）作为设定框架。该开实心环面引入内禀尺度，外尔标架使该尺度显现为一个额外的体方向（bulk direction），从而构造精确且有限的体-边界对（bulk-boundary pairs）。

Result: 所得体-边界对是精确且有限的，无需截断、大N极限、强耦合假设或重算子近似。标准边界锚定字典条目仅作为奇异极限（singular limits）恢复。外尔标架两点函数（Weyl-frame two-point functions）提供了一种无需复制技巧（replica trick）的纠缠熵（entanglement entropy）定义。

Conclusion: 全息对偶包含一个独立于动力学的精确运动学部分，该部分中AdS几何是运动学几何而非动力学半经典体。该运动学部分为全息对偶提供了新的理解视角，并允许在不依赖复制技巧的情况下定义纠缠熵。

Abstract: We propose that holography contains an exact kinematic sector distinct from holographic dynamics. The appropriate setting for this sector is a CFT on an open solid torus in the Weyl frame. The open solid torus introduces an intrinsic scale, and the Weyl frame makes this scale manifest as an extra bulk direction. The resulting bulk-boundary pairs are exact and finite: no cutoff, large-$N$ limit, strong-coupling assumption, or heavy-operator approximation is required. The AdS geometry appearing in this sector should be understood as a kinematic geometry; only in special CFTs and appropriate limits is it promoted to a dynamical semiclassical bulk. The standard boundary-anchored dictionary entries are recovered only as singular limits. As a striking demonstration, we show that Weyl-frame two-point functions provide a replica-free definition of entanglement entropy.

</details>


### [48] [Matching $A$ with $F$ in long-range QFTs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21326)
*Lorenzo Benfatto,Omar Zanusso*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了非幺正的长程多标量φ⁴理论的重整化群流（renormalization group flow），证明其在三圈阶（three-loop order）满足梯度结构（gradient structure），并将该结构与共形场论（conformal field theory）中的球面自由能（sphere free-energy）̃F和Zamolodchikov度量（Zamolodchikov metric）CIJ在领头非平凡阶（leading nontrivial order）匹配，从而在微扰论（perturbation theory）框架下为̃F-定理（̃F-theorem）提供了领头阶证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 幺正性（unitarity）通常是证明重整化群流不可逆性定理（如A-定理）的关键要素。本文旨在考察在非幺正（nonunitary）模型中，重整化群流是否仍能保持梯度结构（gradient structure），从而为̃F-定理提供微扰论证据。

Method: 以长程多标量φ⁴理论（long-range multiscalar φ⁴ theory）为研究对象，展开至三圈阶（third loop order）的微扰计算，验证重整化群流的梯度方程∂_I A = G_{IJ}β^J是否成立。并以长程矢量O(N)模型和超立方H_N模型（hypercubic H_N models）为例，将A和G_{IJ}与共形场论中的球面自由能̃F和Zamolodchikov度量C_{IJ}在领头非平凡阶进行匹配。

Result: 长程多标量φ⁴理论的重整化群流在三圈阶满足梯度结构，且A和G_{IJ}能够在领头非平凡阶与̃F和C_{IJ}匹配。这一结果为̃F-定理在领头非平凡阶提供了微扰论证明。

Conclusion: 本文表明非幺正模型中的重整化群流仍可能在微扰论框架内满足梯度结构，为̃F-定理提供了支持。同时指出该结论是否在更高阶微扰论中依然成立，仍需进一步探讨。

Abstract: Unitarity is often a crucial ingredient in establishing theorems -- such as the $A$-theorem -- on the irreversibility of the renormalization group flow. The strongest thesis of this type of theorems would be that there exists a scalar function $A$ and a positive definite metric $G_{IJ}$ in the space of couplings such that the renormalization group flow satisfies a gradient equation, $\partial_I A= G_{IJ}β^J$, in which case $A$ is locally monotonic along the flow. In this paper we consider the long-range multiscalar $φ^4$ theory, which is a nonunitary model that is believed to be conformally invariant at fixed points, and show that its renormalization group flow satisfies the gradient structure up to the third loop order in the coupling. We also show that $A$ and $G_{IJ}$ can be matched to the leading nontrivial order with the sphere free-energy $\tilde{F}$ and Zamolodchikov's metric $C_{IJ}$ of the corresponding conformal theory concentrating on the examples of the long-range vector $O(N)$ and hypercubic $H_N$ models. Our results imply a perturbative proof of the $\tilde{F}$-theorem at the leading nontrivial order. We conclude the paper discussing briefly whether this result should hold to the next orders in perturbation theory.

</details>


### [49] [Causal UV completions of relativistic hydrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21377)
*Robbe Brants*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明，独立的相对论性流体力学有效场论（hydrodynamic effective field theory）在本质上存在非因果性（acausality），必须通过添加瞬态紫外（UV）模式来恢复因果性（causality）；耗散流体力学在光锥（lightcone）的大部分区域呈指数衰减，使得在晚期时间尺度上仍可约化为流体力学描述的因果性理论成为可能。进一步研究了这些因果紫外完备化（causal UV completion）中非流体力学模式（non-hydrodynamic modes）的涌现及其可能受到的约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 相对论性流体力学（relativistic hydrodynamics）作为一种有效场论（EFT），在描述非平衡系统的低能行为方面取得了成功；然而，独立的流体力学EFT是否具备因果性（causality）尚存疑问。本文旨在证明独立的流体力学EFT内在的非因果性，并探索通过引入紫外模式恢复因果性的可能性。

Method: 通过理论证明的方式论证独立流体力学EFT的非因果性；利用耗散流体力学（dissipative hydrodynamics）在大部分光锥（lightcone）区域的指数衰减特性，分析引入瞬态紫外（UV）模式以恢复因果性（causality）的理论可行性。

Result: 独立存在的流体力学有效场论（EFT）内在地具有非因果性（acausal）；耗散流体力学在光锥（lightcone）内的指数衰减为引入紫外（UV）模式、构建因果性描述提供了理论空间。此外，论文还探讨了在这些因果紫外完备化（causal UV completion）中非流体力学模式（non-hydrodynamic modes）的涌现及其可能的约束条件。

Conclusion: 任何独立的流体力学有效场论（hydrodynamic EFT）都需要补充瞬态紫外（UV）模式以恢复因果性（causality）；在晚期时间尺度上，这类因果完备的理论仍可还原为标准的流体力学描述；非流体力学模式（non-hydrodynamic modes）的出现是因果性要求下的必然结果，并可能受限于特定的物理约束。

Abstract: Relativistic hydrodynamics successfully provides an effective field theory description for the low energy regime of many out-of-equilibrium systems. On the other hand, in this paper we proof that any stand-alone hydrodynamic EFT is inherently acausal and therefore requires the addition of transient UV modes in order to restore causality. This is made possible by the exponential decay of dissipative hydrodynamics in a majority of the lightcone, allowing the possibility of a causal description that still reduces to the hydrodynamic one at late timescales. We then investigate the emergence and possible restrictions of the non-hydrodynamic modes in these causal UV completions.

### [50] [Non-invertible Symmetries in Weyl Fermions, and Applications to Fermion-Boundary Scattering Problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19363)
*Pengcheng Wei,Yunqin Zheng*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在二维Weyl费米子理论中构造了一族非可逆拓扑缺陷，揭示了其与有限阿贝尔群规范对偶缺陷及共形边界条件之间的深层联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索二维Weyl费米子理论中非可逆拓扑缺陷（non-invertible topological defects）的构造方法及其与对称性结构的关系。

Method: 利用G-对称共形边界条件（conformal boundary conditions）对n个Dirac费米子进行展开（unfolding），将其转化为n个Weyl费米子理论中的拓扑缺陷D，该缺陷交织两个G-表示（G-representations）。通过有限阿贝尔群（finite Abelian group）Γ的规范（gauging）来描述该缺陷，并给出确定Γ及其作用的显式算法。

Result: 对于G=U(1)^n，缺陷D可解释为与有限阿贝尔群Γ规范相关的对偶缺陷（duality defect）。对于某些非阿贝尔G的特例，该描述仍然适用；但对于G=SU(2)（出现在1-5-7-8-9问题中），证明了D不能由任何有限阿贝尔群的规范实现对偶缺陷。此外，从对偶缺陷视角给出了费米子从共形边界散射的简化推导。

Conclusion: 非可逆拓扑缺陷与有限阿贝尔群规范对偶缺陷之间的对应关系依赖于对称群G的具体结构，并非普遍成立；对偶缺陷视角为共形边界散射问题提供了更简洁的理论框架。

Abstract: We construct a family of non-invertible topological defects in two-dimensional theories of $n$ Weyl fermions. The construction relies on the existence of $G$-symmetric conformal boundary conditions for $n$ Dirac fermions. Upon unfolding, these boundary conditions become topological defects $\mathcal D$ of $n$ Weyl fermions that intertwine the two $G$-representations, and they are generically non-invertible. For $G=U(1)^n$, we show that $\mathcal D$ is a duality defect associated with gauging a finite Abelian group $Γ$, and we give an explicit algorithm for determining $Γ$ and its action on the fermions. We also show that the same finite-Abelian gauging description applies in certain restricted examples with non-Abelian $G$. By contrast, for certain non-Abelian symmetry structures, including the $G=SU(2)$ symmetry appearing in the $1$-$5$-$7$-$8$-$9$ problem, we prove that $\mathcal D$ cannot be realized as a duality defect for gauging any finite Abelian group. Finally, we explain how the duality-defect perspective gives a streamlined derivation of fermion scattering from a conformal boundary.

</details>

### [51] [Rotating Black Holes Surrounded by Massive Vector Fields in Kaluza Klein Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20239)
*Farokhnaz Hosseinifar,Shahin Mamedov,Kuantay Boshkayev,Soroush Zare,Filip Studnicka,Hassan Hassanabadi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了一种由有质量矢量场和标量场表征的旋转卡鲁扎-克莱因黑洞（rotating Kaluza-Klein black hole），分析了其视界结构、热力学相变、拓扑分类、能层几何以及天体物理观测特征（黑体阴影与薄吸积盘），发现额外维度显著改变相变点和阴影大小，但拓扑分类保持不变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高维引力理论中，Kaluza-Klein 黑洞是检验额外维度效应的重要客体。本文旨在通过热力学与观测信号双重路径，建立区分高维引力模型（higher-dimensional gravity models）的框架。

Method: 首先通过识别视界（horizons）并映射允许参数空间以区分黑洞解与裸奇点（naked singularities）；接着借助霍金温度（Hawking temperature）与热容（heat capacity）研究热力学相变（phase transition），并对热力学势（thermodynamic potentials）进行拓扑研究（topological study）；然后分析能层（ergosphere）几何与自旋的关系；最后考察黑洞阴影（black hole shadow）与薄吸积盘（thin accretion disk）特征。

Result: 霍金温度显示存在常规临界点（conventional critical point），离壳广义自由能（off-shell generalized free energy）将系统归类到特定普适拓扑类（universal group）。额外维度的变化会显著移动相变点并改变阴影大小，但系统的本质拓扑类保持稳定。

Conclusion: 该研究为通过热力学与观测信号区分高维引力模型提供了坚实的框架，拓扑类的稳定性可作为区分不同模型的不变特征。

Abstract: In this paper, we introduce a rotating Kaluza-Klein black hole characterized by a massive vector field and a scalar field. We begin by identifying the horizons and mapping the allowed parameter space to differentiate black hole solutions from naked singularities. The thermodynamic analysis shows a phase transition by examining Hawking temperature and heat capacity. We also conduct a topological study of the thermodynamic potentials. The Hawking temperature indicates a conventional critical point, while the off-shell generalized free energy classifies the system into a specific universal group. We further investigate the geometry of the ergosphere and how it relates to the black holes spin. Additionally, we look at astrophysical signs, such as the black hole shadow and the features of the thin accretion disk. Our results indicate that while the extra-dimensional changes significantly shift phase transition points and modify the shadow size, the essential topological class remains stable. This study provides a solid framework for distinguishing higher-dimensional gravity models through both thermodynamic and observational signs.

### [52] [The third wheel: ringdown and lensing of triple systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20320)
*Vitor Cardoso,Giuseppe Ficarra,Jaime Redondo-Yuste,João Sieiro dos Santos*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过全非线性数值相对论模拟，研究了三体系统中存在伴星时黑洞对头碰撞的动力学，发现了环down阶段的 Doppler 与引力红移、透镜放大效应以及第二像出现和共振模激发的迹象，且即使在极端条件下透镜化的引力辐射也不会导致黑洞坍缩。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三体系统（triple systems）在宇宙中普遍存在，为研究非平凡环境中的引力波产生与传播提供了理想试验场，但对其全非线性动力学行为尚缺乏深入理解。

Method: 采用全非线性数值相对论（numerical relativity）模拟，研究存在伴星（companion）情况下黑洞对头碰撞（head-on collisions）的动力学过程。

Result: 在环down（ringdown）阶段观察到多普勒效应（Doppler effect）与引力红移（gravitational redshift）的证据；发现引力波被透镜化（lensing）放大的明确信号；在某些情形下出现第二像（second image）以及共振模激发（resonant mode excitation）的迹象。

Conclusion: 该结果为理解大质量伴星附近的并合过程奠定了基础；即使在极端设置下，透镜化的引力辐射（lensed gravitational radiation）也不会导致黑洞坍缩。

Abstract: Triple systems have progressively been recognized as ubiquitous in our universe and provide a good testing ground for wave generation and propagation in nontrivial environments. We study the dynamics of triple systems in a fully nonlinear setting. In particular, we analyze numerical relativity simulations of head-on collisions of black holes in the presence of a companion. We show evidence for Doppler and gravitational redshift in the ringdown, and clear signs of amplification by lensing. In certain cases, we also show the appearance of a second image, with hints of resonant mode excitation. Our results pave the way for the understanding of mergers in the vicinity of massive companions. Even in extreme setups we do not find collapse to black holes from lensed gravitational radiation.

### [53] [Transfer observables of rotating acoustic black holes from ray tracing: shadow centroid, redshift asymmetry and flux imbalance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20354)
*Faizuddin Ahmed,Ahmad Al-Badawi,Fernando M. Belchior,Edilberto O. Silva*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个旋转排水浴缸时空（rotating draining-bathtub spacetime）中零声学射线（null acoustic rays）的碰撞参数分辨转移框架，通过直接射线-源相交计算而非半解析环映射，获得了阴影质心、宽度、通量不对称性等可观测量的轮廓，并分析了旋转导致的红移倾斜和分支依赖的通量不平衡，识别出微分诊断量（如阴影质心、通量不对称性、红移不对称性等）作为最有效的环流诊断工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有声学黑洞类比系统中，对于旋转排水浴缸时空中的声学射线转移缺乏一个完整的碰撞参数分辨（impact-parameter-resolved）框架，尤其缺少不依赖半解析近似、直接基于射线-源相交的精确计算方案，因此难以系统提取旋转环流（circulation）的干净可观测诊断量。

Method: 构建了分离源无关射线几何与源-探测器模型的转移形式体系（transfer formalism），显式纳入声学红移（acoustic redshift）、转移约定（transfer convention）、发射率（emissivity）、发射体速度场（emitter velocity field）和源到屏幕映射（source-to-screen mapping），通过直接射线-源相交、有限源宽度或扩展盘积分、探测器卷积及收敛性检查获得可观测轮廓。

Result: 几何捕获区间提供了两个干净可观测量：阴影质心（shadow centroid）随环流线性移动，阴影宽度（shadow width）随环流单调增长。旋转产生左-右红移倾斜（left-right redshift tilt）和分支依赖的通量不平衡（branch-dependent flux imbalance），但总通量单独是简并的环流诊断量。最有效的诊断量为微分量：阴影质心、分支积分通量不对称性、峰值不对称性、左-右红移不对称性和全局红移对比度。

Conclusion: 声学阴影的微分诊断量（如质心偏移和不对称性）是旋转流体环流的最优观测探针；同时需考虑转移约定、固有方位角发射率、左-右分割选择、有限分辨率以及色散（dispersion）、黏性（viscosity）和有限深度修正等物理限制对可观测量的影响。

Abstract: We construct an impact-parameter-resolved transfer framework for null acoustic rays in the rotating draining-bathtub spacetime. The formalism separates the source-independent ray geometry from the source and detector model by keeping explicit the acoustic redshift, transfer convention, emissivity, emitter velocity field, and source-to-screen mapping. The geometric capture interval provides two clean observables: a shadow centroid that shifts linearly with circulation and a shadow width that grows monotonically with circulation. Observable profiles are obtained from direct ray-source intersections, finite source width or extended-disk integration, detector convolution, and convergence checks, rather than from an approximate semi-analytic ring map. The transfer calculation shows that rotation produces a left-right redshift tilt and a branch-dependent flux imbalance, while the total flux alone remains a degenerate circulation diagnostic. The most useful diagnostics are differential quantities: the shadow centroid, branch-integrated flux asymmetry, peak asymmetry, left-right redshift asymmetry, and global redshift contrast. We also discuss how these observables respond to the transfer convention, intrinsic azimuthal emissivity, the choice of left-right split, finite resolution, and physical limitations such as dispersion, viscosity, and finite-depth corrections.

### [54] [Two asymptotically flat spinning black holes balanced by their self-interacting, synchronised scalar hair](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20374)
*Chen Liang,Carlos Herdeiro,Eugen Radu*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在前期工作（arXiv:2305.15467）中，作者已构建了渐近平直的双旋转黑洞平衡构型，本文进一步探究四次标量自相互作用（quartic scalar self-interactions）对该族解（包括2sBSs、2sBHs和中间态1sBHs）的影响。

Method: 基于广义Bach-Weyl框架构建双旋转玻色星（2sBSs）和双旋转黑洞（2sBHs），并在各组分中心放置视界，引入四次标量自相互作用项进行分析。

Result: (1) 对2sBSs，自相互作用的排斥力在强引力区域驱动ergoregion从单环面（single torus）拓扑转变为双环面（double torus）拓扑。(2) 对1sBHs，增强耦合使解变得“毛发更浓密”（hairier），但视界质量不能增加；自相互作用扩展了解析有效模型的有效适用范围。(3) 对2sBHs，增大耦合重塑解序列的分叉结构（bifurcation structure），且只有吸引性自相互作用（attractive self-interactions）才能使视界携带更大的质量占比。

Conclusion: 四次标量自相互作用对旋转玻色星和黑洞的ergoregion拓扑、毛发特性及分叉结构均有显著影响；排斥性自相互作用不能增加视界质量，而吸引性自相互作用是实现更大视界质量占比的必要条件。

Abstract: Asymptotically flat balanced configurations of two spinning black holes with synchronised scalar hair (2sBHs) are possible (arXiv:2305.15467). These are constructed within a generalized Bach-Weyl framework and arise from two spinning boson stars (2sBSs) by placing a horizon at the center of each component. Here, we investigate the effects of quartic scalar self-interactions on this family of solutions, comprising the 2sBSs, the 2sBHs, and an intermediate configuration--single spinning black hole with quadrupolar scalar hair (1sBHs). For 2sBSs, the additional repulsive force introduced by the self-interactions drives a topological transition of the ergoregion, from a single torus to a double torus, in the strong-gravity regime. For 1sBHs, as the self-interaction coupling strength increases, the solutions become "hairier" but their horizons cannot become heavier; moreover, the self-interactions broaden the regime in which an analytical effective model accurately describes these solutions. For 2sBHs, increasing the coupling reshapes the bifurcation structure of the solution sequences and, as in the 1sBH case, repulsive self-interactions cannot make the horizons heavier; horizons carrying a larger mass fraction are obtained only when attractive self-interactions are considered.

</details>


### [55] [Remarks on electrical Penrose process for magnetized Reissner-Nordström black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20492)
*A. Baez,Nora Breton,I. Cabrera-Munguia*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在电彭罗斯机制（electric Penrose mechanism）框架下分析了磁化Reissner-Nordström黑洞的能量提取。研究发现，外部磁场会诱导轴对称几何结构与能层（ergosphere），使负能态成为可能；磁场作为控制参数，既能决定能层构型，也能调控能量提取效率，文中还给出了决定能量提取开启与抑制的临界磁场解析表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有电彭罗斯过程的研究主要集中于非磁化情形，磁化配置下能量提取的机制尚不清晰，外部磁场对能层结构与提取效率的调控作用缺乏系统分析。

Method: 通过对径向运动转折点处的粒子衰变进行分析，基于时空度规系数（metric coefficients）与电磁势（electromagnetic potential）导出了能量提取效率的一般表达式，并利用该表达式给出了识别能区（ergoregions）的直接判据。

Result: 推导出了决定能量提取开启与抑制的临界磁场（critical magnetic fields）的解析表达式，表明磁场可作为控制参数同时影响能层的构型与能量提取效率。

Conclusion: 该结果将电彭罗斯过程的分析拓展至磁化配置，阐明了外部磁场在增强或抑制带电黑洞能量提取中的具体作用。

Abstract: The energy extraction from a magnetized Reissner-Nordström black hole is analyzed within the framework of the electric Penrose mechanism. The presence of an external magnetic field induces an axisymmetric configuration and an ergosphere (the region where energy extraction is possible) arises, allowing for negative energy states even in an otherwise static spacetime. By analyzing the decay of particles at turning points of the radial motion, we derive the general expression for the efficiency of the process in terms of the metric coefficients and the electromagnetic potential. This formulation provides a direct criterion for identifying the ergoregions and we show that the magnetic field acts as a control parameter that governs both the configuration of the ergosphere and the efficiency of the process. In particular, analytical expressions for the critical magnetic fields that determine the onset and suppression of energy extraction are determined. Our results extend previous analysis of the electric Penrose process for magnetized configurations and clarify the role of the external field in enhancing or inhibiting energy extraction from charged black holes.

### [56] [Electromagnetic duality degeneracy in dynamical black hole mergers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20493)
*José Ferreira,Gabriele Bozzola,Carlos A. R. Herdeiro,Vasileios Paschalidis,Miguel Zilhão*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文通过数值相对论模拟带电黑洞合并，首次在动力学强引力体系中实现了电磁对偶（electromagnetic duality）的完全非线性实现，证明所有对偶构型具有相同的时空动力学，电磁辐射的偏振则按对偶角旋转，从而建立了电磁对偶作为动力学爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦（Einstein-Maxwell）解的一个组织原则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电磁对偶是无源爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦方程组的一种对称性，可将电场与磁场相互旋转同时保持应力-能量张量（stress-energy tensor）不变。此前该对称性尚未在动力学强引力体系中得到完全非线性验证，本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 对带电黑洞双星体系进行数值相对论（numerical relativity）模拟，从带电双星出发，通过对偶旋转生成带dyon电荷及纯磁荷的构型，并在同一数值框架下演化整个连续对偶族（continuous duality family）。

Result: 所有对偶构型表现出完全相同的时空动力学；电磁辐射的偏振（polarization）按对偶角发生旋转，从而揭示了引力观测量在电磁对偶下的简并性（degeneracy）。

Conclusion: 电磁对偶可作为动力学爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦解的一个组织原则（organizing principle），为对偶构型在辐射层面提供了具体的映射关系。

Abstract: Electromagnetic duality is a symmetry of the source-free Einstein-Maxwell equations that rotates electric and magnetic fields while leaving the stress-energy tensor invariant. We present the first fully nonlinear realization of this symmetry in dynamical strong-gravity regimes by performing numerical relativity simulations of charged black hole mergers across a continuous duality family. Starting from electrically charged binaries, we generate dyonic and magnetically charged configurations via duality rotations and evolve them within a common numerical framework. We find that all dual configurations exhibit identical spacetime dynamics, while the emitted electromagnetic radiation is related by a rotation of its polarization equal to the duality angle. Our results demonstrate a degeneracy of gravitational observables under electromagnetic duality and provide a concrete mapping between dual configurations at the level of radiation, establishing electromagnetic duality as an organizing principle for dynamical Einstein-Maxwell solutions.

### [57] [Light Deflection due to Spinoptic Effects in Parametrized and Spherically Symmetric Hairy Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20524)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 研究发现，RZ参数化系数（RZ parametrization coefficients）和毛状黑洞参数（hairy black hole parameter）均在偏折角上留下了清晰的印记，表明这些参数对偏折角具有可观测的影响。

Conclusion: 本文评估了利用RZ参数化模拟毛状正则黑洞的可行性，讨论了该近似的有效性与局限性，为区分不同类型黑洞的引力光学特征提供了理论依据。

Abstract: In the standard geometric optics approximation, null rays propagating in a spherically symmetric black hole background follow planar geodesics. This picture changes, however, when the helicity-dependent effects of light are incorporated into the dynamics. Specifically, the interaction between the helicity of light and the spacetime curvature induces a significant angular deflection out of the geodesic plane. In this paper, we employ the spinoptics formalism to study light deflection due to the helicity-curvature interaction in two spherically symmetric geometries: the Rezzolla--Zhidenko (RZ) parametrized metric, and a hairy regular black hole solution obtained via gravitational decoupling. Our results reveal clear imprints of both the RZ parametrization coefficients and the hairy black hole parameter on the deflection angle. Furthermore, we assess the viability of using the RZ parametrization to mimic the regular hairy black hole, discussing the validity and limitations of such an approximation.

### [58] [Convergence of post-Newtonian for quasi-circular non-precessing comparable mass ratios BBHs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20562)
*Dongze Sun,Béatrice Bonga,Leo C. Stein,Guido Da Re*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过比较后牛顿（PN）能量流与高精度数值相对论（NR）模拟，系统研究了非自旋、准圆形双黑洞系统在早期旋进阶段PN级数的收敛性，发现轨道速度v≲0.45时高阶PN（尤其是6PN）持续改善与NR的一致性，但收敛性在接近最内稳定圆轨道时丧失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 后牛顿（Post-Newtonian, PN）理论是双黑洞早期旋进建模的解析基础，但作为渐近级数（asymptotic series），高阶PN项不一定改善与完整非线性动力学的一致性。此前极端质量比极限下的收敛性已有研究，但对当前观测最相关的等质量系统尚缺乏系统的高阶PN基准检验。

Method: 研究非自旋、准圆形双黑洞系统，通过对比未来零无穷远（future null infinity）处的PN能量流与长期高精度数值相对论（numerical relativity, NR）模拟实现收敛性分析。为保证规范一致性，将两种描述置于同一BMS参考系（BMS frame）中，并通过在早期旋进阶段拟合NR波形来校准内禀PN参数。

Result: 在轨道速度v≲0.45时，高阶PN项持续降低PN–NR能量流差异，（不完整的）6PN项在所考虑阶数中一致性最佳。PN阶数提高带来的改善呈现非单调性，在2.5PN和4PN附近存在局部极值。当v接近~0.5（最内稳定圆轨道附近）时，高阶PN不再改善NR与PN的一致性，表明收敛性丧失。

Conclusion: PN级数的最佳截断阶数（optimal truncation order）无法通过能量流残差的第一个局部最小值确定，这与先前工作建议相悖。这些结果激励继续推进高阶PN计算，同时明确了验证这些计算所需的NR精度要求。

Abstract: Post-Newtonian (PN) theory provides the analytic foundation for modeling the early inspiral of binary black holes. However, as an asymptotic series, successive PN orders do not necessarily improve agreement with the full nonlinear dynamics. While this has been explored in the extreme-mass-ratio limit, comparable-mass systems most relevant to current observations have not been benchmarked as systematically at high PN order. We study the convergence of the PN series for non-spinning and quasi-circular systems by comparing the PN energy flux at future null infinity to a long, high-accuracy numerical relativity (NR) simulation. To enable a gauge-consistent comparison, we place both descriptions in the same BMS frame and calibrate the intrinsic PN parameters by fitting to the NR waveform in the early inspiral. We find that for orbital velocities $v\lesssim0.45$, higher PN orders continue to reduce the PN--NR flux discrepancy, with (incomplete) 6PN providing the best agreement among the orders considered. The improvement with PN order is non-monotonic with local extrema around 2.5PN and 4PN. This implies that the optimal truncation order of the PN series cannot be identified from the first local minimum in the energy flux residuals, contrary to suggestions in earlier work. As $v$ approaches $\sim 0.5$ near the innermost circular orbit, higher PN orders no longer improve the agreement between NR and PN, indicating a loss of convergence. These results motivate continued high-order PN calculations and clarify the NR accuracy needed to validate them.

Abstract: In this article, we investigate the optical, thermodynamic, and scattering properties of a ModMax black hole surrounded by a cloud of strings within the framework of Einstein-bumblebee gravity. We then analyze in detail the thermodynamic properties of this black hole, including the Hawking temperature, entropy, and other relevant thermodynamic quantities, and examine the outcomes. Furthermore, we study the greybody factors (GFs) associated with the emission of various perturbative fields propagating in this black hole background. In particular, we consider spin-0 scalar fields, spin-1 electromagnetic fields, and spin-2 graviton fields, and evaluate the corresponding absorption probabilities and energy emission rates. ### [60] [Post-Newtonian orbital mechanics around a black hole in modified gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20574)
*Ioannis Liodis,Gernot Heissel,Rita Mastroioanni,Jai Grover,Dario Izzo*

TL;DR: 本文基于标量-张量-矢量引力（MOG）框架，数值积分S恒星的post-Newtonian轨道运动方程，分析MOG对轨道根数、观测量的影响，并揭示其与暗物质（dark matter）信号之间的潜在简并性（degeneracy）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Scalar-tensor-vector gravity, also known as modified gravity (MOG), has emerged as an alternative to General Relativity (GR). It aims to explain astrophysical phenomena without invoking dark matter. The S-stars orbiting the supermassive black hole at the Galactic centre provide a unique opportunity to test the predictions of MOG because the orbital measurements are highly precise. We investigate the perturbations in the orbits of S-stars under MOG, focusing on the effects on orbital elements, observables such as right ascension, declination, and radial velocity, and the potential degeneracy with dark matter scenarios. We numerically integrated the first post-Newtonian equations of motion for S-stars within the MOG framework, considering contributions from the space-time geometry and the fifth force. We analysed the time evolution of orbital elements and projected the orbits onto the plane of the sky to assess deviations from GR. Furthermore, we compared the MOG-induced effects with those expected from a dark matter distribution. We found that MOG significantly alters the orbital precession, particularly for higher values of the MOG parameter $α$. For sufficiently large $α$ or long observational baselines, the deviations in the observables can reach amplitudes comparable to current observational precision. Furthermore, we demonstrate that MOG effects can mimic those of a dark matter distribution, particularly in the argument of pericentre, and we reveal an unexplored connection between MOG and GR with electromagnetism. The effects of MOG on stellar orbits are distinct from those predicted by GR and can be tested with precise astrometric and spectroscopic measurements of the S-stars. However, a potential degeneracy with dark matter signatures necessitates careful interpretation of observational data.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在圈量子引力（loop quantum gravity）框架下，将圈量子宇宙学（Loop Quantum Cosmology）中已成熟的路径积分方法推广到球对称真空时空，旨在获得包含逆三重态（inverse triad）修正和完整修正（holonomy corrections）的显式有效模型，从而探索圈量子化对经典黑洞奇点问题的修正效果。

Method: 采用路径积分方法（path integral method）推导球对称真空时空的圈量子修正有效模型；引入表征完整路径长度的量子参数，修正经典哈密顿约束（Hamiltonian constraint）；随后对简化版修正理论的有效动力学进行求解，分析其几何性质。

Result: 得到的半经典理论在量子参数取小值时退化为经典情形。逆三重修正下的有效几何描述了一个内部存在曲率奇点（curvature singularity）的黑洞，但与经典解不同，该奇点不导致零测地线不完备性（null geodesic incompleteness）。对于完整修正，初步论证表明其具有潜在的奇点消解能力。

Conclusion: 圈量子修正可在不消除奇点的情况下改善黑洞时空的测地线完备性，而完整修正可能进一步实现奇点消解，说明圈量子化方法为处理经典引力理论中的奇点问题提供了可行的修正机制。

Abstract: In this work a loop quantum corrected model is obtained for spherically symmetric space-times in the vacuum. This effective model is derived by the use of the path integral method, previously employed in several models of Loop Quantum Cosmology. Our principal aim is to find explicit corrections corresponding to inverse triad and holonomy effects that commonly arise from the loop quantization procedure. These corrections modify the Hamiltonian constraint of the classical theory, adding quantum parameters that represent the length of the holonomies considered during quantization. The semiclassical theory yielded reduces to the classical case when small values of such length are taken to be small. Solutions to the effective dynamics of a simplified version of the complete corrected theory are then found and used to describe an effective geometry with inverse triad corrections. This modified space-time represents a black hole with a curvature singularity in its interior which, contrary to its classical counterpart, does not lead to null geodesic incompleteness. For the case of holonomy corrections, preliminary arguments are given in favor of a potential singularity resolution.

</details>


### [63] [Constraint-satisfying binary boson star initial data via XCFC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20888)

Method: 采用扩展共形平坦条件（eXtended Conformally Flat Condition, XCFC）形式论，对物质变量进行共形重标度（conformal rescaling），并引入辅助矢量场（auxiliary vector field）。利用迭代求解器方法求解与约束相关的二阶椭圆型方程（second-order elliptic equations），以克服解在局部唯一性与收敛性方面的问题。

Result: 针对高斯型分布、拓扑环面构型及等质量玻色星双星（equal-mass boson star binaries）等标量场体系，XCFC迭代求解方法均实现了收敛。对于玻色星双星，该方法生成了严格满足约束的初始数据，显著优于常用的叠加两个孤立玻色星解的构建方式。

Conclusion: XCFC形式论能够为数值相对论模拟提供更可靠的初始数据，特别是在玻色星双星等复杂物质构型场景中，相较于叠加方法具有本质优势。

Abstract: Numerical-relativity simulations with non-trivial matter configurations require initial data that satisfy the Hamiltonian and momentum constraints of the Einstein equations. We construct constraint-satisfying scalar-field initial data using the eXtended Conformally Flat Condition (XCFC) formalism, in which the matter variables are conformally rescaled and an auxiliary vector field is introduced. In doing so, we overcome the issues of local uniqueness and convergence of the solutions that arise in the second-order elliptic equations associated with the constraints. Using an iterative solver method, we demonstrate the convergence of the XCFC approach to a solution for several scalar-field matter systems. Those include Gaussian-like profiles, topological torus configurations, and equal-mass boson star binaries. In particular, for the latter case, it is common to employ the superposition of two isolated boson star solutions in order to build the initial data. We show that our formalism significantly improves upon a superposition approach by generating genuinely constraint-satisfying initial data for boson star binaries.

Method: 采用 $f(Q,T)=\alpha Q+\beta T$ 形式的修正引力理论，通过作用量变分（action variation）导出场方程；选取 $L_m=-T$ 和 $L_m=\rho$ 两类物质拉格朗日密度，结合线性和渐近线性状态方程（equation of state）求解虫洞解。

The field equations, derived via action variation, share a common general structure but are fundamentally dictated by the parameters $α$ and $β$ through the coefficients $A_i$. The energy conditions and physical characteristics of these solutions are shown to be distinct and critically dependent on the selected $L_m$.

### [66] [Thermodynamics of homogeneous Universes: de Sitter, Bonnor-Melvin and static Einstein](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21047)
*G. E. Volovik*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在动态引力场（dynamic gravitational field）从底层物质场（underlying matter fields）涌现的理论中，引力场可被视为物质的一部分。作者希望基于这一视角，构建均匀宇宙的热力学描述，并检验不同物质场构成的宇宙是否具有统一的热力学行为。

Method: 采用引力场从物质场涌现的理论框架，将引力场视为物质的一部分，进而对三类均匀宇宙（de Sitter宇宙、Bonnor-Melvin-Λ宇宙和静态爱因斯坦宇宙）进行热力学构造。

Result: 三类宇宙尽管包含不同类型的物质场（普通物质、磁场、引力场和真空能），却展现出相同的热力学性质。其能量密度（energy density）满足同一方程，该方程包含相应的物质密度以及热力学共轭变量对（thermodynamically conjugate variables）。在普通物质、磁场和引力场均不存在的闵可夫斯基真空（Minkowski vacuum）中，该方法自动导致零宇宙常数（zero cosmological constant）。

Conclusion: 均匀宇宙的热力学性质在多种物质场构成下具有普适性；该涌现框架可自然解释闵可夫斯基真空中宇宙常数为零的结果。

Abstract: In the theories, in which dynamic gravitational field emerges from the underlying matter fields, the gravitational field can be considered as a part of matter. Using this approach, we construct the thermodynamics of the homogeneous Universes -- the de Sitter Universe, the Bonnor-Melvin-$Λ$ Universe and the static Einstein Universe. It is demonstrated that although these three Universes have different types of matter fields (ordinary matter, magnetic field, gravitational field and vacuum energy), they have the same thermodynamic properties. Their energy densities obey the same equation, which contains the corresponding matter densities and the pairs of the thermodynamically conjugate variables. In Minkowski vacuum, where the ordinary matter and magnetic and gravitational fields are absent, this thermodynamic approach automatically leads to zero cosmological constant.

### [67] [Constraints on Kaniadakis Cosmology from Starobinsky Inflation and Primordial Tensor Perturbations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21050)

Conclusion: 广义视界热力学与暴涨宇宙学之间存在直接联系，量子统计修正熵-面积律可以传播为早期宇宙物理中潜在的可观测信号，该模型在现象学上是ΛCDM范式的一致扩展。

Abstract: We investigate a generalized entropic cosmology obtained by applying the gravity-thermodynamics conjecture to the Universe horizon using Kaniadakis statistics, namely a relativistic extension of the standard Boltzmann--Gibbs formalism. The resulting deformation of the horizon entropy naturally modifies the Friedmann dynamics and provides a phenomenologically consistent extension of the $Λ$CDM paradigm. Within this framework, we explore the implications of the modified cosmological dynamics for the physics of the early Universe, focusing in particular on primordial gravitational waves (PGWs) and slow-roll inflation in a Starobinsky-like scenario. We show that the generalized entropic corrections simultaneously affect the evolution of tensor perturbations and the inflationary slow-roll dynamics, inducing characteristic deviations in the PGW spectrum as well as nontrivial corrections to the main inflationary observables. By confronting the theoretical predictions with the latest Planck and BICEP/Keck observations, we derive stringent constraints on the Kaniadakis parameter and assess the observational viability of the model. Our results establish a direct connection between generalized horizon thermodynamics and inflationary cosmology, showing that quantum-statistical modifications of the entropy-area law can propagate into potentially observable signatures in the physics of the early Universe.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在描述两点格林函数的非齐次狄拉克方程（inhomogeneous Dirac equation）中引入了一个特设（ad hoc）源项，旨在模拟反对易关系的修改效应。通过求解该方程得到了稳态解。

Result: 获得的稳态解被解释为事件视界附近费米子的两点格林函数。由于这些格林函数具有稳态（stationary）性质，它们描述了一个位于事件视界附近的费米子凝聚（fermion condensate）。

Conclusion: 修改费米子的正则反对易关系会导致事件视界附近出现费米子凝聚，这可能为黑洞量子性质的研究提供新的视角。

Abstract: Some arguments are considered in favor of the idea that the canonical anticommutation relations for fermions should be modified in curved spacetime near the event horizon of a black hole. Such a modification is expected to lead to a change in the source term of the inhomogeneous Dirac equation describing the two-point Green's function. By introducing an {\it ad hoc} source into the Dirac equation that mimics the modification of these anticommutation relations, stationary solutions are obtained and interpreted as two-point Green's functions of fermions located near the event horizon. ### [69] [Kinematic selection of the viscous stress in relativistic dissipative hydrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21359)
*Zhi-Wei Wang,Samuel L. Braunstein*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文基于拉格朗日运动学（Lagrangian kinematic）构造，在洛伦兹时空（Lorentzian spacetime）上推导出相对论耗散流体力学（relativistic dissipative hydrodynamics）中粘性应力（viscous stress）不依赖于涡度（vorticity）和加速度（acceleration）的标准结构，并证明BDNK框架的非相对论极限在粘性扇区（viscous sector）中普遍给出变形拉普拉斯算子（deformation Laplacian），同时利用运动学应变率（kinematic strain rate）直接推导出Weinberg引力波阻尼公式（gravitational-wave damping formula）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有相对论耗散流体力学的各种标准表述（从Eckart到Israel-Stewart再到BDNK框架）均假设粘性应力依赖于剪切张量（shear tensor）与膨胀标量（expansion scalar），而不依赖于涡度与加速度，但这一结构缺乏从底层运动学出发的系统推导。本文旨在填补这一理论空白。

Method: 在洛伦兹时空上采用拉格朗日运动学构造方法，将空间应变率（spatial strain rate）定义为李拖拽连接矢量（Lie-dragged connecting vectors）空间内积变化率的空间投影，即投影度规（projected metric）的空间投影李导数（spatially projected Lie derivative）。通过分析加速度项在空间投影下的精确相消以及涡度项的对称性消除，导出粘性应力的标准结构。

Result: 加速度项在空间投影下精确消去，涡度项由对称性相消；材料框架无关性（material frame-indifference）对一般的Killing扰动（Killing perturbations）不成立，偏差量正比于加速度，仅在流保持等距（flow-preserving isometries）下恢复。BDNK方程的非相对论极限在粘性扇区中普遍给出变形拉普拉斯算子，其BDNK参数依赖性完全来自热扇区（heat-flux sector）。此外，从扰动FRW时空中的运动学应变率直接导出了Weinberg引力波阻尼公式。

Conclusion: 该工作从拉格朗日运动学出发，为相对论耗散流体力学中粘性应力与涡度、加速度无关的标准假设提供了严格的几何推导，揭示了材料框架无关性在广义相对论框架下的局限与恢复条件，并建立了BDNK框架与非相对论极限以及引力波阻尼公式之间的直接联系。

Abstract: All standard formulations of relativistic dissipative hydrodynamics, from Eckart through Israel-Stewart to the recent BDNK framework, assume that the viscous stress depends on the shear tensor $σ_{αβ}$ and the expansion scalar $θ$ but not on the vorticity $ω_{αβ}$ or the acceleration $a_α$. We derive this structure from a Lagrangian kinematic construction on Lorentzian spacetimes, extending a recent result on Riemannian manifolds. The spatial strain rate, constructed from the rate of change of spatial inner products of Lie-dragged connecting vectors, is the spatially projected Lie derivative of the projected metric $h_{αβ} = g_{αβ} + u_αu_β$. The acceleration terms drop out exactly under spatial projection, and the vorticity cancels by symmetry. We show that material frame-indifference fails for generic Killing perturbations by an amount $δ\mathfrak{h}_{αβ} = +ε(ξ_αa_β+ ξ_βa_α)$ proportional to the acceleration, and is restored only for flow-preserving isometries. We prove that the non-relativistic limit of the BDNK equations gives the deformation Laplacian universally in the viscous sector, with the BDNK parameter dependence identified by Hegade K R, Ripley, and Yunes arising entirely from the thermal (heat-flux) sector. As an application, we derive the Weinberg gravitational-wave damping formula directly from the kinematic strain rate in a perturbed FRW spacetime.

</details>


### [70] [Versal transition scenarios in inflationary cosmology: slow roll, ultra-slow roll, and oscillatory exit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21393)
*Spiros Cotsakis*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文针对标量场宇宙学（scalar-field cosmology）构建了一个面向物理学的持久/转变-多样性（persistence/transition-variety）分析框架，旨在将暴胀动力学（inflationary dynamics）中的慢滚（slow roll）、超慢滚（ultra-slow roll）及振荡后暴胀行为等不同阶段统一理解为持久 regime 与普适过渡 episode 的拼接，并指出这些 regime 转变恰好发生在双曲性丧失（loss of hyperbolicity）之处，因而无法被纯双曲或渐近处理捕捉。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 观测上可行的暴胀模型往往无法被单一渐近阶段所充分描述，因此需要一种能够刻画多个持久 regime 及其之间普适过渡的理论框架，以弥补纯双曲或渐近处理方法在 regime 转变处的盲区。

Method: 采用持久/转变-多样性（persistence/transition-variety）框架，以指数势模型（exponential model）作为参考 regime 图谱（atlas），以有质量势模型（massive case）作为斜率漂移（slope drift）的动力学实现，对 scalar-field 宇宙学中的暴胀历史进行几何化组织和解读。

Result: 慢滚表现为稳健的持久平衡（robust persistent balance），超慢滚表现为非双曲组织集（nonhyperbolic organising set）附近的瓶颈通道（bottleneck passage），振荡后暴胀行为表现为循环性退出扇区（recurrent exit sector）；Regime 转变恰好发生在谱线穿越虚轴（spectrum crosses the imaginary axis）或双曲性丧失的位置。

Conclusion: 该框架显式表明 relevant 的 regime 转变位于双曲性丧失或谱线穿越虚轴之处，这些转变无法被纯双曲或渐近处理所描述，因此该框架为理解暴胀动力学中的非线性 regime 过渡提供了必要的几何语言。

Abstract: We develop a physics-facing version of the persistence/transition-variety framework for scalar-field cosmology, tailored to inflationary dynamics. The guiding idea is that observationally viable inflationary models are often best understood not as single asymptotic phases but as concatenations of persistent regimes separated by universal transition episodes. In this picture, slow roll appears as a robust persistent balance, ultra-slow roll as a bottleneck passage near a nonhyperbolic organising set, and oscillatory post-inflationary behaviour as a recurrent exit sector. Using the exponential model as a reference regime atlas and the massive case as a dynamical realisation of slope drift, we show how such histories may be organised and read geometrically. The resulting framework makes explicit that the relevant regime transitions are organised precisely where hyperbolicity is lost or the spectrum crosses the imaginary axis, and are therefore invisible to a purely hyperbolic or asymptotic treatment.

</details>

Method: 利用全相干自由电子激光脉冲在薄绝缘膜中干涉形成瞬态光栅，通过该瞬态光栅实现相位匹配（phase-matching），从而激发下方双曲超材料中的布洛赫等离激元极化激元模式；同时采用有限元模拟（finite element simulations）验证瞬态光栅在促进相位匹配与模式激发中的作用。

Conclusion: 该研究展示了一条时空激发布洛赫等离激元极化激元模式的新路径，为永久纳米结构光栅提供了一种替代方案，并有望实现光学模式激发的超快控制。

Abstract: Manipulating materials properties with light drives advances in materials science and photonics. Hyperbolic metamaterials are promising candidates as next-generation quantum optical media. They support Bloch plasmon polaritons, which are characterized by potentially infinite wave-vectors and long lifetimes, but cannot be excited through direct light illumination due to momentum mismatch. Here, we experimentally show that a transient grating, formed via interference of fully coherent seeded free-electron laser pulses in a thin insulator film, enables the excitation of Bloch plasmon polaritons in an underlying hyperbolic metamaterial. Finite element simulations confirm the role of the transient grating in facilitating phase-matching and mode excitation. Our findings demonstrate a route to spatiotemporally excite Bloch plasmon polaritons modes, offering an alternative to permanently nanostructured gratings and potentially enabling ultrafast control of optical modes excitation.

### [72] [Probing Lattice Dynamics in Real-Space and Real-Time](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20631)
*Navdeep Rana*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本论文利用高次谐波光谱学（HHS）研究固体中相干晶格振动对阿秒电子响应的影响，观察到石墨烯面内声子模式产生谐波边带，并展示了HHS表征声子模式能量、偏振、相位差及手性的能力；同时，提出了结合非弹性散射技术与理论分析的方法，作为探测实空间与实时晶格动力学的替代方案，具有原子级时空分辨率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 相干晶格振动显著影响固体中的物理与化学过程，但高次谐波光谱学（HHS）在探测相干晶格振动对电子响应影响方面的适用性尚未得到探索。

Method: 利用高次谐波光谱学（HHS）探测固体中的相干晶格动力学对阿秒电子响应的影响；在论文后半部分，采用非弹性散射技术结合理论分析，用于实空间与实时探测相干晶格动力学。

Result: 在石墨烯中，面内声子模式的相干激发导致谐波光谱中出现由激发声子模式频率分隔的边带；HHS能够表征声子模式的能量、偏振、相位差及手性；非弹性散射方法与理论分析的结果与泵浦-探测构型下的时间分辨衍射和成像测量结果具有可比性，并与时间分辨漫射X射线散射实验高度吻合。

Conclusion: HHS提供了一种以亚周期时间分辨率探测固体中声子驱动过程的途径；所提出的非弹性散射方法可作为时间分辨衍射与成像方法的替代方案，用于实现原子级时空分辨率下晶格动力学的探测。

Abstract: The coherent lattice vibrations significantly impact physical and chemical processes in solids, such as heat transfer, displacive phase transitions, and thermal conductivity. Thus, probing lattice dynamics in real-space and real-time is essential for understanding ubiquitous phenomena in solids. High-harmonic spectroscopy (HHS) has emerged as a preferred technique for investigating static and dynamic properties of solids on ultrafast timescales. Yet, despite these accomplishments, the applicability of HHS to probe the influence of coherent lattice vibrations on electronic responses has remained unexplored.
  In this thesis, we explore the impact of coherent lattice dynamics on attosecond electronic responses in solids using HHS. We observe that coherent excitation of the in-plane phonon mode in graphene results in sidebands in the harmonic spectrum, separated by the frequency of the excited phonon mode. Additionally, we demonstrate the capability of HHS to characterize energy, polarization, phase difference, and the "chirality" of phonon modes. This thesis offers an avenue to probe phonon-driven processes in solids with sub-cycle temporal resolution.
  In the later segment, our focus shifts toward probing coherent lattice dynamics in real-space and real-time. We demonstrate that inelastic scattering techniques, combined with theoretical analysis, yield comparable results to those from time-resolved diffraction and imaging measurements within pump-probe configurations. Our findings exhibit excellent agreement with results from a time-resolved diffuse x-ray scattering experiment. Our proposed method serves as an alternative to time-resolved diffraction and imaging methods for probing lattice dynamics in real-space and real-time with atomic-scale spatiotemporal resolution.

### [73] [Spin-polarized lasing in a photonic lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20927)
*A. Herrero Otermin,N. Carlon Zambon,A. Bieganowska,F. Jabeen,L. Viña,C. Antón-Solanas*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文在GaAs/InGaAs半导体微腔制备的二维光子晶格中实现了自旋极化激光，通过偏振、角度和能量的显微光致发光测量，展示了从强耦合区到光子激射的转变，并验证了可控的圆偏振发射。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在扩展光学系统中实现自旋可控相干发射的平台，具体关注光子晶格垂直腔面发射激光器（photonic-lattice VCSELs）的自旋极化激射特性。

Method: 采用GaAs/InGaAs半导体微腔样品制备二维光子晶格，晶格由交错排列的圆角矩形微米级台面（mesas）构成，以横向限制并耦合光学模式。利用偏振分辨、角度分辨和能量分辨的显微光致发光（micro-photoluminescence）测量表征发射特性。

Result: 观测到从强耦合区（strong-coupling regime）到光子激射（photon lasing）的转变，伴随跨多个晶格单元的扩展空间相干性。在圆偏振非共振激发下，发射光获得可控的圆偏振，其手性（handedness）与泵浦光一致。

Conclusion: 该结果确立了光子晶格VCSELs作为扩展光学系统中自旋可控相干发射的平台。

Abstract: We characterize spin-polarized lasing in a two-dimensional photonic lattice fabricated from a GaAs/InGaAs semiconductor microcavity sample. The lattice is defined by a staggered arrangement of rounded rectangular micrometric mesas that laterally confine and couple the optical modes. Polarization-, angle-, and energy-resolved micro-photoluminescence measurements reveal the transition from the strong-coupling regime to photon lasing, accompanied by extended spatial coherence across several lattice unit cells. Under circularly polarized nonresonant excitation, the emitted light acquires a controllable circular polarization whose handedness follows that of the pump. These results establish photonic-lattice VCSELs as a platform for spin-controlled coherent emission in extended optical systems.

### [74] [A Universal Magnetoelectric Limit for Chiral and Tellegen Bi-Isotropic Scatterers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21011)
*Jorge Olmos-Trigo*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了任意双各向同性（bi-isotropic）纳米粒子在磁电耦合（magnetoelectric coupling）上存在一个普适上界（universal upper bound），该上界仅由能量守恒（energy conservation）决定，并且对互易（reciprocal/手性）和非互易（non-reciprocal/Tellegen）粒子都适用，同时球形粒子的手性Mie系数（chiral Mie coefficient）在所有多极散射通道（multipolar scattering channels）中也服从同一上界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双各向同性纳米粒子的磁电耦合是否存在一个普适的物理极限，以及该极限是否依赖于材料属性、光照条件或互易性，此前尚不清楚。

Method: 基于能量守恒（energy conservation）这一基本物理原理进行理论推导，不依赖于具体的材料参数或入射条件，并分别考虑了互易（手性）与非互易（Tellegen）两种情况。

Result: 发现了一个仅由能量守恒决定的普适上界，该上界与材料属性和光照条件无关，且对互易和非互易纳米粒子都相同；进一步证明球形粒子的手性Mie系数在所有多极散射通道下均满足同一上界。

Conclusion: 该工作为双各向同性物体的磁电耦合引入了一个普适度量（universal metric），在单粒子水平上为手性和Tellegen光-物质相互作用设定了相同的极限。

Abstract: We reveal the existence of a universal upper bound on the magnetoelectric coupling of any bi-isotropic nanoparticle. The bound arises solely from energy conservation, making it independent of the specific material properties of the nanoparticle and illumination conditions. Moreover, the bound does not rely on reciprocity, being identical for reciprocal (chiral) and non-reciprocal (Tellegen) nanoparticles. We further show that the chiral Mie coefficient of spherical particles of arbitrary optical size obeys the same bound across all multipolar scattering channels. Our results introduce a universal metric on the magnetoelectric coupling of bi-isotropic objects, setting identical limits on chiral and Tellegen light-matter interactions at the single particle level.

### [75] [Modeling phase separation in polymer-derived carbonitride ceramics through extended machine learning molecular dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20358)
*Fabien Mortier,Sylvian Cadars,Olivier Masson,Mauro Boero,Guido Ori,Yun Wang,Samuel Bernard,Assil Bouzid*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究开发了一种适用于碳氮化硅基（Si-C-N-H）体系的机器学习原子间势（machine learning interatomic potential），基于包含9000多种构型的多样化数据库进行训练，成功实现了对聚合物衍生陶瓷（polymer-derived ceramics）在热处理过程中原子尺度演化的大规模分子动力学模拟，揭示了碳域从非晶SiCN基体中逐步成核相分离并形成类石墨烯片层的机制，同时通过缺陷碳环（5元和7元环）向稳定6元芳香结构转变的过程解释了材料的陶瓷-石墨复合特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 聚合物衍生陶瓷兼具陶瓷的热稳定性和碳域的多功能特性，但由于传统计算方法的局限，对其加工过程中原子尺度的演化进行建模仍然困难。该研究旨在突破这一瓶颈。

Method: 开发并应用了一个针对Si-C-N-H体系的机器学习原子间势（machine learning interatomic potential），使用包含非晶模型、高温态、表面和晶体结构预测的9000多种构型的多样化数据库进行训练。基于该势函数，对包含8000个原子的大体系进行了分子动力学（molecular dynamics）模拟。

Result: 模拟揭示了热处理过程中碳域从非晶SiCN基体中逐步成核相分离（phase separation）的现象，形成类石墨烯片层结构的同时保持了陶瓷网络的完整性。缺陷5元和7元碳环介导了向稳定6元芳香结构的转变。所得模型与实验原子对分布函数（atomic pair distribution functions）高度吻合。

Conclusion: 该工作为聚合物衍生陶瓷的热稳定性和结构转变路径提供了新的原子尺度见解，所建立的方法为以第一性原理精度在实验相关尺度上研究复杂非晶体系开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Polymer-derived ceramics combine the thermal stability of ceramics with the versatile properties of carbon domains, but modeling their atomic-scale evolution during processing remains elusive due to the limitations of traditional computational methods. To address this issue, here we develop and apply a machine learning interatomic potential for silicon carbonitride-based (Si-C-N-H) systems, trained on a diversified database of over 9000 configurations -including amorphous models, high-temperature states, surfaces, and crystal structure predictions - to capture the full complexity of these materials. This potential enables large-scale molecular dynamics simulations of 8000-atom systems revealing the atomic-scale evolution of the polymer-derived ceramic during thermal treatment. A key result of this work is the occurrence of a phase separation where carbon domains progressively nucleate from the amorphous SiCN matrix during thermal processing, forming distinct graphene-like sheets while preserving the integrity of the ceramic network. The resulting models reproduce the experimental atomic pair distribution functions with exceptional fidelity, validating our approach and providing microscopic explanations for the material unique combination of ceramic and graphitic properties. In this process, defective 5- and/or 7-member carbon rings, mediate the transformation to stable 6-member aromatic structures. These findings offer new atomic-scale insights into the thermal stability and structural transformation pathways of polymer-derived ceramics, while our methodology opens avenues for studying complex amorphous systems with first-principles accuracy at experimentally relevant scales.

### [76] [Dataset-aware entropy-maximized active learning for machine-learned interatomic potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20384)
*Meiyan Wang,Rishi Rao,Li Zhu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 提出一种主动学习框架，通过局域熵驱动分子动力学与全局数据集熵过滤相结合，高效生成机器学习原子间势（MLIP）的训练数据。该方法在仅需数百个DFT标记结构的情况下，即可达到近亚meV/原子精度，并在碳、硅和NaCl三种体系中相比随机MD采样将能量MAE降低约3–10倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机器学习原子间势（MLIP）的性能依赖于高质量训练数据，而传统随机分子动力学（MD）采样效率低下，容易产生冗余或覆盖不全的构型。为此，需要一种更高效的数据生成策略，能够在有限的DFT计算预算下最大化构型空间的覆盖范围和信息量。

Method: 结合局域熵（per-configuration entropy）驱动的MD轨迹偏置与全局熵过滤（global dataset-aware filtering）机制：局域熵项使MD采样偏向结构多样性高的快照，全局熵（以整个数据集指纹协方差矩阵的对数行列式衡量）用于筛选真正提供新信息的构型。采用双协方差模式（per-atom用于无序结构、per-config用于有序相），结合预训练基础模型（Allegro-OAM-L）以及来自高斯重叠矩阵（Gaussian overlap matrix）特征值的解析指纹梯度。

Result: 在碳（共价）、硅（共价/金属）和NaCl（离子）三种体系上测试，训练集规模为$10^{2}$–$10^{3}$个熵筛选的DFT标记结构，在相同分布测试数据上达到近亚meV/原子精度。与随机MD采样对比（$N=100$–$800$，每种条件三次独立抽取），熵驱动采样在$N=800$时能量MAE降低约3–10倍，增益幅度取决于键合类型和随机MD基线的饱和规模。

Conclusion: 熵驱动的主动学习框架能以极少量的DFT标记结构高效生成高质量MLIP，显著优于随机MD采样，适用于不同键合类型的材料体系及压力驱动相变场景。该方法为领域特定势函数（domain-specific potential）的自动化数据生成提供了实用方案。

Abstract: We present an active learning framework for efficiently generating training data for machine-learned interatomic potentials (MLIPs). The method combines local entropy-driven molecular dynamics with global dataset-aware filtering: a per-configuration entropy term biases MD trajectories toward structurally diverse snapshots, while a global entropy measure, the log-determinant of the fingerprint covariance matrix of the entire dataset, selects only those configurations that provide genuinely new information. We employ dual covariance modes (per-atom for disordered structures and per-config for ordered phases) to achieve broad coverage of configuration space. Combined with a pre-trained foundation model (Allegro-OAM-L) and analytical fingerprint gradients from Gaussian overlap matrix eigenvalues, the framework produces high-quality domain-specific potentials with near- or sub-meV/atom accuracy on test data drawn from the same distribution at training-set sizes of order $10^{2}$ to $10^{3}$ entropy-selected DFT-labeled structures. We demonstrate the method on three systems spanning diverse bonding types and pressure-driven phase transitions: carbon (covalent), silicon (covalent/metallic), and NaCl (ionic). In learning curve comparisons against random molecular dynamics sampling at matched training set sizes ($N = 100$ to $800$), evaluated over three independent training-set draws per condition, entropy-driven sampling achieves a factor of approximately $3$ to $10$ lower energy MAE at $N = 800$ on in-distribution holdouts across the three systems, with the magnitude of the gain depending on the bonding type and the size at which the random-MD baseline saturates.

</details>


### [77] [Evaluating Blended Refrigerants for Thermochemical Energy Storage and Circular Refrigerant Recovery using Activated Carbons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20446)
*H. Lucassen,A. Luna-Triguero,J. M. Vicent-Luna*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究开发了一种多尺度计算工作流，结合蒙特卡洛模拟、热力学建模和穿透模拟，基于纯组分吸附数据预测制冷剂混合物在活性炭中的吸附、储存和分离行为，用于热化学储能和制冷剂回收。结果表明，混合制冷剂因协同吸附效应可实现比纯组分更高的储能密度，且活性炭能选择性分离关键制冷剂组分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 气候危机要求快速转向可持续能源技术并提升现有能源系统的效率。吸附式热化学储能（adsorption-based thermochemical energy storage）因其高能量密度和与可再生热源的兼容性，成为一种有前景的替代方案；同时，制冷剂的循环回收也具有重要的环境意义。

Method: 开发了一个多尺度计算工作流（multiscale computational workflow），整合蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）、热力学建模（thermodynamic modeling）和穿透模拟（breakthrough simulations），从纯组分吸附数据预测吸附、储存和分离行为。该方法结合了吸附势理论（adsorption potential theory, APT）、理想吸附溶液理论（ideal adsorbed solution theory, IAST）以及等量吸附热模型，并开发了内部计算框架用于计算纯制冷剂和多组分混合物的吸附热与储能密度。

Result: 混合制冷剂由于协同吸附（cooperative adsorption）和更高效的分子堆积（molecular packing），能够实现比纯制冷剂更高的储能密度。此外，活性炭能够选择性分离关键制冷剂组分，展示了其在可持续制冷剂回收方面的潜力。

Conclusion: 本研究提供了一个通用框架，用于吸附驱动型储能和分离应用中下一代制冷剂混合物的理性设计与筛选。该工作流虽以分子模拟为基准开发，但由于仅需纯组分吸附等温线作为输入，可直接推广应用于实验研究。

Abstract: The climate crisis demands a rapid shift to sustainable energy technologies and higher efficiency in existing energy systems. Adsorption-based thermochemical energy storage is a promising alternative due to its high energy density and compatibility with renewable heat sources. In this work, we investigate the adsorption behavior of pure refrigerants (R32, R125, R134a, and R600) and their commercial blends (R410A, R407F, R417A, and R417C) in six activated carbons for thermochemical energy storage and circular refrigerant recovery. A multiscale computational workflow combining Monte Carlo simulations, thermodynamic modeling, and breakthrough simulations is developed to predict adsorption, storage, and separation behavior from pure-component adsorption data. The methodology integrates adsorption potential theory (APT), ideal adsorbed solution theory (IAST), and models for the isosteric heat of adsorption. In addition, an in-house computational framework is developed to calculate heats of adsorption and energy storage densities for both pure refrigerants and multicomponent mixtures. Although developed using molecular simulations as a benchmark, the methodology is directly applicable to experimental studies, since it only requires adsorption isotherms of the pure components as input to evaluate the performance of refrigerant blends. The results show that refrigerant blends can achieve higher storage densities than their pure counterparts due to cooperative adsorption and more efficient molecular packing. Furthermore, the activated carbons selectively separate key refrigerant components, highlighting their potential for sustainable refrigerant recovery. Overall, this work provides a general framework for the rational design and screening of next-generation refrigerant blends for adsorption-driven energy storage and separation applications.

</details>

Abstract: Triple junctions, line defects formed by the intersection of different grain boundaries, exist within all polycrystalline materials. While it has long been recognized that triple junctions could play an important role in microstructural evolution, there remains much uncertainty regarding their properties. Triple junctions are line defects capable of carrying dislocation content. However, no general method for calculating this content has been established. In this work, we derive the necessary equations to calculate the intrinsic dislocation content of a triple junction whose trichromatic pattern forms a coincidence site lattice. Importantly, we identify two distinct charge-state-dependent coupling regimes and extend this picture to correlated defect ensembles, explaining the wide diversity of experimental observations. In this work, a machine learning force field is developed based on the moment tensor potential approach, allowing us to understand the atomistic origin of the structural evolution and crystallization kinetics in Sb$_2$S$_3$ for the first time, by enabling large-scale molecular dynamics simulations (up to 7680 atoms for 40 ns). Sb$_2$S$_3$ shows anisotropic growth rates with the [100] facet exhibiting the fastest growth due to the strong Sb-S covalent bonding along its quasi-1D ribbon-like structure of its crystalline phase. The activation energy for crystal growth is found to be 0.55-0.57 eV, whereas that for diffusion is around 1.16-1.56 eV. The lower activation energy for crystal growth indicates that its heterogeneous crystallization is interface controlled rather than diffusion limited, unlike GST and GeTe with atomic attachment at the solid-liquid interface being energetically favoured over long range atomic transport. Abstract: Topological phononics extends the foundational concepts of topological condensed matter physics to the realm of lattice vibrations and classical mechanical waves, unlocking robust, defect-immune states and phenomena beyond the reach of conventional phononic engineering. This review provides a unified, systematic framework for understanding topological phonons across natural and artificial systems, spanning solid-state materials, acoustic/mechanical metamaterials, and non-Hermitian platforms. We also highlight technological applications in robust waveguides, on-chip surface-acoustic-wave devices, and acoustofluidics, while outlining future challenges and opportunities in quantum phononics, nonlinear topological phenomena, and interdisciplinary integration with photonics and electronics. ### [85] [High-performance linear-scaling electronic structure method via chromatic superposition states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20918)
*Zhikang Jiang,Zhizhi Xiao,Mingfa Tang,Weiyu Li,Zhaoru Sun,Ke Xia,Youqi Ke*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于色叠加态（chromatic superposition states, CSS）的高性能线性标度电子结构方法，通过图着色方案将不相关的轨道聚合为低维高保真表示，结合块-Lanczos Krylov 方法实现线性标度计算，已在小规模上比传统线性标度密度矩阵纯化方法快一个数量级以上，并成功应用于 10000 个 H₂O 的分子动力学模拟和 100 万个 H₂O 的自洽计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有线性标度电子结构方法在大规模体系（如数万至百万原子）的计算效率仍有限，需要一种既能大幅降低表示维度、又能保持高精度且具有硬件高效性的方法，以推动大尺度 Kohn-Sham 密度矩阵的快速求解。

Method: 基于体系的有限关联长度（finite correlation length），利用图着色（graph-coloring）方案将不相关轨道聚合为色叠加态（CSS），形成独立于体系大小、低维且高保真的表示空间；通过块-Lanczos Krylov 方法（block-Lanczos Krylov method）高效计算 CSS 上的投影，实现线性标度（linear-scaling）成本和硬件高效性，从而快速求解 Kohn-Sham 密度矩阵。

Result: 该方法在小规模体系上已比传统线性标度密度矩阵纯化方法（density matrix purification method）的计算速度快一个数量级以上，且保持高精度；成功完成了 10000 个 H₂O 的分子动力学模拟（molecular dynamics simulation）和 100 万个 H₂O 的自洽计算（self-consistent calculation），计算资源需求适中。

Conclusion: 基于色叠加态（CSS）的线性标度电子结构方法在大规模体系计算中展现出显著的速度优势和精度保障，有望成为大尺度 Kohn-Sham 方程求解的高效实用工具。

Abstract: We introduce a high-performance linear-scaling electronic structure method that employs chromatic superposition states (CSS) as a low-dimensional, high-fidelity representation, which can be orders of magnitude smaller than the full Hilbert space. Grounded in the system's finite correlation length, the CSS representation aggregates the uncorrelated orbitals into a single basis via a graph-coloring scheme, and is independent of the system size yet accurately preserves all sparse operators in solving the Kohn-Sham equations. The projection onto CSSs is efficiently computed by employing the block-Lanczos Krylov method which features high hardware efficiency and linear-scaling cost, enabling fast calculation of large-scale Kohn-Sham density matrix. We show that this method already outperforms previous linear-scaling density matrix purification method by more than one order of magnitude in computational speed at even small scale, while preserving high accuracy. The practical utility of the CSS method is demonstrated through molecular dynamics simulation of a 10000 $H_2O$, and self-consistent calculation of a 1-million $H_2O$ with modest resources.

</details>

Conclusion: K$_{1-x}$CrTe$_2$的铁磁序与CrTe$_2$类似，但与LiCrTe$_2$和NaCrTe$_2$的层间反铁磁序不同，这些差异可能源于层间距、Cr氧化态或堆叠方式的变化。该材料为研究二维磁体（two-dimensional magnets）中的自旋取向和维度效应提供了可调谐的平台。

Abstract: Layered chromium tellurides are model systems for studying low-dimensional magnetism in van der Waals materials. Neutron diffraction reveals ferromagnetic alignment of Cr spins within and between layers. This contrasts with the out-of-plane A-type antiferromagnetism in LiCrTe$_2$ and NaCrTe$_2$, but resembles CrTe$_2$. These differences likely arise from changes in interlayer spacing, Cr oxidation state, or stacking. Overall, K$_{1-x}$CrTe$_2$ provides a tunable platform for studying spin orientation and dimensionality in two-dimensional magnets.

### [90] [Observation of spin-free interatomic orbital angular momentum in a chiral crystal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21124)
*Dongjin Oh,Sungsoo Hahn,Chiara Pacella,Junseo Yoo,Angel Rubio,Domenico Di Sante,Changyoung Kim*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 实验上，利用角分辨光电子能谱（ARPES）在手性Te晶体中解析出与p轨道能带明确分离的孤立s轨道能带；结合圆二色性ARPES（circular dichroism ARPES）和第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）分析OAM的起源；使用自旋分辨ARPES（spin-resolved ARPES）检验自旋极化（SAM）的存在与否。

Result: 实验观察到孤立的s轨道能带，圆二色性ARPES和计算表明这些能带上的OAM完全来自于原子间跃迁（interatomic hopping），无原子内贡献；自旋分辨ARPES确认不存在自旋角动量（SAM），即实现了无自旋极化的OAM态。

Conclusion: 该工作证实了在晶体中可在无自旋极化的情况下存在纯轨道角动量，强调了原子间OAM的关键作用，并为设计无自旋OAM态和实现纯轨道电流提供了通用框架，推动了轨道电子学（orbitronics）的发展。

Abstract: The inherent spin-orbit interaction of electrons inevitably couples spin to the orbital angular momentum (OAM), posing a fundamental challenge to spin-free orbital transport. Here, we propose a novel strategy to achieve spin-decoupled OAM states in crystalline solids. Using angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy (ARPES), we resolve well-isolated s-orbital bands in a chiral Te crystal, clearly separated from the p-orbital manifold. Combined circular dichroism ARPES and first-principles calculations reveal that these bands host OAM arising exclusively from interatomic hopping, with no intra-atomic contribution. Spin-resolved ARPES further confirms the absence of SAM, providing decisive evidence of spin-free OAM states. This work provides a general framework for designing spinless OAM states, opening an opportunity toward pure orbital currents for orbitronics.
