<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有非常规磁性研究已根据自旋纹理在动量反演（momentum inversion）下的宇称将其分为交变磁体（altermagnets，偶宇称）和奇宇称磁体（odd-parity magnets），但完整对称性图谱（symmetry landscape）尚未被充分探索，亟需一个更系统的分类框架来发现新磁性相。

Method: 基于自旋纹理的表示理论以及与之关联的宇称性质，构建系统分类框架；推导出将混合宇称磁体划分为三种类型的普适对称性判据（universal symmetry criteria）；以FePO4为例进行第一性原理计算来验证理论预测。

Result: 预测了两种新型磁体类别：混合宇称磁体（其自旋纹理各笛卡尔分量呈现对比性宇称）和无约束宇称磁体（自旋纹理宇称无法定义）；HPM可结合交变磁体与奇宇称磁体的自旋分裂（spin splitting）特性，实现自旋流与埃德尔斯坦效应的共存；FePO4的第一性原理计算证实了这一共存现象。

Conclusion: 该工作为非常规磁性提供了全面的对称性分类，并将混合宇称磁体确立为多功能自旋电子学（multi-functional spintronics）的一个有前景的平台。

Abstract: Unconventional magnetism has emerged as a transformative frontier in condensed matter physics. Such phases are characterized by substantial non-relativistic spin splitting (NSS) in symmetry-compensated magnets. They have been classified by the parity of their spin textures under momentum inversion, leading to the paradigms of altermagnets (even-parity) and odd-parity magnets. However, the full symmetry landscape remains largely unexplored. In this Letter, we present a systematic classification framework for unconventional magnetism based on the representation theory of the spin textures and the associated parity properties. Within this framework, we predict two previously unidentified classes beyond the established pure-parity categories: hybrid-parity magnets (HPMs) and unconstrained-parity magnets (UPMs), where the spin textures exhibit contrasting parities among their Cartesian components and the parity of the spin textures is ill-defined, respectively. We derive universal symmetry criteria that categorize HPMs into three distinct types. Importantly, by combining the spin splitting characteristics of altermagnets and odd-parity magnets, HPMs can enable the coexistence of the spin current and Edelstein effects. Taking FePO4 as an example, we perform first-principles calculations to demonstrate this coexistence. Finally, we discuss the potential applications of HPMs in spintronic devices. Our work provides a comprehensive symmetry classification of unconventional magnetism and establishes HPMs as a promising platform for multi-functional spintronics.

</details>


### [94] [Occupation Dynamics of Floquet-Volkov States and Spectral Sum Rule](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21339)
*Xuanxi Cai,Changhua Bao,Benshu Fan,Haoyuan Zhong,Fei Wang,Shaohua Zhou,Tianyun Lin,Hongyun Zhang,Pu Yu,Peizhe Tang,Wenhui Duan,Shuyun Zhou*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文利用时间分辨角分辨光电子能谱（TrARPES）在两种半导体（黑磷和MoSe₂）中揭示了Floquet-Volkov态的瞬态占据，并发现亚带隙驱动下所有边带的总光谱权重守恒。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解时间周期光场如何调控量子材料中电子态的瞬态占据及其对瞬态材料性质的影响，是光场调控材料性质的关键问题，但此前对Floquet态占据动力学的直接实验观测尚不充分。

Method: 采用时间分辨角分辨光电子能谱（time- and angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy, TrARPES）直接测量光诱导边带的光谱权重，从而揭示Floquet-Volkov态的瞬态占据行为。

Result: 在亚带隙驱动条件下，尽管光诱导边带的占据强烈依赖于驱动场，但将所有边带求和得到的总光谱权重（spectral weight）是守恒的。

Conclusion: 该发现为Floquet布居动力学（Floquet population dynamics）提供了关键见解，这对利用光场调控瞬态材料性质具有重要意义。

Abstract: Time-periodic light fields can dress electronic states in quantum materials, forming Floquet states whose dynamic occupation determines transient material properties. Here by using time- and angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy (TrARPES), we reveal the transient occupation of Floquet-Volkov states in two semiconductors, black phosphorus and MoSe$_2$. While the occupation of the light-induced sidebands, directly reflected by TrARPES spectral weight, strongly depends on the driving field, we find that the total spectral weight obtained by summing up all sidebands is conserved upon below-gap driving. Our work provides critical insights into the Floquet population dynamics, which are essential for light-field tailoring of transient material properties.

</details>


### [95] [Ultra-Confinement of Polaritons in Single Atomic Layer Ag Photonic Quantum Dots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21345)
*Xinyi Li,Tetyana Ignatova,Chengye Dong,Krishnan Mekkanamkulam Ananthanarayanan,Rinu Abraham Maniyara,Arpit Jain,Furkan Turker,Vinay Kammarchedu,Aida Ebrahimi,Joshua A. Robinson,Slava V. Rotkin*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文针对二维范德华异质结构（vdWHs）中受限极化激元（confined polaritons）的定量分析难题，发展了一种解析方法，能够在亚波长尺度揭示局部传播常数（local propagation constant）并实现亚波长分辨率映射。应用于SiC/2D-Ag/EG光子纳米结构后，发现极化激元在垂直（~λ/50）和水平方向（~λ/40）均被高度压缩。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维范德华异质结构（vdWHs）中受限极化激元（confined polaritons）的定量分析面临挑战，现有方法无法在亚波长尺度上映射波动周期，也难以识别合适的基底“背景”以进行扣除，从而难以提取波长等关键参数。

Method: 发展了一种解析方法（analytical approach），用于在亚波长映射受限条件下揭示受限极化激元的局部传播常数（local propagation constant），并实现亚波长分辨率（sub-wavelength resolution）的映射。

Result: 将该方法应用于SiC/2D-Ag/EG（外延石墨烯，epitaxial graphene）光子纳米结构（photonic nanostructures），发现极化激元在垂直方向被压缩至约λ/50，在水平方向被压缩至约λ/40，表明二维金属实现了高度的双向光场局域。

Conclusion: 所提出的解析方法有效克服了受限极化激元定量分析的现有障碍，能够获得高分辨率的局部传播常数映射，为深入理解vdWHs中的光-物质相互作用及极化激元传播特性提供了新工具。

Abstract: Light scattering by two-dimensional (2D) van der Waals heterostructures (vdWHs) is immense, especially given their infinitesimal volume, thus enabling strong light-matter interactions. Surface 2D polariton waves manifest through large concentration of electromagnetic field in vertical direction, normal to their propagation. By confining vdWH materials into 2D photonic shapes, one can manipulate and compress light in lateral directions. Scattering-type scanning near-field optical microscopy is a perfect tool for direct imaging of the propagating polaritons and studying the properties of confined polaritons in nanostructures. Though, thus far the quantitative analysis, such the wavelength extraction, has been challenged for confined polaritons by incapability of mapping of the wave period on sub-wavelength scale and difficulty of identifying an adequate substrate's "background" to subtract. Here, an analytical approach is developed to reveal the local propagation constant of confined polaritons under abovementioned constraints and map it with the sub-wavelength resolution. Applied to analysis of the SiC/2D-Ag/EG (epitaxial graphene) photonic nanostructures, the technique uncovered that the polaritons are highly confined in both vertical ($\simλ$/50) and lateral directions ($\simλ$/40) by 2D metal.

</details>


### [96] [Pulse-Driven Reconfiguration of Fractional Polar Topology in Zr-Substituted Barium Titanate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21368)
*Florian Mayer*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过有效哈密顿量分子动力学模拟，在有序掺锆钛酸钡中发现了一种由分数拓扑荷（拓扑夸克）构成的极化拓扑结构，并证明通过皮秒级局域电场脉冲可以重构这一结构，实现多态可配置自由度，为超快铁电拓扑器件的概念验证提供了计算基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索铁电体中极化拓扑纹理（polar topological textures）能否承载超越单一整数拓扑荷的内部结构，以及这种内部分数拓扑（fractional topology）能否通过局域电激励实现可重构。

Method: 采用有效哈密顿量分子动力学（effective-Hamiltonian molecular-dynamics）模拟，对有序12.5% Zr取代钛酸钡（barium titanate）施加皮秒级局域电场脉冲，并通过二元脉冲掩模协议（binary pulse-mask protocol）对六个涡旋核心柱进行寻址，在低温条件下计算弛豫后的亚稳态构型。

Result: 化学倍周期沿极化轴方向稳定了一种由交替Q = -2反斯格明子切片与Q = +4斯格明子切片构成的耦合纳米畴纹理，局域拓扑荷碎裂为六个-1/3和六个+2/3的局域贡献（拓扑夸克）。64种二元脉冲掩模均导致不同的亚稳态构型，程序化状态在模拟时间尺度上至少稳定1纳秒，且可通过扇区分辨拓扑指纹与实空间极化场区分。

Conclusion: 计算结果表明，铁电纳米畴中的分数极化拓扑（fractional polar topology）可通过超快电激励实现局域重构，并在理想低温条件下作为一种多态可配置自由度（multistate configurational degree of freedom）使用，提供了概念验证的计算依据。

Abstract: Polar topological textures in ferroelectrics can host internal structure beyond a single integer topological charge. Here, effective-Hamiltonian molecular-dynamics simulations are used to examine whether such internal fractional topology can be reconfigured by local electric excitation in ordered 12.5% Zr-substituted barium titanate. Chemical doubling along the polar axis stabilizes a coupled nanodomain texture consisting of alternating Q = -2 antiskyrmionic and Q = +4 skyrmionic slices, in which the local topological charge fragments into six -1/3 and six +2/3 localized contributions, denoted here as topological quarks, separated by Bloch-point-like singular conversion regions. Picosecond local electric-field pulses applied to selected vortex-core columns drive reconfiguration of the internal dipolar texture of a 2.6 nm nanodomain. Under a binary pulse-mask protocol addressing the six vortex cores, all 64 masks lead, within the chosen low-temperature simulation protocol, to distinct relaxed metastable configurations. The switching calculations are performed in a cryogenic regime, and the programmed states remain stable over at least 1 ns of field-free evolution on the simulation timescale. The resulting configurations are distinguishable both by sector-resolved topological fingerprints and by their real-space polarization fields. These results provide a computational proof of concept that fractional polar topology in a ferroelectric nanodomain can be locally reconfigured by ultrafast electric excitation and used as a multistate configurational degree of freedom in an idealized low-temperature setting.

</details>


### [97] [Phonon Interactions in Metal Halide Perovskites elucidated by Raman Scattering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21415)
*Alejandro R. Goñi*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本篇综述文章聚焦金属卤化物钙钛矿（MHPs）中无机笼状晶格与A位阳离子亚晶格之间的耦合作用，重点通过拉曼散射（Raman scattering）技术分析其振动谱特征。文章特别讨论了强拉曼背景信号——中心峰（central peak）的起源，将其归因于无序诱导的二阶声学声子拉曼散射，并借助其他半导体体系（如Ge量子点和GaAs/AlAs超晶格）的类比，构建了一个统一的声子相互作用图像，以解释MHPs的拉曼光谱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 金属卤化物钙钛矿（metal halide perovskites, MHPs）优异的光电性质被认为主要源于无机笼状晶格与A位阳离子亚晶格之间的特殊耦合作用，这种耦合通过晶格势的非简谐性（anharmonicity）和/或静态/动态无序显著影响其振动谱（声子频率、线宽和寿命）。理解这些声子相互作用的本质，对于正确解读MHPs的拉曼光谱（Raman spectra）至关重要。

Method: 本文以综述（perspective）形式，系统梳理了已有的实验证据，重点分析了拉曼散射（Raman scattering）信号在不同耦合机制（主要依赖氢键（hydrogen bonding）或空间位阻（steric hindrance））下的特征。特别针对在立方相和四方相稳定温度范围内观测到的、随A位阳离子动力学展开而出现的强拉曼背景（即中心峰（central peak））的起源争议，进行了专门讨论。

Result: 中心峰信号主要被解释为无序诱导的二阶声学声子拉曼散射（disorder-induced second-order acoustic-phonon Raman scattering）。这一解释得到了其他具有纳米尺度结构无序的半导体系统的支持，例如多堆叠异质结构中Ge量子点的垂直错位，以及短周期GaAs/AlAs超晶格的界面粗糙度所导致的中心拉曼峰现象。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一个关于MHPs中声子相互作用及其对各类拉曼过程影响的统一图像，该图像对于正确解读MHPs拉曼光谱具有关键意义。

Abstract: There is a growing consensus that the exceptional optoelectronic properties of metal halide perovskites (MHPs) are largely due to the peculiar interplay between the inorganic cage lattice, composed of a labile network of corner-sharing metal halide octahedra, and the A-site cationic sublattice. This interaction significantly affects the vibrational spectrum of MHPs (phonon frequencies, linewidths, and lifetimes), resulting from the effects of lattice potential anharmonicity and/or static/dynamic disorder. Raman scattering is a suitable technique to probe phonon interactions in solids, allowing for the in-situ characterization of chemical environments, revealing the nature of lattice vibrations. In this perspective, the available experimental evidence of the aforementioned interplay will be reviewed with special emphasis on understanding Raman signatures depending on whether the coupling is principally mediated by hydrogen bonding or steric hindrance. The controversy about the origin of a strong Raman background, steeply rising towards zero Raman shift and called central peak, will be specifically addressed. This background signal, which is typically observed in the temperature range of stability of cubic and tetragonal phases when the A-site cation dynamics unfold, will be shown to be mostly due to disorder-induced second-order acoustic-phonon Raman scattering. This interpretation receives support from other semiconductor systems with nanoscale structural disorder, where the central Raman peak arises either from the vertical misalignment of Ge quantum dots in multi-stack heterostructures or from the interface roughness exhibited by short-period GaAs/AlAs superlattices. In this way, a unifying picture of phonon interactions in MHPs and how they impact different Raman processes is provided, which is key to interpreting their Raman spectra.

</details>

### [98] [Random Matrix Spectra from Boltzmann-Weighted Lattice Ensembles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21254)
*Yaprak Önder,Abbas Ali Saberi,Roderich Moessner*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文引入了一个随机矩阵（random matrix）框架，通过谱可观测量研究统计力学晶格系统。该框架将平衡构型映射为矩阵系综，其协方差结构继承自底层模型的空间关联，从而在实空间关联函数与动量空间方差剖面之间建立直接桥梁。通过二维伊辛模型和三维Edwards–Anderson自旋玻璃的蒙特卡洛数据验证，发现谱分布从高温下的半圆律（semicircle law）演变为反映关联结构的模型依赖临界形式，为探测有序与无序统计系统中的集体行为提供了一条量化谱路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的统计力学方法主要通过实空间关联函数描述多体系统的集体行为，缺乏一种将谱可观测量（spectral observables）与统计关联直接联系起来的统一数学框架。本文旨在填补这一空白，通过随机矩阵理论构建从空间关联结构到动量空间谱特征的桥梁。

Method: 从玻尔兹曼测度（Boltzmann measure）采样的平衡构型被映射为矩阵系综，其协方差结构由底层模型的空间关联决定。该方法将实空间关联函数变换为动量空间方差剖面（variance profile），并在有限关联长度和临界区域内推导该剖面。谱矩的计算通过Wick收缩展开（Wick-contraction expansion）实现，体密度（bulk density）的自洽描述则利用预解式形式（resolvent formalism）完成。

Result: 对于二维伊辛模型和三维Edwards–Anderson自旋玻璃，谱分布在高温极限下收敛于半圆律，而在临界区域内演变为反映关联结构的模型依赖形式。该框架成功将统计力学关联与相关随机矩阵系综（correlated random matrix ensembles）联系起来，并通过蒙特卡洛数据验证了理论预测。

Conclusion: 该框架提供了一条通过谱可观测量定量探测有序与无序统计系统中集体行为的路径，同时定义了一类具有物理动机的相关随机矩阵系综，为统计力学与随机矩阵理论之间的交叉研究开辟了新方向。

Abstract: We introduce a random matrix framework for studying statistical-mechanical lattice systems through spectral observables. Equilibrium configurations sampled from a Boltzmann measure are mapped to matrix ensembles whose covariance structure is inherited from the spatial correlations of the underlying model. This construction maps real-space correlation functions to a momentum-space variance profile, providing a direct bridge between statistical-mechanical correlations and correlated random matrix ensembles. We derive this variance profile in finite-correlation-length and critical regimes, and compute spectral moments within a Wick-contraction expansion. A complementary self-consistent description of the bulk density is developed using the resolvent formalism. These analytical methods are benchmarked against Monte Carlo data for the two-dimensional Ising model and three-dimensional Edwards--Anderson spin glasses. In both cases, the spectra evolve from the semicircle law at high temperature to model-dependent critical forms reflecting the structure of correlations. The framework, therefore, provides a quantitative spectral route to probing collective behavior in ordered and disordered statistical systems, while also defining a class of physically motivated correlated random matrix ensembles.

</details>


### [99] [Dynamical systems on ultra small-world networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21364)
*Nirbhay Patil,Ada Altieri,Fabian Aguirre-Lopez*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个适用于高度异质性网络（highly heterogeneous networks）的动力学平均场理论（dynamical mean-field theory）框架，能够处理由网络约束引起的度相关（degree correlations），即结构截断（structural cut-offs）。将该框架应用于无序Lotka-Volterra模型后，发现在超小世界网络（ultra small-world networks）上，存活率（survival rates）和稳定性（stability）等常见观测量的预测与模拟及经验网络数据吻合更好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实中的社会、经济和生态网络往往具有小世界性质（small-world nature），节点间距离甚至随系统规模呈亚对数增长，但理论分析常假设系统处于该区间之外以便于解析处理。现有理论无法充分解释高度异质性网络中由网络约束自然产生的度相关，即结构截断。

Method: 推导了一个基于动力学平均场理论（dynamical mean-field theory）的框架，专门针对高度异质性网络，能够纳入由网络约束引起的度相关（结构截断）。将该框架应用于无序Lotka-Volterra模型，并在超小世界网络上进行分析。

Result: 对于模拟的幂律网络（power-law networks）和经验网络，该框架在所有指数范围内对存活率和稳定性等观测量的预测与实际数据吻合更好。

Conclusion: 所提出的框架显著提升了在高度异质性和超小世界网络条件下对生态网络模型行为的理论预测精度，验证了考虑结构截断等网络约束的重要性。

Abstract: Despite the knowledge that social, economical, and ecological networks are often of a small-world nature with inter-nodal distance growing even slower than logarithmically with system size, we often assume theoretical systems to be outside of this regime, to make them easier to treat analytically. Here we derive a framework to apply the powerful dynamical mean-field theory on highly heterogeneous networks that is able to account for more of the degree correlations naturally arising from network constraints, known as structural cut-offs. We apply this framework to the well-studied and understood disordered Lotka-Volterra model, and show typically reported observables such as survival rates and stability for these systems on ultra small-world networks. We find much better agreement for these variables for all ranges of exponents for simulated power-law networks as well as empirically sourced networks.

</details>


### [100] [Temperature-induced optical enhancement near a localization transition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21423)
*Raul Liquito,Miguel Gonçalves,Bruno Amorim,Eduardo V. Castro*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该论文系统研究了Aubry-André模型中准周期势（quasiperiodic potential）对有限频率光电导（optical conductivity）的影响，发现临界点附近低频光信号出现不连续闭合的光学带隙（optical gap），并揭示了热激活Pauli阻塞跃迁导致特定共振频率处光电导显著增强的机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准周期系统在金属-绝缘体转变（metal-insulator transition，MIT）附近的输运性质已被广泛研究，但有限频率光电导的系统性分析尚付阙如。本文旨在填补这一空白，深入理解临界区附近的光学响应行为。

Method: 以Aubry-André模型为范例，通过理论计算对零温与有限温下的光学电导率（optical conductivity）进行详细研究，分析准周期势对低频光信号的重构效应，并识别共振增强的微观起源。

Result: 零温下低频光学信号被准周期势强烈重构，出现一个在MIT临近时不连续闭合的光学带隙；在有限温下，特定共振频率处观察到低频光电导的显著增强，该增强源于强共振范霍夫奇点（van Hove singularities）之间Pauli阻塞跃迁的热激活。

Conclusion: 该机制为准周期系统中有限频率输运提供了新见解，并开辟了一条操控局域化转变（localization transition）附近光学特性的新途径。此外，光学响应可作为一种强有力的实验探针，用于检测非平凡准周期效应。

Abstract: Quasiperiodic systems are an intermediate class of systems between periodic crystals and disordered systems, famously exhibiting metal-insulator transitions (MITs) even in one dimension. While their transport properties have been studied extensively, a systematic analysis of the finite-frequency optical conductivity near the critical point has been lacking. In this work, we carry out a detailed study of the optical conductivity in the paradigmatic Aubry-André model. We find that the zero-temperature low-frequency optical signal is strongly restructured by the quasiperiodic potential, exhibiting an optical gap that closes discontinuously as the system approaches the MIT. Most strikingly, we uncover a mechanism for a strong enhancement of the low-frequency finite temperature optical conductivity at certain resonant frequencies. This enhancement stems from the thermal activation of Pauli-blocked transitions between strongly resonant van Hove singularities. This mechanism provides new insight into finite-frequency transport in quasiperiodic systems and a new pathway for manipulating optical properties near a localization transition. Furthermore, our findings establish the optical response as a powerful, experimentally accessible tool for probing non-trivial quasiperiodicity effects.

</details>

# astro-ph.CO [[Back]](#toc)

### [101] [Effective Field Theory for a Baryon-Correlated Dark Matter Profile](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20217)
*Kento Kamada*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文针对标准ΛCDM模型在小尺度上遇到的核尖-核团问题、星系旋转曲线多样性和Tully-Fisher关系等挑战，提出一个有效场论（EFT）框架为经验规律ρ_DM ∝ Φ_b²提供理论基础。通过引入质量简并的标量、矢量和张量中介子（耦合比4:6:3）以及一个5维时空起源，揭示了暗物质与重子物质之间的相互作用机制，使得暗物质场χ在宇宙学尺度表现为标准冷暗物质（CDM），而在星系尺度由其相互作用能主导动力学，并最终为Tully-Fisher关系提供了理论解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准ΛCDM模型在大尺度上取得成功，但在小尺度上面临核尖-核团问题（core-cusp problem）、星系旋转曲线多样性（diversity of galaxy rotation curves）和Tully-Fisher关系等持续挑战。作者此前提出的经验规律ρ_DM ∝ Φ_b²虽能复现观测旋转曲线并解决核尖和多样性问题，但缺乏理论基础，因此需要构建一个理论框架来为该经验规律提供微物理学起源。

Method: 构建一个有效场论（EFT），引入有质量标量、矢量和张量中介子（mediator）作为重子物质与暗物质场χ之间的媒介。通过设定中介子耦合比为4:6:3且质量简并，精确抵消了作用在重子上的额外第五力（fifth forces）至O(v²)阶。进一步将该理论框架推广至5维（5D）时空，将重子源视为5D零流（null fluid），揭示三个中介子起源于单个5D对称张量场。将场χ限制在4D膜（brane）上，分析其与中介子的相互作用。

Result: 三个中介子可由单个5D对称张量场导出；场χ被限制在4D膜上时，其与中介子的相互作用产生一个无压能密度（pressureless energy density）ρ_int ∝ Φ_b²，满足经验所需的重子关联廓线。场χ呈现尺度依赖的转变：在宇宙学尺度上，其质量能表现为标准冷暗物质（CDM）；在星系尺度上，其相互作用能主导局部动力学。通过评估该局域化相互作用区域的动力学边界，得到关系μ = K M_b^{-3/2}，为Tully-Fisher关系提供了理论依据。

Conclusion: 本研究为经验规律ρ_DM ∝ Φ_b²提供了从有效场论到高维时空的理论基础，统一解释了ΛCDM模型在小尺度上的多个难题。暗物质场χ的尺度依赖行为（宇宙学尺度上的CDM与星系尺度上的相互作用能主导）是该框架的核心特征，而导出的μ = K M_b^{-3/2}关系为Tully-Fisher关系提供了物理解释。

Abstract: While the standard $Λ$CDM model succeeds on large cosmological scales, it faces persistent small-scale challenges, including the core-cusp problem, the diversity of galaxy rotation curves, and the Tully-Fisher relation. To address these issues, we recently proposed an empirical law where the effective dark matter energy density is directly correlated with the baryonic gravitational potential, $ρ_{\rm DM} \propto Φ_b^2$, which reproduces observed rotation curves and resolves the core-cusp and diversity problems. To provide a theoretical foundation for this empirical law, we construct an effective field theory (EFT) introducing massive scalar, vector, and tensor mediators between baryons and a dark sector field $χ$. We demonstrate that aligning the mediator couplings to a specific ratio (4:6:3) with degenerate masses exactly cancels the additional fifth forces acting on baryons up to $O(v^2)$. We then show that this theoretical framework originates from a 5-dimensional (5D) spacetime. Treating the baryonic source as a 5D null fluid reveals that the three mediators emerge from a single 5D symmetric tensor field. By confining the field $χ$ to a 4D brane, we reveal that its interaction with these mediators generates a pressureless energy density ($ρ_{\rm int} \propto Φ_b^2$) that yields the empirically required baryon-correlated profile. Consequently, the field $χ$ exhibits a scale-dependent transition: on cosmological scales, its mass energy acts as standard Cold Dark Matter (CDM), whereas on galactic scales, its interaction energy governs local dynamics. Finally, by evaluating the dynamical boundary of this localized interaction region, we provide a physical interpretation that yields the relation $μ= K M_b^{-3/2}$, offering a theoretical basis for the Tully-Fisher relation.

</details>


### [102] [Cosmological perturbations with $f(R)$ gravity scalarons : Galaxy power spectra and the scalaron mass](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20227)
*Abhijit Talukdar,Sanjeev Kalita,Shadab Alam*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究 $f(R)$ 引力标量场（scalaron）引起的宇宙学微扰，分析从早期广义相对论（GR）相向晚期非 GR 相过渡时期物质功率谱（matter power spectrum）相对于 $Λ$CDM 模型的偏离，发现单极及四极功率在小尺度增大、四极功率在大尺度保持较高，并报告标量场质量（scalaron mass）在星系与黑洞尺度的 GR 极限及其随宇宙时演化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前宇宙学模型以 $Λ$CDM 为基准，但 $f(R)$ 修正引力理论（modified gravity theory）可能解释暗能量与早期膨胀。本研究旨在考察 $f(R)$ 理论在宇宙从早期 GR 相到晚期非 GR 相过渡时期的可观测效应，特别是物质功率谱的偏离，为未来星系巡天提供检验引力的可观测特征（observables）。

Method: 采用接近 $Λ$CDM 的可行 $f(R)$ 引力拉格朗日量（Lagrangian），分析宇宙学微扰（cosmological perturbations）演化。利用星系偏差（galaxy bias）、速度弥散（velocity dispersion）和修正引力参数（modified gravity parameters）生成星系功率谱多极矩（galaxy power spectra multipoles），对比 $Λ$CDM 预言。

Result: 在 $f(R)$ 理论中，单极（monopole）与四极（quadrupole）物质功率谱在大波数 $k$（小尺度）增大；四极功率谱在小波数 $k$（大尺度）相对 $Λ$CDM 保持较高，直至 $k \approx 0.02$。标量场质量（scalaron mass）在星系与超大质量黑洞（massive black hole）尺度得到合适的 GR 极限。

Conclusion: 标量场质量随宇宙时（cosmic time）减小导致与 GR 的偏离。所得功率谱可作为 DESI、EUCLID、4MOST 和 PFS 等当前及未来星系巡天任务检验引力的可观测预示。

Abstract: In this paper we study cosmological perturbations with $f(R)$ gravity scalaron. We consider epoch of transition from early general relativity (GR) phase to late time non-GR phase of cosmogenic history for a viable $f(R)$ gravity Lagrangian close to the $Λ$CDM theory at early cosmic history. We study deviation in matter power spectra from $Λ$CDM scenario. Galaxy power spectra multipoles are generated using galaxy bias, velocity dispersion and modified gravity parameters. While monopole and quadrupole matter power in $f(R)$ theory increase towards larger $k$ (small scales), quadrupole power spectrum remains elevated relative to $Λ$CDM for smaller $k$ (large scales), upto $k\approx 0.02$. These power spectra provide observables for testing gravity through the current and future galaxy survey missions such as DESI, EUCLID, 4MOST and PFS. We report appropriate GR limit of scalaron mass in galactic and massive black hole scales. Evolution of the scalaron mass and its general relativistic limit for various cosmic structures are reported. Deviation from GR in cosmogenic evolution is attributed to decrease in scalaron mass with cosmic time.

</details>


### [103] [CMB Acoustic Power Spectra in STVG-MOG](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20231)
*John W. Moffat*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种标量-张量-矢量引力（STVG-MOG）的宇宙学实现，其中重组前的标量扰动动力学与ΛCDM模型简并，且无需引入粒子暗物质。通过让非相对论性的STVG矢量场激发充当有效尘埃组分，并在声学峰相关傅里叶尺度上保持有效引力耦合近似为牛顿引力常数，该模型能再现标准宇宙学模型的温度与偏振功率谱，从而由引力场自由度承担粒子暗物质的动力学角色。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在不引入粒子暗物质的前提下，探索是否能够通过引力理论本身的修正（STVG-MOG）来实现与ΛCDM模型在早期宇宙扰动动力学上的简并性，从而为暗物质现象提供另一种理论解释。

Method: 利用STVG-MOG理论中的有质量矢量场φ_μ，将其非相对论性激发作为零声速、无碰撞、密度正比于a^{-3}的尘埃组分；通过分析有效引力耦合G_eff(k,a)在声学峰尺度上近似等于牛顿引力常数G_N，使重子-光子振荡的度规势演化与标准模型一致；使用玻尔兹曼编码CLASS进行数值拟合。

Result: 在重组前的声学峰相关傅里叶尺度上，有效引力耦合G_eff≃G_N，引力势在视界进入时足够深，可维持第三个声学峰（对尘埃组分最敏感的指标）的观测高度；温度与极化功率谱可与标准ΛCDM预测一致。

Conclusion: STVG-MOG中的矢量场尘埃在早期宇宙中与冷暗物质动力学简并，但并非等同于粒子暗物质流体；该框架表明暗物质的动力学角色可由引力场自身的自由度承担。

Abstract: We present a cosmological realization of Scalar--Tensor--Vector Gravity (STVG--MOG) in which the pre-recombination scalar perturbation dynamics become degenerate with those of $Λ$CDM without invoking particle dark matter. In the early universe, nonrelativistic excitations of the massive STVG vector field $φ_μ$ behave as a collisionless, pressureless component with vanishing sound speed and background density $ρ_φ\propto a^{-3}$. On the Fourier scales relevant for the acoustic peaks, the effective gravitational coupling satisfies $G_{\rm eff}(k,a)\simeq G_N$, so that the metric potentials governing baryon--photon oscillations evolve in the same way as in the standard cosmological model. The gravitational wells remain sufficiently deep at horizon entry to preserve the observed height of the third acoustic peak, the most sensitive indicator of a clustering pressureless component prior to recombination. Since Thomson scattering, recombination, baryon loading, and photon diffusion are unchanged, the temperature and polarization spectra can coincide with the standard $Λ$CDM predictions once the vector sector supplies the effective dust component. In this framework, the dynamical role usually attributed to cold dark matter is carried instead by a degree of freedom belonging to the gravitational sector itself. We explain why this vector-sector dust, although dynamically degenerate with cold dark matter in the early universe, is not equivalent to a particle dark matter fluid. The Boltzmann code CLASS is used to obtain a MOG fit to the acoustical power spectrum data.

</details>


### [104] [Probing late-time deviations from $Λ$CDM with a quadratic dark energy expansion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20748)
*Sehjal Khandelwal,Abraão J. S. Capistrano,Suresh Kumar,Rafael C. Nunes*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究了一种二次暗能量膨胀（QDEE）模型作为标准ΛCDM宇宙学框架的现象学扩展，利用普朗克2018、ACT DR6、SPT-3G、DESI DR2和Pantheon Plus等多种宇宙学数据集对其进行约束，发现该模型在缓解哈勃常数张力的同时与早期宇宙约束保持一致，贝叶斯模型比较支持该模型优于标准ΛCDM。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准ΛCDM模型中暗能量为严格常数，但该假设在解释哈勃常数张力（Hubble tension）等观测异常时面临挑战。本研究旨在通过引入二次暗能量膨胀模型（quadratic dark energy expansion, QDEE）提供更灵活的描述，从而检验其能否在保持早期宇宙行为不变的前提下缓解现有观测矛盾。

Method: 采用二次暗能量膨胀（QDEE）模型，引入额外自由度以实现晚期暗能量成分偏离常数的温和演化。利用联合数据集进行贝叶斯参数约束（Bayesian parameter constraints），数据集包括Planck 2018 CMB、ACT DR6、SPT-3G、DESI DR2以及Pantheon Plus Ia型超新星样本，并通过贝叶斯模型比较（Bayesian model comparison）和后验预测检验（posterior predictive checks）评估模型性能。

Result: QDEE模型将推断的哈勃常数（Hubble constant）向更高值偏移，部分缓解了与局域测量之间的哈勃常数张力，且与早期宇宙约束不冲突。多种数据集组合下的贝叶斯模型比较显示支持QDEE模型的强证据。后验预测检验表明模型预测与观测数据在统计不确定性内一致。

Conclusion: QDEE模型作为ΛCDM的现象学扩展具有观测可行性，能够在缓解哈勃常数张力的同时保持与现有宇宙学数据的兼容性。贝叶斯模型比较结果强烈支持该框架优于标准ΛCDM。

Abstract: We investigate the observational viability of a quadratic dark energy expansion (QDEE) model as a phenomenological extension of the standard $Λ\mathrm{CDM}$ cosmological framework. This approach introduces the additional degrees of freedom that permit mild late-time deviations from a constant dark-energy component while preserving the standard early-Universe behavior. We constrain the model using a comprehensive combination of cosmological datasets, including Planck 2018 cosmic microwave background (CMB) measurements, Atacama Cosmology Telescope (ACT) Data Release 6 (DR6) and South Pole Telescope (SPT-3G) data, Dark Energy Spectroscopic Instrument (DESI) Data Release 2 (DR2), and the Pantheon Plus type Ia supernova compilation. Our results show that the QDEE framework shifts the inferred Hubble constant toward higher values relative to $Λ\mathrm{CDM}$, partially alleviating the tension with local measurements while remaining consistent with early-Universe constraints. Bayesian model comparison indicates strong evidence in favor of this framework over standard $Λ\mathrm{CDM}$ across multiple dataset combinations. Posterior predictive checks further demonstrate that the model yields predictions consistent with the observed data within statistical uncertainties.

</details>

### [105] [Study of the thermodynamic properties of hot QCD matter with the CMS experiment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21052)
*Cesar A. Bernardes*

Main category: nucl-ex

TL;DR: 该论文基于CMS在LHC上的实验测量，通过超中心铅铅（PbPb）碰撞中平均横动量对多重数的依赖关系，提取了极端温度下强相互作用物质的声速平方（$c_s^2$），结果为$c_s^2 = 0.241 \pm 0.002\, (\mathrm{stat}) \pm 0.016\, (\mathrm{syst})$，与格点量子色动力学（lattice-QCD）计算结果吻合；同时也在质子铅（pPb）碰撞中开展了补充研究，以探索小系统内可能的夸克-胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma）信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究极端温度下强相互作用物质的属性，特别是其声速平方（$c_s^2$），是理解量子色动力学（quantum chromodynamics, QCD）相图及夸克-胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma, QGP）性质的关键。该工作旨在通过LHC实验数据检验格点QCD（lattice-QCD）理论预言，并探究小碰撞系统中是否存在QGP信号。

Method: 利用CMS探测器在$\sqrt{s_{\mathrm{NN}}} = 5.02\ \mathrm{TeV}$的超中心铅铅（PbPb）碰撞中，分析平均横动量对多重数的依赖关系，从中提取声速平方（$c_s^2$）。此外，还在质子铅（pPb）碰撞中进行了类似的补充测量，以对比研究小系统行为。

Result: 在有效温度$T_{\mathrm{eff}} = 219 \pm 8\, (\mathrm{syst})\,\mathrm{MeV}$下，测得声速平方$c_s^2 = 0.241 \pm 0.002\, (\mathrm{stat}) \pm 0.016\, (\mathrm{syst})$。该结果与格点量子色动力学（lattice-QCD）计算在误差范围内一致。

Conclusion: CMS实验测量提供了极端温度下强相互作用物质声速平方（$c_s^2$）的实验约束，验证了格点QCD（lattice-QCD）理论预言。质子铅（pPb）碰撞的补充分析为进一步探索小系统中的夸克-胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma, QGP）信号提供了基础。

Abstract: These proceedings summarize recent CMS measurements at the LHC that extract the squared speed of sound, $c_s^2$, of strongly interacting matter at extreme temperatures from the multiplicity dependence of the mean transverse momentum in ultra-central lead-lead (PbPb) collisions at $\sqrt{s_{\mathrm{NN}}} = 5.02\ \mathrm{TeV}$. The analysis yields $c_s^2 = 0.241 \pm 0.002\, (\mathrm{stat}) \pm 0.016\, (\mathrm{syst})$ at an effective temperature of $T_{\mathrm{eff}} = 219 \pm 8\, (\mathrm{syst})\,\mathrm{MeV}$, in good agreement with lattice-QCD calculations. Complementary studies in proton-lead (pPb) collisions are also presented to investigate possible quark-gluon plasma signatures in smaller systems.

</details>

### [106] [An AI-driven robotic system for two-dimensional hetero-assemblies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20420)
*Xiaoxi Li,Jinkun He,Haojie Liu,Xipeng Liu,Zewen Wu,Jing Li,Kai Zhao,Shan Li,Xingdan Sun,Xiaoxue Fan,Zhiren Xiong,Xingguang Wu,Xuanzhe Sha,Zhili Lin,Caixia Yang,Luosha Han,Jie Xu,Woye Pei,Kaining Yang,Jing Zhang,Xiaolong Feng,Tongyao Zhang,Zhu Liang,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Ming Tian,Neng Wan,Jing Zhang,Jianming Lu,Wenjing Hong,Zheng Vitto Han*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一套智能自动化系统，用于按需堆叠二维范德华（vdW）层状纳米材料，并通过强化学习持续优化性能。作者以扭转双层石墨烯（TBLG）为例，展示了该系统在魔角附近制备非常规超导体的能力，有望推动低维纳米材料的高通量制备与新物理现象的发现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前纳米材料堆叠组装（如旋转组装的二维范德华层状化合物）仍依赖低效的手工操作，限制了其在量子模拟和奇特电子相探索中的应用。因此，亟需一种高精度、自动化的堆叠技术，以实现二维扭转电子学异质结（twistronic heterostructures）的可扩展制备。

Method: 该系统遵循剥离二维材料干法转移的最先进协议，实现范德华堆叠的自动化。同时，系统利用每次自动化堆叠过程生成的元数据（metadata），进行强化学习（reinforcement learning），从而持续提升自身性能。

Result: 成功制备了制备难度较高的扭转双层石墨烯（twisted bilayer graphene, TBLG），并在魔角（magic angle）附近观测到了非常规超导电性（unconventional superconductivity）。

Conclusion: 该工作为包括扭转电子学异质结在内的低维纳米材料的高通量制备铺平了道路，表明将数据挖掘（data mining）与人工智能（AI）相结合，可以加速新颖物理现象的发现。

Abstract: Nanomaterials stacked on-demand, such as rotationally assembled two-dimensional (2D) van der Waals (vdW) layered compounds, provides a versatile platform for quantum simulation and the exploration of exotic electronic phases. Currently, however, such nanoassemblies remain largely confined to inefficiency, manually operated process, limiting their potential for probing emergent physical phenomena. There is a pressing need in the field for high-precision, automated assembling techniques, especially for the scalable fabrication of 2D twistronic heterostructures. Here, we present an intelligent automation system dedicated to the fabrication of van der Waals stacks, following the state-of-the-art protocol for dry transfer of exfoliated 2D materials. The system further employs metadata generated from each automated stacking procedure to perform reinforcement learning, thereby continuously bettering its performances. As a concrete demonstration, we fabricate twisted bilayer graphene (TBLG) -- known for its challenging preparation -- and exhibit its unconventional superconductivity near the magic angle. Our work may pave the way for high-throughput fabrication of low-dimensional nanomaterials including twistronic heterostructures, where integrating data mining and artificial intelligence can accelerate the discovery of novel physical phenomena.

</details>


### [107] [Fröhlich-type Polarons in Isotopically Enriched Hexagonal Boron Nitride](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20428)
*Ioannis Chatzakis,Timur Abdilov,Elliot Walker,Jaime Freitas,Song Liu,James H. Edgar*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过低温阴极发光（cathodoluminescence）定量揭示了硼-10同位素富集的六方氮化硼（hBN）中的Fröhlich型激子-声子耦合，获得了Fröhlich耦合常数α=0.159、激子结合能161 meV、极化子结合能~48 meV及有效质量1.045 m₀等关键参数，并指出同位素富集导致结合能增大，表现为大极化子行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 激子-声子相互作用在决定六方氮化硼（hexagonal boron nitride，hBN）的光学响应中起核心作用，但其定量测定一直不完整，因此需要精确表征该耦合强度及相关物理参数。

Method: 利用低温阴极发光（cathodoluminescence）技术，对硼-10同位素富集的hBN样品进行测量，解析间接激子（indirect exciton）能级（5.95±0.02 eV）及其纵向光学（longitudinal optical，LO）声子复制峰（detuned by 184±56 meV），并基于这些光谱特征提取耦合常数和激子/极化子参数。

Result: 获得了Fröhlich耦合常数α=0.159；激子结合能（exciton binding energy）为161 meV，高于自然丰度hBN的报道值；极化子半径（polaron radius）超过晶格常数，表现为大极化子（large-polaron）行为；激子散射时间（exciton scattering time）约97 fs，对应均匀线宽（homogeneous linewidth）约6.76 meV；极化子结合能（polaron binding energy）约48 meV，有效质量（effective mass）为1.045 m₀。

Conclusion: 该结果直接定量表征了同位素工程化hBN中的激子-声子耦合，为调控其声子极化激元（phonon-polaritonic）和量子光学（quantum-optical）性质建立了基础。

Abstract: Exciton-phonon interactions play a central role in defining the optical response of hexagonal boron nitride (hBN), yet their quantitative determination has remained incomplete. Here, we reveal the Fröhlich-type exciton-phonon coupling in boron-10-enriched hBN using low-temperature cathodoluminescence. We resolve the indirect exciton 5.95$\pm$0.02 eV together with its longitudinal optical (LO) phonon replica detuned by 184$\pm$56 meV, enabling the extraction of a Fröhlich coupling constant $α$=0.159 and a larger exciton binding energy of 161 meV, larger than previously reported values for natural-abundance hBN, which is attributed to isotope enrichment. The inferred polaron radius exceeds the lattice constant, indicating large-polaron behavior. We deduced an exciton scattering time ~of 97 fs, corresponding to a homogeneous linewidth of ~6.76 meV. We further obtain a polaron binding energy of ~48 meV and an effective mass of 1.045 $m_0$. These results provide a direct quantitative characterization of exciton-phonon coupling in isotopically engineered hBN and establish a foundation for tailoring its phonon-polaritonic and quantum-optical properties.

</details>


### [108] [Excitation-Energy-Selective Control of Hot-Carrier Cooling via a Resonant Optical-Phonon Bottleneck in Graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20430)
*Sachin Sharm,Elliott Walker,Rachael Myers-Ward,Jenifer Hajzus,Yijing Liu,Paola Barbara,Ioannis Chatzakis*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文利用中红外泵浦和太赫兹探针实验，发现单层与双层石墨烯中载流子弛豫时间对激发光子能量存在显著的非单调依赖关系。在0.42–0.48 eV的窄光谱窗口内，载流子寿命因光学声子（optical phonon）寿命的共振增强而延长一个数量级，该现象被统一载流子-声子能量平衡框架所描述，揭示了激发能量选择性调控热载流子弛豫的机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解并控制石墨烯中的热载流子弛豫（hot-carrier relaxation）对于发展超快光电子学（ultrafast optoelectronics）和太赫兹技术（terahertz technologies）至关重要，但此前对激发光子能量如何影响弛豫动力学的认识尚不完全。

Method: 采用中红外泵浦脉冲（mid-infrared pump pulses，能量范围0.22–0.73 eV）激发样品，并利用太赫兹探针脉冲（terahertz probe pulses）探测单层与双层石墨烯中的载流子冷却动力学（carrier cooling dynamics）。

Result: 发现载流子弛豫时间对激发光子能量呈现显著且可复现的非单调依赖关系；在0.42至0.48 eV的窄光谱窗口内，载流子寿命比其他能量下观测到的皮秒量级冷却时间增加了一个数量级。该异常减缓源于光学声子寿命的共振增强（resonant enhancement），导致热光学声子积累与再吸收，从而抑制了能量向晶格（lattice）的传递。

Conclusion: 所有观测行为均可通过统一的载流子-声子能量平衡框架（carrier-phonon energy-balance framework）描述，其中有效光学声子衰变路径随激发能量的变化主导冷却动力学。这些发现证明了激发能量选择性调控石墨烯中热载流子弛豫的可行性，并为光学声子瓶颈（optical-phonon bottleneck）附近的非平衡载流子-声子相互作用提供了新见解。

Abstract: Understanding and controlling hot-carrier relaxation in graphene is crucial for advancing ultrafast optoelectronic and terahertz technologies. Here, we investigate carrier cooling dynamics in monolayer and bilayer graphene using mid-infrared pump pulses (0.22-0.73 eV) and terahertz probe pulses. We uncover a pronounced, reproducible, and non-monotonic dependence of the carrier relaxation time on excitation photon energy. Remarkably, within a narrow spectral window (0.42 to 0.48 eV), the carrier lifetime increases by an order of magnitude compared to a few picosecond-scale cooling observed at other energies. We show that this anomalous slowdown originates from a resonant enhancement of the optical-phonon lifetime, causing accumulation and reabsorption of hot optical phonons that suppress energy transfer to the lattice. All observed behaviors are captured within a unified carrier-phonon energy-balance framework, where excitation-energy-dependent variations of the effective optical-phonon decay pathway govern the cooling dynamics. These findings demonstrate excitation-energy-selective control of hot-carrier relaxation in graphene and provide new insight into non-equilibrium carrier-phonon interactions near the optical-phonon bottleneck.

### [109] [Coexisting Ballistic and Diffusive Heat Transport in Micrometer-Scale Molecular Junctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20517)
*P. M. Martinez,O. Mateos-Lopez,J. C. Cuevas,J. G. Vilhena*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过金-烷烃-金单分子结的原子模拟，发现玻尔兹曼输运理论（Boltzmann transport theory）对热导率（thermal conductivity）的预测在真实分子系统中失效：热导率在长达微米尺度上永不收敛，低频率声学模式（acoustic modes）因动量守恒而保持弹道输运（ballistic transport），导致热导率呈现$L^{1/3}$发散，符合Kardar-Parisi-Zhang普适类（universality class）的标度律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准的热导率预测框架——玻尔兹曼输运理论假定所有振动模式（vibrational mode）最终都会散射并产生有限寿命，从而得到收敛且与长度无关的热导率（即傅里叶定律）。本文旨在检验这一假设在真实分子系统中的有效性。

Method: 对金-烷烃-金单分子结（Au-alkane-Au single-molecule junctions）进行原子模拟（atomistic simulations），系统长度跨越五个数量级（0.5纳米至4微米）。通过频率分辨的热流分解（frequency-resolved decomposition of the heat current）分析热输运机制。

Result: 热导率从未收敛：室温下弹道输运可持续至一百纳米，超出此前单分子测量近两个数量级；此后热导率呈$L^{1/3}$发散。低频率声学模式从未热化，在任何链长下均保持弹道输运，在$L = 2~μ$m时仍携带50%的总热流。其他模式随长度增加从离散振动态合并为有散射活性的声子带（phonon bands）而发生集体热化。

Conclusion: 发散的热导率源于永久弹道输运与正常扩散输运这两个共存区域之间的边界：随着长度$L$增长，散射起始频率逐渐向低频移动，以维持$L^{1/3}$发散的速率抑制弹道通道，在每个长度下都留下有限贡献。这种在抽象一维晶格模型中预言的弹道与扩散输运的共存现象，在真实微米尺度结的结构与化学复杂性中依然存在。

Abstract: Boltzmann transport theory, the standard framework for predicting thermal conductivity, assumes that every vibrational mode eventually scatters, acquiring a finite lifetime that yields a convergent, length-independent thermal conductivity: Fourier's law. Here we show that this assumption fails in a real molecular system. Through atomistic simulations of Au-alkane-Au single-molecule junctions spanning five orders of magnitude in length (0.5~nm to 4~$μ$m), we find that thermal conductivity never converges. Transport is ballistic for up to one hundred nanometers at room temperature, extending nearly two orders of magnitude beyond existing single-molecule measurements. Past this window, conductivity diverges as $L^{1/3}$, the scaling predicted by the Kardar-Parisi-Zhang universality class for momentum-conserving systems. Frequency-resolved decomposition of the heat current reveals the mechanism behind the divergence. Low-frequency acoustic modes never thermalize: protected by momentum conservation, they remain ballistic at every chain length, still carrying 50\% of the total heat current at $L = 2~μ$m. All other modes thermalize collectively as discrete vibrational states merge into scattering-active phonon bands with increasing length. Hence, the diverging conductivity emerges from the boundary between these coexisting transport regimes: as $L$ grows, the onset of scattering shifts progressively toward lower frequencies, suppressing the ballistic channel at a rate that sustains the $L^{1/3}$ divergence, leaving a finite contribution at every length. This coexistence of permanent ballistic and well-behaved diffusive transport, anticipated in abstract one-dimensional lattice models, survives the structural and chemical complexity of real micrometer-sized junctions.

</details>


### [110] [Field-tunable spin-valley transport in monolayer MoS$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20790)
*Kamal Azaidaoui,Hocine Bahlouli,Clarence Cortes,David Laroze,Ahmed Jellal*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文从包含自旋-轨道耦合的狄拉克哈密顿量出发，利用高频Floquet展开获得激光重正化的有效静态模型，系统研究了单层MoS₂中通过静电势垒和椭圆极化光场调控的自旋-谷（spin-valley）输运特性，发现通过调节激光强度和极化形状可实现宽带谷滤波与共振选择性操作之间的切换。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在单层MoS₂中利用外部光场（椭圆极化辐照）和静电势垒对自旋-谷（spin-valley）输运进行可调控的场控，以期实现可光重构的谷电子学（valleytronic）和自旋电子学（spintronic）功能。

Method: 采用包含内禀自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）的大质量狄拉克哈密顿量（massive Dirac Hamiltonian），通过高频Floquet展开（high-frequency Floquet expansion）得到激光重正化质量项（laser-renormalized mass term）的有效静态模型；利用旋量匹配（spinor matching）求解散射问题，推导出透射率的精确解析表达式。

Result: 数值结果显示，激光驱动可以调控势垒内的自旋-谷依赖的传播阈值和法布里-珀罗相位（Fabry-Pérot phase），从而产生可控的通带/阻带（pass/stop bands）；通过改变激光强度和极化形状，同一结可在宽带谷滤波（broadband valley filtering）和共振选择性操作之间切换，且谷对比度（valley contrast）在朗道电导（Landauer conductance）中仍然可见。

Conclusion: 研究建立了一种在MoS₂中实现可光重构的谷电子学和自旋电子学功能的有效路径。

Abstract: We study field-controlled spin-valley transport in monolayer MoS$_2$ through a single electrostatic barrier and a uniform off-resonant elliptically polarized irradiation. Starting from the massive Dirac Hamiltonian with intrinsic spin-orbit coupling, we use a high-frequency Floquet expansion to obtain an effective static model with a laser-renormalized mass (gap) term. We solve the scattering problem by spinor matching and derive the exact analytic expression for the transmission. The numerical results show that the drive tunes both the spin-valley-dependent propagation threshold inside the barrier and the Fabry-Pérot phase, creating controllable pass/stop bands. By varying both the laser intensity (amplitude) and the polarization shape, we show that the same junction can be switched between broadband valley filtering and resonance-selective operation, and the valley contrast remains visible in the Landauer conductance. Our findings establish an efficient route for realizing optically reconfigurable valleytronic and spintronic functionalities in MoS$_2$.

### [111] [Probing topological phase transitions via nonlinear Hall response in strained moiré dice lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21229)
*Gourab Paul,Srijata Lahiri,Bilal Tanatar,Saurabh Basu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文证明，在考虑双谷（valley）对称性的扭曲双层骰子晶格（twisted bilayer dice lattice）中，施加单轴应变（uniaxial strain）可引发非线性霍尔效应（nonlinear Hall effect），该效应可作为探测拓扑相变（topological phase transition）的探针，尤其适用于远离电荷中性点（charge neutrality）的能谷极化拓扑平坦带（valley polarized topological flat bands）。非线性反常霍尔信号在拓扑相边界处发生符号反转，并在手征对称性（chiral symmetry）破缺时显著增强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扭曲双层骰子晶格在远离电荷中性点处存在拓扑非平庸的平坦带，但由于时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry）在考虑双谷时被恢复，基于贝里曲率（Berry curvature）探测能谷特定拓扑相的方法受到严重阻碍。本文旨在寻找一种可探测此类拓扑相变的有效探针。

Method: 在扭曲双层骰子晶格上施加单轴应变，通过计算贝里曲率偶极子（Berry curvature dipole）得到非线性反常霍尔响应，分析其随载流子密度（carrier density）和交错质量（staggered mass）的变化，并分别在手征极限（chiral limit）和手征对称性破缺（broken chiral symmetry）条件下进行研究。

Result: 非线性反常霍尔信号在拓扑相边界处发生符号反转，可标记与中间子带下边缘特定能量态相关的拓扑相变。在手征对称性破缺区域，非线性霍尔效应显著增强。

Conclusion: 非线性霍尔效应可作为探测能谷极化系统中拓扑相变的有效探针，尤其在时间反演对称性恢复导致贝里曲率整体检测失效时，该效应提供了替代方案。

Abstract: Valley polarized twisted bilayer dice lattice hosts topologically nontrivial flat bands far from charge neutrality due to broken time reversal symmetry, whereas the ones in the vicinity of it remain topologically trivial. However, when both valleys are taken into consideration, the time reversal symmetry is preserved, which poses a serious hindrance to enumerate the valley specific topological phases that rely on the detection of the Berry curvature. In this work, we demonstrate that such a twisted structure with an applied uniaxial strain exhibits a nonlinear Hall effect far from charge neutrality. We ascertain that the nonlinear anomalous Hall signals can serve as a probe for topological phase transitions associated with a specific energy state that is constrained to reside at the lower edge of the middle subband and controlled via a staggered mass. Specifically, we show that the nonlinear anomalous Hall response undergoes a sign reversal across the topological phase boundaries. By tuning the carrier density, we compute the nonlinear Hall response obtained from the Berry curvature dipole, both in the chiral limit, and also when the chiral symmetry is broken. It is further seen that the nonlinear Hall effect is significantly enhanced in the broken chiral symmetry regime.

### [112] [Destructive interference of second harmonic generation in AA stacked MoTe$_2$/WSe$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21231)
*Yiduo Wang,Yao Lu,Changshen Chen,Xiaotong Liao,Siyu Fan,Zhenyu Wang,Yaotian Liu,Subi Du,Yingze Jia,Ye Zhu,Yingwei Wang,Jun He,Song Liu,Jiawei Ruan,Zhen Chen,Kai-Qiang Lin,Yang Xu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过原子级成像和激子杂化测量两种独立探针，报告了在近乎0°堆叠（AA堆叠）的MoTe₂/WSe₂异质双层中观测到的反常破坏性二次谐波干涉现象，并利用GW和Bethe-Salpeter方程计算揭示了WSe₂ C激子与MoTe₂ D激子不同的双光子共振导致二阶非线性磁化率χ⁽²⁾产生近π相位差（Δφ）的物理机制。进一步展示了在小角度扭转MoTe₂/WSe₂中，SHG偏振态由扭转角α和相位差Δφ共同决定，并可在庞加莱球上映射出轨迹，在满足Δφ + 3α = 180°的激发能量下实现了近圆偏振SHG输出和几何偏振奇点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统认知认为，在过渡金属硫族化物（TMDC）双层中，0°堆叠由于层分辨非线性极化相长干涉应增强二次谐波（SHG），而60°堆叠则因相消干涉抑制SHG。本文旨在探究这一常规预期是否在异质双层中依然成立，并揭示可能存在的非常规干涉机制。

Method: 采用原子级分辨率成像和堆叠敏感激子杂化测量两种独立探针进行实验观测，并结合从头算GW方法和Bethe-Salpeter方程（Betth-Salpeter equation）进行理论计算，分析双层中不同激子共振对二阶非线性磁化率χ⁽²⁾相位的影响。

Result: 在近乎0°堆叠（AA堆叠）的MoTe₂/WSe₂异质双层中观测到反常破坏性SHG干涉；WSe₂ C激子和MoTe₂ D激子的双光子共振导致χ⁽²⁾之间产生近π相位差（Δφ）；小角度扭转下SHG偏振态由扭转角α和Δφ共同决定，在Δφ + 3α = 180°时输出近圆偏振光（椭圆率约0.91）并发生90°方位角突变，对应参数空间中的几何偏振奇点。

Conclusion: 该发现打破了传统对0°堆叠增强SHG的简单预期，揭示了激子共振诱导的相位差在调控非线性光学响应中的关键作用，为激子共振工程化的非线性光子学以及莫尔材料中堆叠分辨光学功能开发提供了新途径。

Abstract: The stacking configuration of two-dimensional materials critically governs their optical and electronic responses. Monolayer transition-metal dichalcogenides (TMDC) lack inversion symmetry and exhibit exciton-enhanced second-harmonic generation (SHG). In TMDC bilayers, 60° (0°) stacking is conventionally expected to suppress (enhance) SHG owing to destructive (constructive) interference of the layer-resolved nonlinear polarizations. Here, we report an unconventional destructive SHG interference in nearly 0°-stacked (AA-stacked) MoTe2/WSe2 heterobilayers using two independent probes: atomic-resolution imaging and stacking-sensitive exciton hybridization measurements. Supported by ab initio GW and Bethe-Salpeter equation calculations, we show that distinct two-photon resonances associated with the WSe2 C exciton and the MoTe2 D exciton generate a nearly $π$ phase difference ($Δφ$) in their second-order nonlinear susceptibilities $χ^{(2)}$, leading to the anomalous destructive interference. We further demonstrate that in small-angle twisted MoTe2/WSe2, the SHG polarization state is governed by the interplay between twist angle $α$ and phase difference $Δφ$, and can be mapped onto trajectories on the Poincaré sphere. At excitation energies satisfying $Δφ$ + 3$α$ = 180°, the SHG output becomes nearly circularly polarized (ellipticity ~ 0.91) and undergoes an abrupt 90° azimuthal rotation, corresponding to a geometric polarization singularity in the parameter space. Our findings open new routes for exciton-resonance engineered nonlinear photonics and stacking-resolved optical functionality in moiré materials.

### [113] [Stacking-order-dependent electronic properties of MoTe2/WSe2 moiré bilayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21233)
*Zhongdong Han,Wenjin Zhao,Eegene Clara Chung,Chia-Hao Lee,Zui Tao,Zhengchao Xia,Yichi Zhang,Yiyu Xia,Jekwan Lee,Bowen Shen,Ariana Ray,Yu-Tsun Shao,Tingxin Li,Shengwei Jiang,Yihang Zeng,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,David Muller,Kin Fai Mak,Jie Shan*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过扫描透射电子显微镜（STEM）校准了MoTe₂/WSe₂莫尔双层中光学二次谐波产生（SHG）对堆叠次序的标定，直接比较了两种不同堆叠次序下的输运、磁性及电子相图，澄清了此前关于陈绝缘体、金属-绝缘体相变及近藤晶格物理解释的争议，建立了堆叠次序与电子性质之间的一致图像。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 过渡金属二硫族化物（TMD）莫尔双层中，层间堆叠次序（interlayer stacking order）对强关联和拓扑物性敏感，但最常用的偏振分辨光学二次谐波产生（SHG）表征方法在大多数异质双层中尚未经实验验证，存在标定不明确的问题，导致相关物理解释存在争议。

Method: 对角度对齐的MoTe₂/WSe₂双层同时进行偏振分辨光学SHG测量与扫描透射电子显微镜（STEM）成像，将SHG信号与原子级堆叠结构直接对照，完成标定；在此基础上，系统比较两种不同堆叠次序下的输运性质、磁性行为及电子相图。

Result: 成功校准了MoTe₂/WSe₂中SHG对堆叠次序的指认；基于校准后的堆叠归属，澄清了此前研究中关于陈绝缘体（Chern insulator）的本性、半满填充时电场调控的金属-绝缘体相变（metal-insulator transition）机制以及近藤晶格（Kondo lattice）物理解释中存在的歧义。

Conclusion: 该工作为MoTe₂/WSe₂莫尔双层中堆叠次序与电子性质之间的关系提供了一致且自洽的解释框架，表明经STEM校准的SHG是可靠的表征手段，对理解TMD莫尔体系中堆叠依赖的强关联与拓扑物性具有重要意义。

Abstract: Transition metal dichalcogenide (TMD) moiré bilayers have realized a wide range of strongly correlated and topological phenomena. The physics in these materials is often sensitive to the interlayer stacking order. Polarization-resolved optical second harmonic generation (SHG) is the most used technique for stacking order characterization but unverified for most heterobilayers. Here we calibrate the optical SHG for angle-aligned MoTe2/WSe2 bilayers by the scanning transmission electron microscopy (STEM). We directly compare the transport and magnetic properties and the electronic phase diagram for two distinct stacking orders. With the calibrated stacking order assignment, we clarify the interpretation of earlier results, including the nature of the Chern insulator, mechanism of an electric-field-tuned metal-insulator transition at half band filling, and the Kondo lattice physics. Our work provides a consistent picture of the relation between the stacking order and the electronic properties of MoTe2/WSe2 moiré bilayers.

</details>


### [114] [Designer Quantum States in Magnetic Topological Insulator Multilayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21287)
*Deyi Zhuo,Han Tay,Cui-Zu Chang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文综述了过去十年通过分子束外延（molecular beam epitaxy, MBE）生长磁性拓扑绝缘体（topological insulator, TI）多层膜的实验进展，展示了如何将磁性掺杂与非掺杂TI层作为“拓扑乐高”单元，通过调控层厚、磁性掺杂、异质结构架构和堆叠顺序，在原子层精度上控制磁交换能隙、层间耦合和拓扑陈数（Chern number, C），进而实现从量子反常霍尔效应（quantum anomalous Hall, QAH）到轴子绝缘体（axion insulator）和半整数奇偶反常（C = 1/2 parity anomaly）态等多种量子态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁性拓扑绝缘体为工程化拓扑与磁性相互作用的量子态提供了高度可调的平台，有必要系统总结过去十年中基于分子束外延（MBE）生长磁性拓扑绝缘体（TI）多层膜的实验进展，以阐明层厚、磁性掺杂、异质结构架构及堆叠顺序等参数对量子态调控的作用。

Method: 将磁性掺杂与非掺杂拓扑绝缘体（TI）层视为“拓扑乐高”构建单元，通过分子束外延（MBE）方法生长多层膜，系统调控层厚度、磁性掺杂浓度、异质结构架构及堆叠顺序，实现对磁交换能隙、层间耦合及陈数（C）的原子层精度控制。

Result: 2013年实现了均匀Cr掺杂(Bi,Sb)2Te3薄膜的C=1量子反常霍尔（QAH）效应，2015年实现了均匀V掺杂薄膜的同类效应；进一步通过Cr掺杂与非掺杂(Bi,Sb)2Te3层组合，在磁性调制掺杂三层膜中实现C=1 QAH效应并将其拓展至三维（three-dimensional, 3D）体系；还发展了高陈数QAH态、工程化平台相变、介观QAH器件及手性边缘电流的电学开关；最终在非对称磁性TI三层膜中实现了轴子绝缘体（axion insulator）和C=1/2奇偶反常（parity anomaly）态。

Conclusion: 磁性拓扑绝缘体（TI）多层膜已成为一种通用的材料平台，可用于创造包括合成外尔半金属（synthetic Weyl semimetal）和量子反常霍尔（QAH）金属相在内的新型设计量子态，并可用于探测厚轴子绝缘体（axion insulator）和三维（3D）QAH绝缘体中的拓扑磁电效应（topological magnetoelectric effect）。

Abstract: Magnetic topological insulators (TIs) provide a highly tunable platform for engineering quantum states that emerge from the interplay between topology and magnetism. In this review article, we summarize experimental progress over the past decade in designing magnetic TI multilayers by molecular beam epitaxy (MBE). By treating magnetically doped and undoped TI layers as topological Legos, we discuss how layer thickness, magnetic doping, heterostructure architecture, and stacking sequence can be used to control magnetic exchange gaps, interlayer coupling, and the Chern number C with atomic-layer precision. We first briefly review the realization of the C = 1 quantum anomalous Hall (QAH) effect in uniformly Cr-doped (Bi,Sb)2Te3 films in 2013 and uniformly V-doped (Bi,Sb)2Te3 films in 2015. We then discuss how Cr-doped and undoped (Bi,Sb)2Te3 layers can be combined to realize the C = 1 QAH effect in magnetically modulation-doped trilayers, including its extension into the three-dimensional (3D) regime. Next, we review the development of high-C QAH states, engineered plateau phase transitions, mesoscopic QAH devices, and electrical switching of chiral edge-current chirality. Finally, we discuss the realizations of axion insulator and C = 1/2 parity anomaly states in asymmetric magnetic TI trilayers. These advances establish magnetic TI multilayers as a versatile materials platform for creating new designer quantum states, including synthetic Weyl semimetal and QAH metal phases, and for probing the topological magnetoelectric effect in thick axion insulators and 3D QAH insulators.

### [115] [Huge ultrafast spin Seebeck effect mediated by laser-excited superdiffusive magnon currents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21389)
*Luca Mikadze,Peter M. Oppeneer,Markus Weißenhofer*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个基于第一性原理参数化的微观理论框架，通过量子玻尔兹曼方程（quantum Boltzmann equation）描述非热磁子（nonthermal magnon）的散射与输运，成功模拟了bcc Fe薄膜中超快激光诱导退磁过程，预测了超快自旋塞贝克效应（ultrafast spin Seebeck effect）和超扩散输运（superdiffusive transport）行为，并计算了可实验观测的磁光克尔角（magneto-optical Kerr angle）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的理论方法，如三温度模型（three-temperature model）和扩散方程（diffusion equations），难以准确描述亚皮秒时间尺度上电子、声子和磁子之间强非平衡态（nonequilibrium）的散射与输运过程。

Method: 基于第一性原理（ab initio）参数化构建微观理论框架，通过量子玻尔兹曼方程（quantum Boltzmann equation）纳入非热磁子的散射与输运，并对bcc Fe薄膜的超快激光诱导退磁进行模拟。

Result: 模型预测了超快自旋塞贝克效应（ultrafast spin Seebeck effect），表现为强爆发式快速移动的磁子自旋流（magnonic spin current），达到技术相关幅度；同时识别出超扩散输运（superdiffusive transport）过程——从初始弹道输运（ballistic transport）到后期扩散输运（diffusive regime）的交叉。

Conclusion: 该框架提供了一条超越扩散模型、描述超快非热磁子输运的路径，将有助于时间分辨自旋输运实验（time-resolved spin-transport experiments）的设计与解释。

Abstract: Subpicosecond laser excitation of ferromagnetic metals induces strongly nonequilibrium dynamics involving scattering and transport of electrons, phonons, and magnons. Widely used theoretical approaches, such as the three-temperature model and diffusion equations, are ill-suited to capture these processes on ultrafast timescales. Here, we present an ab initio-parameterized microscopic framework that incorporates nonthermal magnon scattering and transport via the quantum Boltzmann equation. We apply this approach to simulate ultrafast laser-induced demagnetization in bcc Fe films. The model predicts an ultrafast spin Seebeck effect, characterized by a strong burst of fast-moving magnonic spin current reaching technologically relevant amplitudes. Furthermore, we identify a superdiffusive transport regime: a crossover from initially ballistic magnon transport to a diffusive regime at later times. To connect our theoretical predictions to experimentally accessible observables, we calculate the magneto-optical Kerr angles resulting from the predicted depth-resolved magnetization profiles. Our framework provides a route to describe ultrafast nonthermal magnon transport beyond diffusive models and will aid in the design and interpretation of time-resolved spin-transport experiments.

</details>

### [116] [Superconducting PdTe Thin Film Via Topotactic Transformation, Toward Topological Superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20437)
*Hee Taek Yi,Min Ge,Renjie Xie,Colby J. Stoddard,David H. Yi,Xiaoyu Yuan,Xiong Yao,Seongshik Oh*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文报道了通过分子束外延（MBE）技术成功制备出具有类块材超导性质的高质量PdTe薄膜，该薄膜通过拓扑转变（topotactic transformation）从PdTe₂缓冲层转化而来，展现出锐利的超导转变（onset温度4.43 K，转变宽度0.06 K）、NiAs型结构、二维超导行为及优异的空气稳定性，为拓扑超导（topological superconductivity）和马约拉纳物理（Majorana physics）研究提供了有前景的平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑超导体（TSCs）因承载马约拉纳零模（Majorana zero modes, MZMs）而有望实现容错量子计算。PdTe因其拓扑表面态和约4.5 K的超导临界温度（superconducting critical temperature）而成为有前景的候选材料，但制备具有类块材超导性质的PdTe薄膜一直面临挑战。

Method: 采用分子束外延（molecular beam epitaxy, MBE）技术生长PdTe薄膜，具体策略为先生长PdTe₂缓冲层，再在碲缺乏（Te-deficient）条件下在PdTe₂上生长Pd，通过拓扑转变（topotactic transformation）形成PdTe相。

Result: 所制备的PdTe薄膜具有锐利的超导转变（T_onset = 4.43 K，转变宽度0.06 K），与块材晶体相当。结构分析确认其为NiAs型结构，输运分析显示二维超导行为，且薄膜展现出优异的空气稳定性。

Conclusion: MBE生长的PdTe薄膜及其异质结构为拓扑超导和马约拉纳物理研究提供了一个有前景的平台。

Abstract: Topological superconductors (TSCs) hosting Majorana zero modes (MZMs) offer a pathway to fault-tolerant quantum computation. PdTe is a promising TSC candidate due to its topological surface states and a reasonable superconducting critical temperature of ~4.5 K. However, it has been challenging to grow PdTe thin films with bulk-like superconducting properties. Here, we show that high-quality, superconducting PdTe thin films can be grown using molecular beam epitaxy (MBE). The films exhibit a sharp superconducting transition (T_onset = 4.43 K with transition width of 0.06 K), comparable to that of bulk crystals. This was made possible via a topotactic transformation from a PdTe_2 buffer layer to a PdTe phase by growing Pd on top under Te-deficient conditions. Structural and transport analyses confirm the NiAs-type structure of PdTe, as well as its two-dimensional superconducting behavior and excellent air stability. These findings suggest that the MBE-grown PdTe films and their heterostructures are a promising platform for topological superconductivity and Majorana physics.

### [117] [Pressure-induced superconductivity in epitaxially-stabilized Pr$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20653)
*Motoki Osada,Chieko Terakura,Hsiao-Yi Chen,Akiko Kikkawa,Masamichi Nakajima,Ryoma Asai,Jean-Baptiste Morée,Yusuke Nomura,Ryotaro Arita,Yoshinori Tokura,Atsushi Tsukazaki*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究报告通过外延稳定技术在Pr₃Ni₂O₇薄膜中实现了压力诱导的高温超导，起始超导临界温度（T_c）达66 K、零电阻温度约40 K（22 GPa），并系统研究了不同镧系元素（Ln）替代对T_c和临界压力（P_c）的影响，表明外延稳定是拓展双层镍酸盐超导家族的有效手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在La₃Ni₂O₇中发现高压高温超导后，通过镧系元素（Ln）替代和应变薄膜已可扩展超导临界温度（T_c）范围，但新双层镍酸盐的探索受限于热力学稳定性，且体材料单晶合成困难。本研究旨在利用外延稳定（epitaxial stabilization）技术克服合成瓶颈，探索Pr₃Ni₂O₇薄膜中的高压高温超导现象。

Method: 采用外延稳定技术生长Pr₃Ni₂O₇和Nd₃Ni₂O₇薄膜，并对Pr₃Ni₂O₇薄膜施加高压，测量其在不同压力下的电阻-温度行为，同时对比不同镧系元素（Ln = La, Pr, Nd）替代对超导临界温度（T_c）和临界压力（P_c）的影响。

Result: 常压下Pr₃Ni₂O₇薄膜呈现绝缘行为，但在22 GPa下表现出T-线性（T-linear）金属输运，并实现起始超导临界温度（T_c）66 K、零电阻温度近40 K的超导电性。Nd₃Ni₂O₇薄膜虽可稳定生长，但在测量压力范围内未观察到超导。

Conclusion: 镧系元素（Ln）离子半径越小，所需临界压力（P_c）越高，该趋势与体材料中Ln替代的研究结果一致。这表明外延稳定（epitaxial stabilization）是一种有效扩展双层镍酸盐超导家族的技术手段。

Abstract: The discovery of high critical-temperature $T_{\mathrm{c}}$ superconductivity in La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ under high pressure has led to a rapid expansion of the $T_{\mathrm{c}}$ range through lanthanide $Ln$ substitution, and to ambient-pressure superconductivity in strained thin films, yet the exploration of new bilayer nickelates remains strongly constrained by thermodynamic stability. Beyond the difficulty of synthesis of bulk single-crystals, here we report on the pressure-induced high-$T_{\mathrm{c}}$ superconductivity in epitaxially-stabilized Pr$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ thin films. While the Pr$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ films exhibit insulating behaviour at ambient pressure regardless of ozone-annealing treatment, they show $T$-linear metallic transport and superconductivity reaching an onset $T_{\mathrm{c}}$ of 66 K and zero-resistance at nearly 40 K at 22 GPa. Furthermore, Nd$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$, with the smaller rare-earth ion Nd, can also be stabilized, however, superconductivity is not observed in the measured pressure range. Epitaxial stabilization enables us to examine the dependence of $T_{\mathrm{c}}$ and the critical pressure $P_{\mathrm{c}}$ for superconductivity on the $Ln$ ion in $Ln_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ ($Ln$ = La, Pr, Nd). These results suggest that a higher $P_{\mathrm{c}}$ is required for smaller $Ln$ ions, consistent with trends observed in bulk studies of $Ln$ substitution. This study demonstrates that epitaxial stabilization is a powerful technique to further expand the family of superconducting bilayer nickelates.

</details>


### [118] [Multiple Superconducting Phases in Palladium Deuteride Induced by Nuclear-Spin Isotope Effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20966)
*Ryoma Kato,Ten-ichiro Yoshida,Riku Iimori,Masanobu Shiga,Yuji Inagaki,Takashi Kimura,Koichiro Ienaga,Tatsuya Kawae*

TL;DR: 该论文报告了高质量PdDₓ薄膜的超导特性，发现其电阻在1.7 K附近急剧下降，但有限电阻持续存在至约0.6 K才完全消失。在超导态中，电阻随温度和磁场的变化显示出多重异常，表明存在不同的超导相。这些异常在PdHₓ薄膜中未观察到，揭示了PdDₓ与PdHₓ超导相图之间存在明显的定性差异，强调了核自旋同位素效应（nuclear-spin isotope effects）的作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究不同氢同位素对钯基超导体（palladium-based superconductors）超导性质的影响，尤其关注核自旋同位素效应是否会导致超导相图的定性差异。

Method: 制备高质量PdDₓ薄膜，通过测量其电阻率（resistivity）在低温下的温度依赖性和磁场依赖性来表征超导转变行为。

Result: 电阻率在约1.7 K处急剧下降标志着超导转变的开始，但有限电阻持续至约0.6 K才完全消失。超导态内电阻随温度和磁场的变化表现出多重异常，指示存在多个不同的超导相。这些异常在PdHₓ薄膜中未被观察到。

Conclusion: PdDₓ与PdHₓ的超导相图存在清晰的定性差异，表明核自旋同位素效应对钯基氢化物超导体（palladium hydride superconductors）的超导性质具有重要影响。

Abstract: We study the superconducting properties of high-quality PdD$_{x}$ films. The resistivity shows a sharp drop at $T$ $\sim$1.7 K, marking the superconducting transition. However, a finite resistivity persists and vanishes at $\sim$0.6 K. The temperature and magnetic-field dependences of the resistivity exhibit multiple anomalies within the superconducting state, revealing distinct superconducting phases. Such anomalies are absent in PdH$_{x}$ films. These results demonstrate a clear qualitative difference between the superconducting phase diagrams of PdD$_{x}$ and PdH$_{x}$, highlighting the role of nuclear-spin isotope effects.

### [119] [Micro-explosion of emulsion droplets with nanoparticles at high temperature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21354)
*Houpeng Zhang,Zhen Lu,Tianyou Wang,Zhizhao Che*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 该研究通过高速摄影、数字图像处理、光学显微镜和扫描电子显微镜等实验手段，探究了纳米颗粒对乳化液滴微爆（micro-explosion）行为的影响。实验表明，纳米颗粒（尤其是碳纳米颗粒）能够显著增强微爆的强度和概率，主要机制包括促进辐射能吸收、抑制过热蒸汽扩散等；同时，增加纳米颗粒质量分数和含水量也有利于微爆的发生。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 与传统燃料相比，乳化燃料（emulsified fuels）可改善燃料雾化与燃烧性能，而纳米颗粒作为添加剂具有增强燃烧、减少排放的潜力。先前关于微爆（micro-explosion）现象的研究主要关注纯乳化液滴，纳米颗粒在乳化液滴微爆中的具体作用机制仍不明确。

Method: 采用高速摄影（high-speed photography）、数字图像处理（digital image processing）、光学显微镜（optical microscopy）和扫描电子显微镜（scanning electron microscopy）等实验手段，系统观测并分析含纳米颗粒的乳化液滴的微爆过程。

Result: 纳米颗粒的存在可显著提升微爆的强度与概率，尤其是碳纳米颗粒（carbon nanoparticles）效果最为突出。机理分析表明，纳米颗粒在液滴蒸发过程中发生团聚（agglomeration），促进辐射能的吸收、抑制过热蒸汽的扩散，从而促进微爆。此外，增加纳米颗粒质量分数（mass fraction）和含水量（water content）均有助于微爆的发生。

Conclusion: 纳米颗粒可作为乳化燃料中促进微爆的有效添加剂，其作用机制涉及团聚、辐射吸收与蒸汽扩散抑制等多重物理过程。该发现为优化乳化燃料设计、提高燃烧效率及降低排放提供了新的实验依据。

Abstract: Compared with traditional fuels, emulsified fuels can improve fuel atomization and combustion, and nanoparticles as additives have the potential to enhance combustion and reduce emissions. Previous studies on micro-explosion mainly considered emulsion droplets, but the role of nanoparticles in emulsion droplets is still unclear. In this study, we experimentally investigate the micro-explosion of emulsion droplets with nanoparticles via high-speed photography, digital image processing, optical microscopy, and scanning electron microscopy. The results show that the presence of nanoparticles can greatly improve the strength and probability of micro-explosion, particularly for carbon nanoparticles. This is mainly because nanoparticles can agglomerate during the evaporation of emulsion droplets, facilitate the absorption of radiation energy, inhibit the diffusion of superheated vapor, and ultimately promote micro-explosion. The effects of nanoparticle mass fraction and water content are also investigated, and the results show that the increase of nanoparticles and water can facilitate micro-explosion.

</details>

### [120] [Modified Painlevé systems with meromorphic solutions for polynomial Hamiltonians of all degrees](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21166)
*Marta Dell'Atti,Thomas Kecker*

Main category: nlin.SI

TL;DR: 本文研究了两变量多项式非自洽哈密顿系统，其所有解均为复平面上的亚纯函数。通过计算一般系数函数的初始条件空间，获得了系统仅具有亚纯解的微分约束。基于哈密顿函数的牛顿多边形（Newton polygon），分类得到了度为3、4、5、7的所有此类系统（度为6或高于7时不存在），列出12个标准多项式哈密顿量，可作为Painlevé等价问题的参考，其中包含多个先前未报道的新哈密顿量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在系统分类所有解为亚纯函数的非自洽多项式哈密顿系统，并建立它们与Painlevé性质（Painlevé property）哈密顿系统之间的联系，为Painlevé等价问题提供标准参考系。

Method: 采用几何方法，通过计算一般系数函数的Hamitonian系统的冈本初始条件空间（Okamoto's space of initial conditions），获得系统仅具有亚纯解的微分约束条件；并利用哈密顿函数的牛顿多边形（Newton polygon）指导分类，按依赖变量下的仿射等价（affine equivalence）进行分类。

Result: 得到了所有度为3、4、5、7的此类系统，度为6或高于7时不存在；最终列出12个标准多项式哈密顿量，包括Painlevé I和II的四次哈密顿量、修正Painlevé III和V的四次哈密顿量、Painlevé IV的五次哈密顿量以及修正Painlevé VI的五次和七次哈密顿量等新结果。

Conclusion: 成功构建了12个标准多项式哈密顿量作为Painlevé等价问题的参考列表，其中包含多个此前未被记录的新哈密顿量，填补了相关分类空白。

Abstract: We review non-autonomous Hamiltonian systems, polynomial in two dependent variables, with the property that all of their solutions are meromorphic functions in the complex plane. These are related to known Hamiltonian systems with the Painlevé property, for which the solutions are single-valued outside a set of fixed singularities. Our systems are equivalent to them in the absence of fixed singularities, and give modified Painlevé equations otherwise. Using the geometric approach by computing the Okamoto's spaces of initial conditions for certain Hamiltonian systems with general coefficient functions, we obtain differential constraints on these functions for the systems to have only meromorphic solutions. Guided by the Newton polygon of the Hamiltonian function, we obtain all such systems with polynomial Hamiltonian of degree three, four, five, and seven, up to affine equivalence in the dependent variables, while there are none for degree six or degree higher than seven. We thus obtain a list of 12 standard polynomial Hamiltonians that can serve as reference for the Painlevé equivalence problem. This list contains also some new Hamiltonians not previously written down, such as quartic Hamiltonians for Painlevé I and II, quartic Hamiltonians for the modified Painlevé III and V equations, a quintic Hamiltonian for Painlevé IV and quintic and septic Hamiltonians for a modified Painlevé VI equation.

</details>

### [121] [Data-driven stress problem under purely normal homogeneous Neumann boundary conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21044)
*Cristian G. Gebhardt,Kundan Kumar,Florin A. Radu*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文为纯均匀法向诺伊曼边界条件下的数据驱动应力问题建立了严格的泛函分析框架，证明了在实验材料数据为有限离散集的条件下，解的存在性与唯一性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数据驱动连续介质力学（Data-Driven Continuum Mechanics）尽管已有进展，但其分析基础仍处于早期阶段，缺乏严格的数学框架。

Method: 建立一个泛函分析（functional-analytic framework）框架，将问题表述为在$L^p$意义下寻找最接近辅助应力场的应力场；利用散度算子（divergence operator）诱导的拓扑同构性确保平衡响应的存在性，利用材料数据集的有限性保证应力空间中的迫近性（proximinality）。

Result: 散度算子的拓扑同构性保证了平衡响应的存在，有限数据集的迫近性推导出解等价类（solution equivalence classes）的完整存在性与唯一性理论。

Conclusion: 这两个性质共同为纯均匀法向诺伊曼边界条件下的数据驱动应力问题提供了严格的数学基础。

Abstract: Data-Driven Continuum Mechanics -- the continuous counterpart of Data-Driven Computational Mechanics -- is a modern paradigm that enhances classical continuum mechanics by incorporating finite sets of experimental material data directly, avoiding any form of constitutive modeling. Despite recent progress, its analytical foundations remain at an early stage. In this work, we establish a rigorous functional-analytic framework for the data-driven stress problem under purely homogeneous normal Neumann boundary conditions. The problem is formulated as finding a stress field (satisfying the balance of linear and angular momenta and the boundary conditions) that is closest, in an $L^p$-sense, to an auxiliary stress field that is simultaneously sought and locally resembles a finite discrete set of experimental stress states. Our analysis relies on two key ingredients. First, the divergence operator induces a topological isomorphism between the space of symmetric stress fields modulo its kernel and the space of loads balanced by rigid-body motions, ensuring the existence of an equilibrated response. Second, the finiteness of the material data set guarantees proximinality in the stress space, which in turn yields a complete existence and uniqueness theory for solution equivalence classes. Together, these two properties provide a rigorous mathematical foundation for the data-driven stress problem under purely homogeneous normal Neumann boundary conditions.

### [122] [Representability-Aware Neural Networks for Reduced Density Matrices: Application to Fractional Chern Insulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20326)
*Justin B. Hart,Awwab A. Azam,Thomas Li,Yunxuan Li,Ye Bi,Haining Pan,Jiabin Yu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出一种可感知代表性（representability-aware）且可插值（interpolable）的神经网络框架，用于预测双粒子约化密度矩阵（2-RDM）。该框架通过在网络架构和损失函数中嵌入一部分代表性条件（representability conditions），并利用多动量网格上的插值代表性条件（interpolated representability condition），可在小网格上插值或在大网格上变分优化。在转角二硫化钼（twisted bilayer MoTe₂）的分数量子陈绝缘体（fractional Chern insulator）模型中，该网络在能量和精度上均优于传统的边界点半定规划（boundary-point semidefinite programming），且参数量低于后者的1/20。最终，该框架在含48个动量点的对称网格上预测了多体基态能量和多体量子度量（many-body quantum metric）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的双粒子约化密度矩阵（2-RDM）预测方法，如边界点半定规划（boundary-point semidefinite programming），在计算精度和参数效率方面存在不足。因此，亟需开发一种既能有效嵌入代表性条件（representability conditions）、又能跨动量网格灵活插值（interpolable）的神经网络框架，以提升2-RDM预测的精度和计算效率。

Method: 提出一种可感知代表性（representability-aware）且可插值（interpolable）的神经网络（NN）框架。该框架通过网络架构和损失函数嵌入部分代表性条件（representability conditions），并引入跨动量网格的插值代表性条件（interpolated representability condition）。框架支持两种工作模式：从小网格的精确结果插值预测大网格上的2-RDM，或在任意网格上作为变分2-RDM ansatz通过能量最小化进行优化。在转角二硫化钼（twisted bilayer MoTe₂）的分数量子陈绝缘体（fractional Chern insulator）模型（转角3.89°，空穴填充2/3）中，采用六种不同的网络架构，基于12或18个动量点的精确对角化（exact-diagonalization, ED）2-RDM进行训练。

Result: 最佳网络为残差多层感知机（residual multilayer perceptron），在6×6网格上预测2-RDM的精度为97.07%–98.18%，但预测能量比精确对角化（ED）基态能量高77.353 meV。经过变分优化后，在6×6网格上预测能量比ED低0.104 meV，精度维持在98.94%–98.96%。与边界点半定规划（BPSDP）相比（能量比ED低5.560 meV，精度96.40%–98.94%），该神经网络（NN）在能量上更精确、精度相近，且参数量不到BPSDP的1/20。最终在48个动量点的对称网格上，预测了多体基态能量和多体量子度量（many-body quantum metric）。

Conclusion: 所提出的可感知代表性且可插值的神经网络（NN）框架在双粒子约化密度矩阵（2-RDM）预测中，既能达到更高的能量精度和相当的预测精度，又能大幅减少参数数量，展示了神经网络在量子多体问题中结合代表性条件（representability conditions）与插值策略的有效性和优越性。

Abstract: We develop a representability-aware and interpolable neural network (NN) framework for predicting two-particle reduced density matrices (2-RDMs). The NN incorporates a subset of representability conditions through its architecture and loss function, and can operate on different momentum meshes, enabling evaluating the representability conditions across multiple meshes, which we call interpolated representability condition. The framework can be used either to predict 2-RDMs on large momentum meshes by interpolating exact results from small meshes, or as a variational 2-RDM ansatz optimized by energy minimization on arbitrary meshes. We apply this approach to the fractional Chern insulator in the one-band projected model of twisted bilayer MoTe$_2$ at twist angle $3.89^\circ$ and hole filling $2/3$. Trained on exact-diagonalization (ED) 2-RDMs from meshes with $12$ or $18$ momentum points using six different NN architectures, the best NN is the residual multilayer perceptron, which predicts the $6\times6$ 2-RDM with $97.07\%-98.18\%$ accuracy relative to the ED 2-RDM but predicts an energy $77.353$ meV above ED ground-state energy. We then variationally optimize the NN on several meshes including $6\times6$, predicting a $6\times 6$ energy of just $0.104$ meV below ED while maintaining $98.94\%-98.96\%$ accuracy. Compared with the conventional boundary-point semidefinite programming, which gives an energy $5.560$ meV below ED with $96.40\%-98.94\%$ accuracy, the NN achieves a more accurate energy and similar accuracy while using only less than 1/20 as many parameters. Eventually, we add a symmetric mesh of $48$ momentum points to the variational optimization of the NN, and provide a prediction of the many-body ground-state energy and the many-body quantum metric on that mesh.

### [123] [Textured phase diagrams of featureless insulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20339)
*Sashank Singam,Nick G. Jones,Abhishodh Prakash*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文研究电荷守恒“A类”无相互作用费米子的相图，重点关注平凡相（featureless phase）。通过贝里相位（Berry phase）及其高维推广，揭示了由电荷泵（charge pump）等非平凡拓扑态族导致的相图拓扑纹理（topological textures），并分析了相图奇异性、边界模的鲁棒性以及相互作用下的稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对无相互作用费米子系统中通常被视为“无特征”（featureless）的平凡相，揭示其内部隐藏的非平凡拓扑结构，填补对电荷守恒A类费米子相图拓扑纹理系统理解的空白。

Method: 利用贝里相位及其高维推广来可视化相图拓扑纹理；对于具有平移不变性的系统，采用非阿贝尔陈-西蒙斯形式（non-abelian Chern-Simons forms）的积分计算这些“高阶”贝里相位；通过构建微观模型和映射到连续场论（continuum field theory）来探索近邻相图。

Result: 相图中的奇异性对应于能隙闭合的“魔鬼点”（diabolical points），是拓扑非平凡态族收缩的障碍；体-边对应（bulk-boundary correspondence）导致稳健边界模终止于这些魔鬼点。在有限化学势下，二维及更高维度的边缘模无需微调即可保持稳健，而一维边缘模则出现“疏离”（estranged）行为，即不同边缘出现在不同参数值处。

Conclusion: 平凡相相图实际上具有非平凡的拓扑纹理结构，且所发现的边界模在相互作用下具有稳定性，表明该拓扑结构在更一般系统中仍然成立。

Abstract: We study phase diagrams of charge-conserving `class A' non-interacting fermions, focusing on the trivial phase in various dimensions. Such phases are usually termed `featureless' to distinguish them from those others with either symmetry-broken or topological order. We show that the presence of non-trivial topological families of states, including charge pumps and their generalizations, results in phase diagrams being endowed with non-trivial topological textures that can be visualized through Berry phases and their higher-dimensional generalizations. We show that for non-interacting fermion systems with translation invariance, these `higher' Berry phases can be computed using integrals of non-abelian Chern-Simons forms of the Berry-Bloch connection over momentum and parameter spaces. Singularities in these textures correspond to gap-closing loci of `diabolical points', which represent the obstruction to contracting topologically non-trivial families of states, and bulk-boundary correspondence results in a locus of robust boundary modes that terminate at the bulk diabolical points. In the presence of finite chemical potential, we argue that the edge modes are generically robust without any need for fine-tuning for two and higher dimensions, whereas in one dimension they are `estranged' in the phase diagram, i.e. appearing at different parameter values for different edges. We demonstrate our results by constructing several microscopic models of non-interacting fermions. We argue stability to interactions and explore proximate phase diagrams by mapping to continuum field theories.

</details>


### [124] [Velocity collapse and non-conformal spiral phase in the sawtooth spin chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20343)
*Nai Chao Hu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过玻色化理论（bosonization theory）解释锯齿链（sawtooth chain）螺旋相中数值模拟发现的异常现象，包括大表观中心荷、慢动力学标度、近乎平坦的激发谱以及无可检测的二聚化。研究表明，锯齿几何结构抵消了主要的交错相互作用，留下边缘扭曲相互作用，选择性地使慢顶端自旋速度消失，从而进入局域量子临界性（local quantum criticality）的强耦合区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 锯齿链螺旋相中的矩阵乘积态（matrix-product-state）计算显示出一系列与普通共形临界点（conformal critical point）不一致的数值特征，需要新的理论框架来统一解释这些反常现象。

Method: 将锯齿极限嵌入到zigzag梯子模型中，利用两个耦合的SU(2)$_1$共形场论（conformal field theory）来描述，这两个理论具有极端的速度比。通过玻色化方法分析相互作用结构，特别是锯齿几何对交错相互作用的抵消效应以及边缘扭曲相互作用的角色。

Result: 锯齿几何结构取消了主要的交错（staggered）相互作用，留下一个边缘扭曲（twist）相互作用，该相互作用选择性地使慢顶端自旋速度（apical spin velocity）趋于零。随着速度消失，产生的顶端背散射（apical backscattering）相互作用仅在无量纲单位下发散，导致能量尺度独立于空间关联长度而坍塌。

Conclusion: 该机制自然解释了数值模拟中观察到的多个反常现象，并将微扰流解释为进入强耦合区域局域量子临界性的入口。

Abstract: Recent matrix-product-state calculations show that the spiral phase in the sawtooth chain has numerical signatures that are difficult to reconcile with an ordinary conformal critical point: a large apparent central charge, slow dynamical scaling, nearly flat excitations, and no detectable dimerization. We develop a bosonization theory for this phenomenology by embedding the sawtooth limit in a zigzag ladder described by two coupled SU(2)$_1$ conformal field theories characterized by an extreme velocity ratio. We show that the sawtooth geometry cancels the leading staggered interaction, leaving a marginal twist interaction that selectively collapses the slow apical spin velocity. Crucially, as this velocity vanishes, the generated apical backscattering interaction diverges only in dimensionless units, causing the energy scale to collapse independently of the spatial correlation length. This mechanism naturally accounts for many of the numerical anomalies and we interpret the perturbative flow as an entrance to local quantum criticality in the strong-coupling regime.

Conclusion: 晶格通道与电荷通道中截然不同的行为揭示了CDW相中材料依赖的对称性破缺现象的关键信息。结合理论与实验，该研究阐明了AV₃Sb₅ kagome超导体中电荷有序结构的性质。

Abstract: The kagome superconductor family AV3Sb5 (A=Cs, Rb, K) provides a rich platform for exploring diverse electronic symmetry breaking phenomena, including superconductivity and various forms of density wave orders. Although these compounds share the identical lattice structure in the normal state, they exhibit distinct forms of symmetry breaking upon entering the charge density wave (CDW) phase, and the microscopic origin of which remain elusive. Here, we investigate the lattice and charge degrees of freedom in AV3Sb5 using angle-resolved polarized Raman spectroscopy. Our comprehensive polarization-resolved measurements reveal that the lifting of the twofold-degeneracy of the E2g phonon mode in the CDW phase-previously reported only in CsV3Sb5 with a 3 GHz splitting-also appears ubiquitously in the other two compounds. In contrast, the collective CDW excitations exhibit markedly different polarization dependences depending on the alkali-metal species. These distinct behaviors in the lattice and charge channels provide crucial insight into the enigmatic material-dependent symmetry breaking phenomena that appear in the CDW phase. Furthermore, our experiments, together with first-principles calculations and an effective Hamiltonian model, shed light on the nature of the charge order structure in AV3Sb5 kagome superconductors.

Abstract: The understanding of quantum many-body states in twisted bilayer graphene at the magic angle has been greatly improved both in experiment and in theory. However, away from the exactly solvable chiral limit and the sign-problem-free charge neutrality point, the calculation of the ground state properties and the identification of the phase diagram are challenging due to the exponential increase in the complexity, which has rendered explanations of experimentally observed insulating and superconducting phases restricted largely to the perturbative level. Here we focus on the filling factors $ν= \pm2$ away from charge neutrality and address the question of the strain dependence of the interacting ground state. We adjust our continuous field momentum-space quantum Monte Carlo (QMC) method to treat the sign problem approximately, and perform a quantum many-body study together with exact diagonalization (ED) and Hartree-Fock (HF) mean field. Leveraging this combined protocol of QMC, ED, and HF, we investigate the strain-tuned transition from the Kramers intervalley coherent (KIVC) state to the incommensurate Kekulé spiral state (IKS). Our computational protocol sheds light on the KIVC-IKS transition in a projected correlated flat-band setting, and opens the door for further understanding of the rich phase diagram of twisted bilayer graphene and other strongly-correlated flat-band systems.

### [127] [Giant nonlinear conductivity in 2D electron gas from substrate-induced dipolar scattering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20699)
*Dmitry V. Chichinadze,Alexander Seidel,Zohar Nussinov*
