  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管二维材料中的非线性输运（nonlinear transport）备受关注，但现有理论框架无法定量解释近期在二维范德华异质结（2D van der Waals heterostructures）中观测到的巨非线性电导（giant nonlinear conductivities，≥1 μm/ΩV），构成了一个基础性难题。

Method: 提出了一种基于衬底诱导周期性偶极阵列（substrate-induced periodic dipole array）的电子散射（electron scattering）机制，并分析了二维散射中固有的严格运动学约束（strict kinematic constraints）对非线性响应的影响。

Result: 研究发现，二维散射固有的运动学约束会导致非线性响应出现奇异增强（singular enhancement），并从根本上确定了一个自然尺度（natural scale）为1 μm/ΩV。

Conclusion: 该机制为定量理解二维材料中巨非线性电导的来源提供了新的理论视角，弥合了现有理论与实验观测之间的差距。

Abstract: Despite a surge of interest in the nonlinear transport in 2D materials, a fundamental puzzle remains: existing theoretical frameworks are unable to quantitatively account for the giant nonlinear conductivities ($\gtrsim 1 \frac{μ\text{m}}{Ω\text{V}}$) recently reported in 2D van der Waals heterostructures. Here, we introduce a mechanism based on electron scattering from a substrate-induced periodic dipole array. We show that the strict kinematic constraints, inherent to 2D scattering, lead to a singular enhancement of the nonlinear response, fundamentally dictating a natural scale of $1 \frac{μ\text{m}}{Ω\text{V}}$.

</details>


### [128] [Hubbard-$U$-corrected electron-phonon interactions in strongly correlated materials via the finite-displacement method](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20985)
*Jiale Chen,Youyou Tu,Chengliang Xia,Jin Zhao,Hanghui Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文在密度泛函理论加哈伯德U修正（DFT+U）框架内实现了电子-声子g矩阵的全包含算法，并应用于LaNiO₂和RuO₂两种关联材料，揭示了Hubbard U修正对电子-声子耦合的显著影响及其与GW方法的差异来源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管DFT+U方法已广泛应用于强关联材料的电子结构研究，但其向电子-声子g矩阵扩展的工作尚不充分。作者旨在系统地实现将Hubbard U修正同时纳入电子结构、声子谱及电子-声子g矩阵的计算，以更准确地描述关联材料中的电子-声子相互作用。

Method: 将DFT+U方法与有限位移法（finite-displacement method）相结合，实现声子和电子-声子g矩阵的计算。Hubbard U修正同时应用于电子结构、声子结构和电子-声子g矩阵。算法在无限层镍酸盐LaNiO₂和二氧化钌RuO₂两种典型关联材料上进行验证。

Result: 对于20%空穴掺杂的LaNiO₂，Hubbard U修正略微增强了电子-声子相互作用，但总体耦合仍然很小，不足以解释约10–30 K的超导转变温度。这与近期GW方法给出的结果（电子-声子耦合约为DFT值的五倍）存在矛盾，归因于DFT+U与GW方法在费米面拓扑（Fermi surface topology）上的差异。对于RuO₂，加入Hubbard U修正消除了TiO₂衬底应变下的虚声子模（imaginary phonon modes），并显著降低了电子-声子耦合，缓解了理论预测与实验观测之间超导转变温度的差异。

Conclusion: 提供了一种在DFT+U框架内完整包含Hubbard U修正的电子-声子性质计算算法，强调了费米面形状和关联效应对声子谱及电子-声子g矩阵的重要性。

Abstract: Although the density functional theory plus Hubbard $U$ correction method (DFT+U) is broadly used to study electronic structure of strongly correlated materials, the extension of this method to electron-phonon $g$ matrices has received limited attention. Here, we implement an algorithm that integrates DFT+U method with the finite-displacement method for the calculations of phonons and electron-phonon $g$ matrices. The Hubbard $U$ corrections are applied not only to electronic and phonon structures, but, more importantly, also to electron-phonon $g$ matrices. We demonstrate our algorithm in two prototypical correlated materials: infinite-layer nickelates LaNiO$_2$ and ruthenium dioxide RuO$_2$. We find that: i) While the Hubbard $U$ corrections weakly increase the electron-phonon interaction of 20% hole-doped LaNiO$_2$, its total electron-phonon coupling remains small and is insufficient to account for the observed superconducting transition temperature of about 10-30 K. Our results contrast with the recent work showing that the full GW corrections yield an elevated electron-phonon coupling of 20% hole-doped LaNiO$_2$ five times larger than its DFT value. We attribute this discrepancy to the differences in the Fermi surface topology between DFT+$U$ and GW methods. ii) The inclusion of Hubbard $U$ corrections eliminates the imaginary phonon modes of RuO$_2$ under strain on the TiO$_2$ substrate and substantially reduces the electron-phonon coupling. Our results alleviate the discrepancy between the reported large theoretical electron-phonon coupling and the low superconducting transition temperature observed experimentally. Our work provides an algorithm that fully includes the Hubbard $U$ corrections on electron-phonon properties of correlated materials, and highlights the importance of Fermi surface shape and correlation effects on phonon spectrum and electron-phonon $g$ matrices.

</details>


### [129] [Magnetism of single crystalline breathing pyrochlore spinel AgInCr4S8](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21122)
*Andrew F. May,Christopher M. Pasco,V. O. Garlea,Karolina Gornicka,Matthias D. Frontzek,Xiaoping Wang,Pyeongjae Park,Andrew D. Christianson*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本研究通过化学气相输运法生长出AgInCr4S8单晶，确认其呼吸烧绿石（breathing pyrochlore）结构，并借助交流/直流磁化率、比热容和单晶中子衍射等手段，系统表征了其在TN≈9.6 K以下的长程反铁磁序、部分磁熵缺失以及沿(0,0,δ)传播的非公度螺旋磁结构，为呼吸烧绿石材料的单晶研究提供了罕见案例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 呼吸烧绿石（breathing pyrochlore）材料因其几何阻挫（geometrical frustration）和复杂磁序而受到关注，但相关单晶研究非常稀缺。本文旨在通过生长高质量AgInCr4S8单晶，系统揭示其晶体结构、磁有序行为及磁结构特征，填补该材料体系中单晶层面系统研究的空白。

Method: 采用化学气相输运（chemical vapor transport）法生长AgInCr4S8单晶；利用X射线衍射和中子衍射确认Ag/In的晶体学有序及呼吸烧绿石结构；通过交流（ac）和直流（dc）磁化率、比热容（specific heat capacity）以及单晶中子衍射（single crystal neutron diffraction）测量，全面表征其磁学性质。

Result: AgInCr4S8在奈尔温度（Néel temperature）TN≈9.6 K以下出现长程反铁磁有序；比热容在9.5 K附近呈现小λ反常峰，至3TN时累积磁熵仅达理论预期值的约1/3，表明顺磁相中存在显著的短程有序（short-range order）。单晶中子衍射在5 K下确认非公度（incommensurate）自旋结构，传播矢量k=(0,0,δ)，δ=0.343；磁结构由铁磁Cr原子层构成，磁矩位于层内平面，沿垂直方向调制形成螺旋结构（helical structure）。

Conclusion: 本研究首次系统报道了呼吸烧绿石材料AgInCr4S8的单晶磁结构，揭示了非公度螺旋反铁磁序和显著的短程磁关联，证明了该体系是研究几何阻挫与复杂磁序相互作用的理想平台。该工作为呼吸烧绿石家族的单晶物性研究提供了重要实验依据。

Abstract: Single crystals of \ce{AgInCr4S8} were grown by chemical vapor transport and crystallographic ordering of Ag/In that results in a breathing pyrochlore motif of Cr$^{3+}$ was verified by x-ray and neutron diffraction. Long-range antiferromagnetic order is observed below a Néel temperature of $T_{\mathrm N}$ $\approx$ 9.6 K. The magnetic properties are characterized using ac and dc magnetization, specific heat capacity, and single crystal neutron diffraction measurements. The specific heat data are characterized by a small lambda anomaly near 9.5 K and the estimated magnetic entropy reaches $\approx$ $\frac{1}{3}$ of the expected value by 3$T_{\mathrm N}$, suggesting significant short-range order in the paramagnetic phase. Single crystal neutron diffraction evidences an incommensurate spin structure with propagation vector $\textbf{\textit{k}}$ = (0,0,$δ$) and $δ$ = 0.343 at 5 K. The minimal model that accounts for the data consists of ferromagnetic layers of Cr atoms, with magnetic moments lying in the plane of the layers and modulating in the perpendicular direction to form a helical structure propagating along $\textbf{\textit{k}}$. This study represents a rare investigation of single crystals within the family of breathing pyrochlore materials.

</details>

### [130] [Topological Field Theories and the Algebraic Structures of the Two-Sphere](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20846)
*Chris Li*

Main category: math.AT

TL;DR: 本文在三维有向配边范畴中给出了 $S^2$ 的两种表示，定义了 P-幺半群（P-monoid）和 L-幺半群（L-monoid），二者均为交换 Frobenius 幺半群并相互等价，同时引入了由闭不可约素三维流形标号的素结构（prime structure）及“腿关系”（legs relations），揭示了其在代数层面退化为素单位乘法的简洁行为，并提出了一个包含 $\infty$-小三维立方体 operad 的 $\infty$-operad。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解三维定向配边范畴 $\operatorname{Cob}(3)$ 中 $S^2$ 上蕴含的代数结构，并通过拓扑场论（topological field theory）将其提炼为新的幺半群结构，从而探索三维流形拓扑与代数结构之间的深层联系。

Method: 在三维定向配边范畴 $\operatorname{Cob}(3)$ 中给出 $S^2$ 的两种表示，通过拓扑场论定义 P-幺半群和 L-幺半群；证明二者均为交换 Frobenius 幺半群（commutative Frobenius monoid）且等价；引入由闭不可约素三维流形标定的自同态（endomorphism）和单位态射（unit morphism），建立“腿关系”；在代数限制下分析素结构的行为，并提出一个 $\infty$-operad 来编码这些结构。

Result: P-幺半群和 L-幺半群均为交换 Frobenius 幺半群且彼此等价；腿关系强制素自同态退化为素单位（prime unit）的乘法运算，使额外的素结构变得极其简单；所提出的 $\infty$-operad 包含 $\infty$-小三维立方体 operad（$\infty$-little 3-cube operad）作为子 operad。

Conclusion: 三维流形拓扑诱导的素结构在代数层面受到腿关系的严格约束，展现出简洁的代数行为；所构造的 $\infty$-operad 为统一描述这些结构提供了框架，并暗示与三维拓扑场论分类中的 J-代数（J-algebra）存在潜在联系。

Abstract: We give two presentations for bordisms of $S^2$ in the 3-dimensional oriented bordism category $\operatorname{Cob}(3) $, encoding the algebraic structures on $S^2$. After passing through topological field theories, we define two kinds of monoids which we call P-monoids and L-monoids. In addition to both being commutative Frobenius monoids, P-monoids are equipped with a class of endomorphisms while L-monoids are equipped with a class of unit morphisms, all of which are labelled by closed oriented irreducible prime 3-manifolds. They turn out to be equivalent. The new prime structures satisfy some countable relations with the commutative Frobenius structure, the most notable of which we call "legs relations." We then restrict to the setting of algebras and show that the legs relations place strong constraints on the new prime endomorphisms which forces them to act by multiplications by prime units, rendering the additional prime structures remarkably simple. We also propose an $\infty$-operad which encodes these prime structures and contains the $\infty$-little 3-cube operad as a sub-operad.% We briefly discuss the relations between P/L-algebras and J-algebras which classify 3-dimensional TFTs.

### [131] [The Causal Bootstrap: Bounding Smeared Spectral Functions from Non-Perturbative Euclidean Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20509)
*Ryan Abbott,Sarah Fields,William I. Jay,Patrick Oare,Matteo Saccardi*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文提出了因果自举法（causal bootstrap），一个从有限非微扰欧几里得数据（finite non-perturbative Euclidean data）中对涂抹谱观测量（smeared spectral observables）进行上下界约束的框架。该方法通过对与数据相容的正谱密度凸集进行优化，并利用协方差矩阵纳入统计不确定性（包括相关性），来给出目标观测量的严格上下界。对于多项式、有理式和分段有理式核函数，该问题可转化为有限维半定规划（semidefinite program），与数值共形自举法（numerical conformal bootstrap）中的技术相通。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从有限的非微扰欧几里得数据中对涂抹谱观测量进行严格且高效的界约束，是数值共形场论和格点场论中的一个基本问题。现有方法在处理统计相关性时缺乏系统性，且与矩问题（moment problems）、Nevanlinna–Pick插值等数学结构的关系尚不明确。

Method: 该方法将问题表述为在兼容数据的正谱密度凸集上的优化，利用协方差矩阵定义统计相容区域；通过拉格朗日对偶性（Lagrange duality）将原问题转化为对涂抹核（smearing kernel）的认证界问题；对多项式、有理式及分段有理式核，采用半定规划技术将对偶问题降为有限维形式。

Result: 数值算例验证了该方法的有效性。理论分析表明，该框架统一了矩问题、Nevanlinna–Pick插值和线性核重构方法（linear kernel-reconstruction methods），揭示了它们之间的深层联系。

Conclusion: 因果自举法提供了一个统一、严格的框架，能够从带有统计相关性的非微扰数据中系统地计算涂抹谱观测量的界，并与共形自举等已有方法建立了技术联系。

Abstract: This work introduces the causal bootstrap, a framework for bounding smeared spectral observables from finite non-perturbative Euclidean data. The method optimizes over the convex set of positive spectral densities compatible with the data to compute rigorous upper and lower bounds on the target observable. Statistical uncertainties, including correlations, are incorporated through compatibility regions using the covariance matrix. The bounds are equivalent, via Lagrange duality, to certified bounds on the target smearing kernel. For polynomial, rational, and piecewise rational kernels, the resulting dual problems can be reduced to finite-dimensional semidefinite programs using techniques familiar, e.g., in the numerical conformal bootstrap. The present formulation clarifies the relation to moment problems, Nevanlinna--Pick interpolation, and linear kernel-reconstruction methods. Numerical examples demonstrate the method.

</details>

### [132] [Microscopic Nonaffine Deformation Theory of LAOS in Polymers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21021)
*Dario Nichetti,Alessio Zaccone*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个分子动机框架，将缠结高分子中大振幅振荡剪切（LAOS）的非线性行为与无序固体中频率依赖的非仿射（nonaffine）弛豫联系起来。核心思想是将LAOS的一阶谐波解释为残余锁相弹性响应，高阶谐波则编码应变依赖性非仿射弛豫的傅里叶特征。通过约束计数和八链仿射网络表示，得到了非线性指数（NLI）的上限估计值，支持将NLI解释为傅里叶分辨的动态非仿射参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 缠结高分子在LAOS下的非线性响应缺乏来自分子尺度的统一理论解释，现有模型多依赖唯象幂律，缺乏与微观非仿射弛豫机制的桥梁。

Method: 发展了一个分子动机框架，将LAOS谐波分析与无序固体中非仿射弛豫理论相结合；引入约束存活分数概念替代管取向张量；采用八链仿射网络表示与中心力非仿射等静阈值进行约束计数。

Result: 有限振幅模量被解释为演化微结构的局部切线刚度；特征应变幅度$γ_c$控制交叉行为，而非通用固定幂律指数；拟合值$N_{\max}\simeq1.72$表明数据接近但未完全饱和；约束计数给出$|\mathrm{NLI}|_{\max}=3$的限制性估计。

Conclusion: 支持将非线性指数（NLI）解释为傅里叶分辨的动态非仿射参数，并建立了管基高分子动力学、LAOS谐波分析、弹塑性流变学与微观非仿射晶格动力学之间的桥梁。

Abstract: We develop a molecularly motivated framework connecting large-amplitude oscillatory shear (LAOS) nonlinearities in entangled polymers to frequency-dependent nonaffine relaxation in disordered solids. The central idea is that the first harmonic in LAOS measures the residual phase-locked elastic response, whereas the higher harmonics encode the Fourier signature of strain-dependent nonaffine relaxation. The finite-amplitude modulus is interpreted as a local tangent stiffness of the evolving microstructure, in the spirit of elastoplastic and incremental nonaffine models. For entangled polymers, the analogue of the decreasing coordination number in cage-breaking theories of glass mechanics is identified not with the tube-orientation tensor itself, but with the fraction of surviving tube constraints. This distinction leads naturally to a crossover description controlled by a characteristic strain amplitude $γ_c$, rather than by universal fixed power-law exponents. The fitted value $N_{\max}\simeq1.72$ indicates that the present experimental data approach a strong but not fully saturated nonlinear state, remaining below the ideal limiting value predicted for complete constraint collapse. Finally, a constraint-counting argument combining an eight-chain affine network representation with the central-force nonaffine isostatic threshold gives a limiting estimate $|\mathrm{NLI}|_{\max}=3$. The results support the interpretation of the NLI as a Fourier-resolved dynamic nonaffinity parameter and establish a bridge between tube-based polymer dynamics, LAOS harmonic analysis, elastoplastic rheology, and microscopic nonaffine lattice dynamics.

</details>

### [133] [Ultrafast temperature diagnosis of dynamically compressed matter using millielectronvolt inelastic x-ray scattering beyond the first Brillouin zone](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20474)
*P. G. Heighway,J. S. Wark*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对多层动态压缩靶标的毫电子伏特尺度X射线散射光谱开展计算研究。基于Warren的经典热漫散射理论，模型同时包含弹性散射和单声子非弹性散射贡献，聚焦于倒逆散射（umklapp scattering）区域（动量转移位于第一布里渊区之外）。研究表明，尽管该中间波矢（intermediate-$q$）区域非弹性散射谱结构复杂，仍可借助Dornheim等人提出的基于拉普拉斯变换（Laplace transform）的形式体系，从样品晶体可靠地推算出温度，且该结论对样品的织构（texture）细节不敏感。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多层动态压缩靶标中，非晶烧蚀层（ablator layer）的散射信号可能掩盖来自晶体样品层的非弹性散射信号，亟需探索在该背景下有效提取晶体温度信息的可行方案。

Method: 以Warren的热漫散射经典理论为基础，构建包含弹性与非弹性（单声子）散射贡献的动态结构因子$S(\mathbf{q},ω)$模型，并重点关注倒逆散射（umklapp scattering）区域（第一布里渊区以外），以抑制来自烧蚀层的干扰。

Result: 在中间波矢（intermediate-$q$）的倒逆散射区域，尽管非弹性散射谱结构显著复杂化，仍可应用Dornheim等人基于拉普拉斯变换（Laplace transform）的形式体系，可靠地推算出晶体的温度，且该推论不受样品织构（texture）细节的影响。

Conclusion: 所提出的建模与分析方法可在烧蚀层散射干扰存在的条件下，从多层动态压缩靶标的晶体样品层中稳健地提取温度信息，对样品织构细节具有鲁棒性。

Abstract: We present calculations of the millielectronvolt-scale x-ray scattering spectra of multilayered dynamic-compression targets comprising an unstructured ablator layer and a crystalline, textured sample layer. Our model builds on the classic formulation of x-ray thermal diffuse scattering by Warren [B. E. Warren, Acta Crystallogr. 6, 803 (1953)] and includes both elastic and first-order (single-phonon) inelastic scattering contributions to the dynamic structure factor $S(\mathbf{q},ω)$. We focus on the umklapp scattering regime (i.e., at momentum transfers outside the first Brillouin zone) where the ablator scattering that threatens to overwhelm the inelastic scattering from the crystalline layer of interest is suppressed. We show that, despite the considerably more complex structure of the inelastic scattering spectra in this intermediate-$q$ regime, it is still possible to reliably deduce the temperature of the crystal using Dornheim's Laplace-transform--based formalism [Dornheim et al., Phys. Plasmas 30, 042707 (2023)], regardless of the details of the sample's texture.

</details>


### [134] [Lasing from SOI-integrated GaAsSb nanowires via resonator-driven optical feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20832)
*J. Zöllner,C. Doganlar,C. García Marcilla,S. Meder,G. Koblmüller,J. J. Finley*

Main category: physics.app-ph

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 硅光子集成电路（silicon photonic integrated circuits）亟需紧凑的片上光源，纳米线激光器虽有前景，但因光学反馈不足导致线宽较宽且频率稳定性差，限制了实际应用。

Method: 通过转移印刷（transfer-printing）技术将单根GaAsSb纳米线集成到绝缘体上硅（SOI）跑道型谐振器上，利用时域有限差分（FDTD）模拟优化混合纳米线-波导模式与TE谐振器基模的耦合，实现高Q因子（超过10⁴）的谐振腔。

Result: 实验测得低阈值（P_th）为8.6 ± 1.8 μJ/cm²的反馈诱导激射；相比无SOI谐振器的纳米线激光器，在3P_th下线宽降低超过四倍，且在高达5P_th时线宽稳定保持在1.8 meV以下。

Conclusion: 结果表明，通过合理设计谐振器结构，可在SOI平台上实现基于纳米线的光源，并有效改善线宽控制与频率稳定性。

Abstract: Silicon photonic integrated circuits critically depend on compact on-chip light sources, for which nanowire (NW) lasers are an attractive solution. However, their practical implementation is often limited by broad emission linewidths and poor frequency stability resulting from weak optical feedback. Here, we integrate individual GaAsSb NWs by transfer-printing onto silicon-on-insulator (SOI) racetrack resonators to realize optical feedback at silicon-transparent wavelengths. Finite-difference-time-domain simulations reveal efficient coupling between the hybrid NW-waveguide mode and the fundamental TE resonator mode, with calculated cavity Q-factors exceeding 10$^4$. Experimentally, we observe feedback-induced lasing emission at a low threshold (P$_{th}$) of 8.6 $\pm$ 1.8 $μ$J/cm$^2$. Compared to identical NW lasers without SOI resonator, the linewidth is reduced by more than a factor of four at 3P$_{th}$ and remains stable below 1.8 meV up to 5P$_{th}$. Our results demonstrate NW-based light sources on SOI and show that tailored resonator designs enable improved linewidth control and frequency stabilization.

</details>

### [135] [Higher-Rank Connections and Deformed Schrödinger Operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20338)
*Jonah Baerman,Alba Grassi,Giovanni Ravazzini*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了一类与量子Toda链的Baxter方程紧密相关的N阶线性微分方程组的连接问题，推导了满足两端衰减行为的最弱量子化条件，并将其表述为单值数据（monodromy data）的形式。该工作证明了拓扑弦/谱理论对偶（topological string/spectral theory duality）所预言的变形薛定谔方程族的量子化条件，并揭示了一类介于最小条件与N粒子量子Toda链最大衰减边界条件之间的谱问题层次结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动机在于理解一类与量子Toda链的Baxter方程相关的N阶线性微分方程的连接问题（connection problem）。这类方程的解空间为N维，并且在每个奇点处存在多个线性独立的衰减解，这导致了边界值问题的丰富结构，需要系统地加以刻画。

Method: 通过分析微分方程在两端奇点处同时衰减的行为，推导出最弱形式的量子化条件（weakest quantization conditions）。将这些条件转化为与系统单值数据（monodromy data）相关的数学表述，从而建立起边界条件与谱问题之间的严格对应关系。

Result: 证明了拓扑弦/谱理论对偶（topological string/spectral theory duality）对于变形薛定谔方程族所预言的量子化条件。同时发现了一类谱问题的层次结构，该结构将本文所研究的最小条件与N粒子量子Toda链的最大衰减边界条件（maximally decaying boundary conditions）联系起来。

Conclusion: 本文的结论表明，在最小衰减边界条件与最大衰减边界条件之间存在一个连续谱系，这为理解量子可积系统（quantum integrable systems）中不同边界条件下的谱问题提供了统一框架。

Abstract: We study the connection problem for a class of linear differential equations of order $N$ closely related to the Baxter equation of the quantum Toda chain. The space of solutions is $N$-dimensional and several linearly independent solutions decay at each singularity, leading to a rich structure of boundary value problems. We derive the weakest quantization conditions compatible with decaying behavior at both singularities, and formulate these conditions in terms of the associated monodromy data. In doing so, we prove the quantization conditions predicted by the topological string/spectral theory duality for a family of deformed Schrödinger equations. More generally, our results point to a hierarchy of spectral problems interpolating between the minimal conditions studied here and the maximally decaying boundary conditions of the $N$-particle quantum Toda chain.

### [136] [Universal thin-shell limits for the viscous operator on Riemannian hypersurfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20589)
*Zhi-Wei Wang,Samuel L. Braunstein*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文将一个薄壳（thin shell）上切向量场（tangential vector fields）的周围Bochner拉普拉斯算子（ambient Bochner Laplacian）分解为内蕴部分与径向边界剪切部分，并证明无应力（Navier滑移）边界条件普遍给出变形拉普拉斯算子（deformation Laplacian），Hodge（零切向涡量）边界条件普遍给出Hodge拉普拉斯算子（Hodge Laplacian）。该结果将Temam-Ziane和Miura的球面特定结论推广到任意光滑超曲面，并推导出一个连续单参数族边界条件，产生有效粘性算子，该算子在中间部分滑移区域才耦合到外在几何。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将已知仅在球面上成立的Temam-Ziane和Miura关于边界条件与Laplacian型算子对应关系的结果推广到任意光滑超曲面$M^n \hookrightarrow \R^{n+1}$，并解释Chan、Czubak和Yoneda在椭球面上发现的延拓依赖性（extension-dependence）的物理本质为边界条件依赖性。

Method: 将薄壳上作用于切向量场的周围Bochner Laplacian分解为内蕴部分（deformation Laplacian $\Delta_B^{(n)} + \Ric^{(n)}$）和径向边界剪切部分（由速度场的法向剖面决定），并通过分析不同边界条件对分解后算子的影响，建立边界条件与内蕴算子的对应关系。

Result: 无应力（Navier滑移）边界条件普遍给出变形Laplacian；Hodge（零切向涡量）边界条件普遍给出Hodge Laplacian；两者均适用于任意光滑超曲面（不限于常曲率曲面）。进一步导出一个连续单参数族边界条件，产生有效粘性算子$\Delta_\alpha = \Delta_{\text{Def}} - 2\alpha\,\Ric - 4\alpha(1-\alpha)S^2$，其中形状算子平方项$S^2$仅在中间部分滑移（partial-slip）区域耦合到外在几何。

Conclusion: 该工作统一并推广了先前仅对球面成立的边界条件-算子对应关系，阐明了椭球面上延拓依赖性的物理根源，并揭示了外在几何对粘性算子仅在部分滑移边界条件下才产生耦合作用。

Abstract: We decompose the ambient Bochner Laplacian acting on tangential vector fields on a thin shell around an arbitrary smooth hypersurface $M^n \hookrightarrow \R^{n+1}$ into an intrinsic piece and a radial boundary-shear piece. The intrinsic piece is the deformation Laplacian $Δ_B^{(n)} + \Ric^{(n)}$ on every hypersurface, regardless of extrinsic geometry. The boundary-shear piece is determined entirely by the normal profile of the velocity field. We prove that stress-free (Navier slip) boundary conditions yield the deformation Laplacian universally, and that Hodge (zero tangential vorticity) boundary conditions yield the Hodge Laplacian universally. Both results hold on any smooth hypersurface, not only on surfaces of constant curvature. This extends the sphere-specific results of Temam-Ziane and Miura to the general case and explains the extension-dependence found by Chan, Czubak, and Yoneda on the ellipsoid as a physical boundary-condition dependence. We also derive a continuous one-parameter family of boundary conditions interpolating between the two limits, producing an effective viscous operator $Δ_α= Δ_\Def - 2α\,\Ric - 4α(1-α)S^2$ that couples to the extrinsic geometry (through the shape operator squared) only in the intermediate partial-slip regime.

</details>


### [137] [Conformal Barycenters in Quaternionic Hyperbolic Balls](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20662)
*Wensheng Cao,Zhijian Ge*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文将复双曲球上的共形重心（conformal barycenter）推广到四元数单位球（quaternionic unit ball）上，定义了可测集合的四元数共形重心，证明了其存在性与唯一性，并展示了在全等距群Sp(n,1)下的不变性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将Jačimović和Kalaj近期为复双曲球引入的共形重心概念推广到四元数单位球上，以拓展该几何工具的应用范围。

Method: 利用四元数Hua对合（quaternionic Hua involution）构造积分方程定义重心，并等价地通过能量泛函（energy functional）的全局最小值刻画。通过沿测地线（geodesic）的直接计算验证能量泛函的严格测地凸性（strict geodesic convexity），从而证明存在性和唯一性。

Result: 证明了四元数单位球上可测集合的共形重心存在且唯一；该重心在等距群Sp(n,1)作用下保持不变；此外还处理了有限点集的情形并给出了显式算例。

Conclusion: 成功将共形重心概念从复双曲几何推广至四元数双曲几何，为后续在四元数对称空间上的几何与调和分析研究提供了基础工具。

Abstract: We extend the notion of conformal barycenter, recently introduced by
  Jačimović and Kalaj for the complex hyperbolic ball, to the
  quaternionic unit ball $\BH$. The quaternionic
  conformal barycenter of a measurable set $D$ with finite hyperbolic
  measure and finite first moment is defined as the unique point $c$ such that
  $\int_D Φ_c(q)\, \dLam(q) = \mathbf{0}$, where
  $Φ_c$ is the quaternionic Hua involution exchanging $0$ and $c$.
  Equivalently, it is the unique minimum of the energy functional
  $G(x) = \int_D \log\cosh^2\!\big(\frac12 d_H(x,y)\big)\, \dLam(y)$.
  We prove existence and uniqueness using the strict geodesic convexity
  of $G$, which is established by a direct computation along geodesics.
  The barycenter is invariant under
  the full isometry group $\mathrm{Sp}(n,1)$. We also treat finite
  point sets and provide explicit examples.

</details>


### [138] [Alpha-Dependent Cross-Tidal Residuals Beyond the Diagonal Newtonian Lunar Tensor: A Halilsoy-Inspired 45° Eigenframe Channel](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21074)
*Muhittin Cenk Eser,Mustafa Halilsoy*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于 Halilsoy 交叉极化柱面引力波（cross-polarized cylindrical gravitational waves）的启发，提出了一种对月球潮汐张量（lunar tidal tensor）的残差扩展（residual extension），引入了一个非对角（off-diagonal）潮汐分量 chi_H，该分量不改变主潮汐轴（principal tidal axes）的 90 度分离，而是旋转整个本征框架（eigenframe），产生独立的 45 度角残余潮汐信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典牛顿四极潮汐张量（Newtonian quadrupolar tidal tensor）在其主框架（principal frame）中仅包含普通的加型潮汐通道（plus-type tidal channel），不包含独立的交叉潮汐残差（cross-tidal residual）[1-3]。作者受 Halilsoy 交叉极化柱面引力波中非对角潮汐扇区自然旋转局部潮汐本征框架的机制启发，希望在牛顿框架之外探索可能存在但被忽略的隐藏非对角潮汐分量。

Method: 引入了一个依赖于参数 alpha 的残差系数 chi_H(alpha, t, rho)，代表超越对角牛顿主框架张量（diagonal Newtonian principal-frame tensor）的隐藏非对角潮汐分量。该残差不破坏主潮汐轴的 90 度分离特性，而是旋转整个本征框架，产生一个额外的 sin(2 beta) 残余通道。

Result: 残差项产生了一个独特的 45 度角特征信号（angular signature），最强的方向位于 45°、135°、225° 和 315°；相应的残差加速度尺度由 chi_H 控制。

Conclusion: 该模型不取代标准月球潮汐理论，也不将地月系统等同于 Halilsoy 时空（Halilsoy spacetime）；而是提供了一个可检验的残差假设（testable residual ansatz）：牛顿引力解释主导潮汐，Halilsoy 启发的扇区补充了对角牛顿主框架描述中缺失的非对角交叉通道。

Abstract: The Earth-Moon tide is classically explained by the Newtonian quadrupolar tidal tensor. In its principal frame, this tensor gives the familiar 90-degree stretching-squeezing geometry and contains only the ordinary plus-type tidal channel. A projected acceleration can be evaluated along any direction, including the 45-degree direction, but this projection is not an independent cross-tidal residual.
  In this work, we propose a Halilsoy-inspired residual extension of the lunar tidal tensor. The motivation comes from Halilsoy's cross-polarized cylindrical gravitational waves, where an off-diagonal tidal sector naturally rotates the local tidal eigenframe. Using this relativistic mechanism as a guide, we introduce an alpha-dependent residual coefficient, chi_H(alpha,t,rho), representing a possible hidden off-diagonal tidal component beyond the diagonal Newtonian principal-frame tensor.
  The proposed residual does not destroy the ordinary 90-degree separation of the principal tidal axes. Instead, it rotates the whole eigenframe and produces a distinct 45-degree-type angular signature. This signature appears as an additional sin(2 beta) residual channel whose strongest directions are 45, 135, 225, and 315 degrees. The corresponding residual acceleration scale is controlled by chi_H.
  The model does not replace standard lunar tidal theory and does not identify the Earth-Moon system with a Halilsoy spacetime. Rather, it provides a testable residual ansatz: Newtonian gravity explains the dominant lunar tide, while the Halilsoy-inspired sector supplies an alpha-dependent off-diagonal cross channel that is absent from the diagonal Newtonian principal-frame description.

</details>


### [139] [Relative trace formulas for obstacle scattering with Neumann and transmission boundary conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21201)
*Arne Hofmann,Alexander Strohmaier*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对 $\mathbb{R}^d$（$d \geq 2$）中多个散射体问题，建立了诺伊曼边界条件（Neumann boundary condition）与透射边界条件（transmission boundary condition）下的相对迹公式（relative trace formula），该公式与狄利克雷边界条件（Dirichlet boundary condition）下的结果类似。当 $f(x) = x^{1/2}$ 时，该迹可解释为障碍物构型的卡西米尔能量（Casimir energy）。在一维情形下，恢复了一个关于平行板卡西米尔能量的利夫希茨公式（Lifshitz formula）的严格版本，从而加强了卡西米尔效应（Casimir effect）的数学基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有工作在狄利克雷边界条件下获得了相对迹公式，本文旨在将此数学框架推广至诺伊曼边界条件与透射边界条件，以展示该严格方法的灵活性与可扩展性，并进一步巩固卡西米尔效应的数学基础。

Method: 基于 arXiv:2002.07291 中狄利克雷边界条件的方法，将其类比推广到诺伊曼边界条件与透射边界条件，建立相应的相对迹公式。在一维情形下，利用该公式推导出平行板卡西米尔能量的利夫希茨公式的严格数学版本。

Result: 成功建立了诺伊曼边界条件与透射边界条件下的相对迹公式；证明该公式在 $f(x)=x^{1/2}$ 时对应于卡西米尔能量；在一维情形下得到了利夫希茨公式的严格形式。

Conclusion: 本文工作加强了卡西米尔效应的数学理论，并证明了 arXiv:2104.09763 与 arXiv:2002.07291 中建立的严格方法也适用于诺伊曼和透射边界条件，展现了该框架的泛化能力。

Abstract: We consider the case of scattering by several obstacles in $\mathbb{R}^d$ for $d \geq 2$. We establish a relative trace formula for Neumann and transmission boundary conditions analogous to the one obtained in arXiv:2002.07291 for Dirichlet boundary conditions. In the case of $f(x) = x^{1/2}$ the trace has the interpretation of the Casimir energy of the obstacle configuration. In the one-dimensional case, we recover a rigorous version of the Lifshitz formula for the Casimir energy of parallel plates with frequency-independent electric permittivity and magnetic permeability. We thereby strengthen the mathematical foundations of the Casimir effect and demonstrate the flexibility of the rigorous approach established in arXiv:2104.09763 and arXiv:2002.07291.

</details>


### [140] [Universal fusion category symmetries on tensor products of infinite-dimensional Hilbert spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21327)
*Ian Bunner,Corey Jones*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，通过无限维辅助空间（infinite-dimensional ancilla spaces）稳定化后，任意子链（anyon chains）可局域分解为无限维希尔伯特空间（infinite-dimensional Hilbert spaces）的张量积，从而任何幺正融合范畴（unitary fusion category）都能作为对称性实现于该张量积上。进一步证明，具有相同对称范畴的两条任意子链可通过对称性兼容的保域性幺正变换相互关联，表明对固定融合范畴，基于任意子链的格点对称性实现属于单一的稳定等价类。作为推论，Levin-Wen 型模型的物理边界代数在稳定化后是“有界展形同构”（bounded spread isomorphic）的，当且仅当它们具有相同的体拓扑序（bulk topological order）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解任意子链在格点上的对称性实现及其等价分类是拓扑序（topological order）研究中的核心问题之一。本文将探索如何通过引入额外的辅助自由度来统一和简化这一分类。

Method: 本文采用无限维辅助空间稳定化（stabilization）技术，将任意子链提升为无限维希尔伯特空间张量积上的结构。在此基础上利用对称性兼容的保域性幺正变换（symmetry-compatible locality-preserving unitary）建立不同实现之间的等价关系。

Result: 证明了任意子链在无限维辅助空间稳定化后可以局域因子化为无限维张量积结构；任何幺正融合范畴可作为对称性实现于该张量积上；具有相同对称范畴的任意子链属于同一个稳定等价类；Levin-Wen 型模型的物理边界代数同构当且仅当体拓扑序相同。

Conclusion: 对于固定融合范畴，格点上的对称性实现在稳定化意义下存在唯一的等价类；Levin-Wen 模型边界代数的同构条件等价于体拓扑序相同，这为拓扑序与边界代数的对应关系提供了新的判据。

Abstract: We show that anyon chains, after stabilizing with infinite-dimensional ancilla spaces, factorize locally as tensor products of infinite-dimensional Hilbert spaces. This implies that any unitary fusion category can be realized as symmetries on a tensor product of infinite-dimensional Hilbert spaces. We then show that any two anyon chains with the same symmetry category are related by a symmetry-compatible locality-preserving unitary after stabilizing with infinite-dimensional ancilla, showing that for a fixed fusion category, there is a single stable equivalence class of symmetry realizations on the lattice via anyon chains. As a corollary of our proof, we show that the physical boundary algebras of Levin-Wen type models are bounded spread isomorphic after stabilization if and only if they have the same bulk topological order.

</details>


### [141] [Essentially singular limits of Jacobi operators and applications to higher-order squeezing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21355)
*Felix Fischer,Daniel Burgarth,Davide Lonigro*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了一族 Jacobi 算子（Jacobi operators）在耦合参数 λ→0 时的奇异极限行为，证明了该极限在强预解意义下会收敛到不同自伴延拓（self-adjoint extensions），并应用这一结果分析了量子光学中的高阶压缩算子的极限行为与自伴延拓选取问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究一族对角元受耦合参数 λ≥0 调控的 Jacobi 算子在 λ→0 时的极限行为。当 λ=0 时算子仅是对称的（symmetric），存在一族自伴延拓，而 λ>0 时算子自伴；因此需要理解从自伴算子族向对称算子不同自伴延拓收敛的机制。

Method: 推导了在 λ 小区域中平方可和广义特征向量（square-summable generalized eigenvectors）的一致界，该推导结合了离散 WKB 方法（discrete WKB methods）与 Airy 函数渐近分析（Airy-function asymptotics）。基于这些估计，在强预解收敛（strong resolvent sense）意义下分析 λ→0 的极限行为。

Result: 对任意 λ_j→0 的序列，可提取子序列使得对应的 Jacobi 算子收敛到极限算子的某个自伴延拓；反之，极限算子的每个自伴延拓均可由某一序列实现。将该行为称为本质奇异极限（essentially singular limit），类比于复分析中的本质奇点。

Conclusion: 在量子光学的高阶压缩算子（higher-order squeezing operators）中，当自由场项相对强度趋于零时，不同序列会选取不同的自伴延拓。该极限不唯一确定一个物理上特殊的自伴延拓，而是确定了一类与底层对称性相容的延拓子类。

Abstract: We study a family of Jacobi operators in which the diagonal entries are multiplied by a coupling parameter $λ\geq0$. Under suitable conditions, the operator is self-adjoint for every $λ>0$, while the formal limit at $λ=0$ is a symmetric Jacobi operator admitting a one-parameter family of self-adjoint extensions. A central ingredient of our analysis is the derivation of uniform bounds for square-summable generalized eigenvectors in the small-$λ$ regime, which combines discrete WKB methods with Airy-function asymptotics. Using these estimates, we analyze the limiting behavior $λ\to0$ in the strong resolvent sense, proving that for every sequence $λ_j\to0$ one can extract a subsequence along which the corresponding Jacobi operators converge to some self-adjoint extension of the limiting operator; conversely, every such extension can be obtained in this way. We call this behavior an essentially singular limit, by analogy with essential singularities in complex analysis.
  As an application, we study higher-order squeezing operators arising in quantum optics. Using the connection with Jacobi operators, we show that when the relative strength of the free-field term tends to zero, different self-adjoint extensions of the squeezing operator are selected along different sequences. In particular, this limit does not single out a physically distinguished self-adjoint extension, but instead identifies a distinguished subclass of extensions compatible with the underlying symmetry.

</details>

### [142] [Targeting Clause Type Distributions: a Picklock for Random Satisfiability Problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20328)
*J. Schwardt,J. C. Budich*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出 Target-SAT (TSAT) 算法，利用问题组合约束中的统计信息引导随机局部搜索，在随机 3-SAT 的最难参数区域中将可解问题规模提升约三倍，并揭示了现有算法受限于低能陷阱的原因。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: NP 完全的 3-SAT 问题是检验强关联多体系统（strongly correlated many-body systems）中基态搜索困难的基准。统计物理中将随机 3-SAT 视为伊辛自旋哈密顿量（Ising spin Hamiltonians）的研究已揭示可满足性相变（satisfiability phase transition）和临界困难参数线，但多年来在这些最难实例上的求解进展缓慢。

Method: 引入 Target-SAT (TSAT) 算法，利用问题组合约束中隐藏的统计信息，在随机局部搜索（stochastic local search）过程中主动引导搜索朝向相关参数空间中的目标方向。

Result: 在最难参数区域中，可解问题规模提升约三倍；在邻近的广阔区域中改进更为显著。分析表明，现有局部搜索算法因存在大量低能陷阱（low-energy trap）而被限制在较小系统尺寸。TSAT 仅在临界线周围的参数空间中能够快速克服指数标度（exponential scaling）的复杂度屏障。

Conclusion: TSAT 使解决最难已知随机可满足性问题的领先优势重新回到随机局部搜索算法（stochastic local search algorithms）的范畴。

Abstract: Optimization problems such as the NP-complete 3-SAT provide an important benchmark for the difficult task of finding ground-states in strongly correlated many-body systems with rugged energy landscapes. The study of random 3-SAT problems as Ising spin Hamiltonians in statistical physics has yielded major insights including the existence of a satisfiability phase transition, and the prediction of a critical parameter line of particularly hard instances. Yet, progress on solving those instances has been scarce for several decades. Here, introducing the Target-SAT (TSAT) algorithm, we roughly triple the tractable problem sizes in the hardest regime, with an even greater improvement in a vast range of neighboring regions. By leveraging statistical information hidden in the combinatorial constraints of the problem, TSAT is actively guided in its stochastic local search toward a target within the relevant parameter space. Our analysis also explains why established local search algorithms are limited to relatively small system sizes due to a vast low-energy trap. Furthermore, we characterize the aforementioned critical line in terms of a dominant additional complexity barrier, whose exponential scaling is quickly overcome by TSAT only in the surrounding parameter space. With TSAT, the lead in solving the hardest known random satisfiability problems returns to the realm of stochastic local search algorithms.

</details>


### [143] [Physical completion of the Navier-Stokes equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21357)
*Samuel L. Braunstein*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文利用庞加莱引理（Poincaré's lemma）的拓扑论证，证明在不可压缩纳维-斯托克斯方程（incompressible Navier-Stokes equations）中，涨落-耗散定理（fluctuation-dissipation theorem）可以在完整非线性动力学下精确成立，无需线性化或结构假设，并由此推导出随机系统具有唯一的吉布斯平衡态（Gibbs equilibrium）和指数收敛性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 涨落-耗散定理的传统推导依赖于线性化或特定的结构假设，限制了其在完全非线性流体动力学中的适用性。作者希望在不引入这些假设的前提下，严格证明该定理对完整非线性纳维-斯托克斯方程成立。

Method: 采用基于庞加莱引理的拓扑论证方法，证明非线性对流项（Hamiltonian项）在福克-普朗克平衡条件（Fokker-Planck equilibrium condition）中精确消去，从而推导出涨落-耗散关系。该论证还证明了GENERIC框架中可逆/不可逆分解的正确性。

Result: 推导出带有物理分子尺度谱截断的随机系统，该系统等价于有限维随机微分方程（stochastic differential equation），具有非退化噪声和约束性李雅普诺夫函数（confining Lyapunov function），被证明是全局适定的；该系统具有唯一的吉布斯平衡态，并以指数速率收敛至该平衡态。

Conclusion: 纳维-斯托克斯方程中著名的克莱千年难题（Clay Millennium Prize Problem）的困难完全源于两个理想化假设——零温度（zero temperature）和无限谱分辨率（infinite spectral resolution），而没有任何实际流体满足这些条件。

Abstract: The incompressible Navier-Stokes equations contain viscous dissipation but no thermal noise. I show, using a topological argument based on Poincaré's lemma, that the fluctuation-dissipation relation for the full nonlinear dynamics can be derived without the linearisation or structural assumptions that all previous derivations require. The nonlinear convective term is Hamiltonian (energy-preserving and phase-space-volume-preserving) and drops out of the Fokker-Planck equilibrium condition exactly, so the noise derived from linearised fluctuations near equilibrium is in fact exact for the full nonlinear system. This result proves, rather than assumes, the reversible/irreversible decomposition that the GENERIC framework postulates, provided Poincaré's lemma holds on the phase space. The resulting stochastic system, with a physical molecular-scale spectral cutoff, is trivially globally well-posed: a finite-dimensional stochastic differential equation with non-degenerate noise and a confining Lyapunov function. It has a unique Gibbs equilibrium and converges to it exponentially. The difficulty of the Clay Millennium Prize Problem arises entirely from two idealisations, zero temperature and infinite spectral resolution, neither of which is satisfied by any physical fluid.

</details>


### [144] [Competing anisotropies and phase transitions in the $q$-state clock model with a $p$-fold crystalline field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20990)
*Milan Žukovič*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 通过蒙特卡洛模拟，研究了二维 q 态时钟模型在 p 重对称性破缺晶场下的相图变化，发现弱晶场即可抑制 BKT 拓扑相并诱导出真正长程序，其行为由内禀 Z_q 对称性与外加 Z_p 各向异性的竞争决定，无法仅从对称性推断。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纯时钟模型（clock model）在大 q 下呈现 Berezinskii–Kosterlitz–Thouless (BKT) 转变，但引入竞争性离散各向异性（competing discrete anisotropies）对该拓扑相的影响尚不清楚，因此需要系统研究外加晶场如何改变相图。

Method: 采用蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulation），在二维 q 态时钟模型中引入一个额外的 p 重对称性破缺晶场（p-fold symmetry-breaking crystalline field）。

Result: 即使微弱的晶场也能抑制 BKT 相并诱导出真正长程序（true long-range order）；对于六态时钟模型（q=6），当 p=2 时，正晶场（h₂>0）导致单次转变，负晶场（h₂<0）则出现含中间有序相的两步序化过程；当 p=3 时，系统发生与三态 Potts 临界性（three-state Potts criticality）一致的直接转变。

Conclusion: 相结构不能仅从对称性考虑（symmetry considerations）推断，而由不同锁定机制（locking mechanisms）之间的竞争主导；该结果为广义 XY 模型的多频 sine-Gordon 描述提供了离散对应，并展示了附加各向异性如何重塑二维拓扑相变。

Abstract: We study the two-dimensional $q$-state clock model in the presence of an additional $p$-fold symmetry-breaking crystalline field using Monte Carlo simulations. While the pure clock model exhibits Berezinskii--Kosterlitz--Thouless (BKT) transitions for sufficiently large $q$, the effect of competing discrete anisotropies on this topological phase remains nontrivial. We show that even weak crystalline fields qualitatively modify the phase diagram by suppressing the BKT phase and inducing transitions to states with true long-range order. The resulting behavior depends sensitively on the interplay between the intrinsic $\mathbb{Z}_q$ symmetry and the imposed $\mathbb{Z}_p$ anisotropy. In particular, in the six-state clock model for $p=2$ we observe qualitatively different scenarios depending on the sign of the field: a single transition for $h_2>0$ and a two-step ordering process for $h_2<0$ with an intermediate ordered phase. For $p=3$, the system exhibits a direct transition consistent with three-state Potts criticality. These results demonstrate that the phase structure cannot be inferred from symmetry considerations alone, but is governed by the competition between distinct locking mechanisms. Our findings provide a discrete counterpart to the multi-frequency sine-Gordon description of generalized $XY$ models and illustrate how additional anisotropies reshape topological phase transitions in two dimensions.

</details>
